RV agre bṛhannuṣasāmūrdhvo asthān nirjaganvān tamasojyotiṣāgāt
RV agnirbhānunā ruśatā svaṅga ā jātoviśvā sadmānyaprāḥ
RV sa jāto garbho asi rodasyoragne cārurvibhṛta oṣadhīṣu
RV citraḥ śiśuḥ pari tamāṃsyaktūn pra mātṛbhyo adhikanikradat gāḥ
RV viṣṇuritthā paramamasya vidvāñ jāto bṛhannabhi pātitṛtīyam
RV āsā yadasya payo akrata svaṃ sacetaso abhyarcantyatra
RV ata u tvā pitubhṛto janitrīrannāvṛdhaṃ prati carantyannaiḥ
RV tā īṃ pratyeṣi punaranyarūpā asi tvaṃ vikṣumānuṣīṣu hotā
RV hotāraṃ citrarathamadhvarasya yajñasyayajñasya ketuṃruśantam
RV pratyardhiṃ devasyadevasya mahnā śriyā tvagnimatithiṃ janānām
RV sa tu vastrāṇyadha peśanāni vasāno agnirnābhāpṛthivyāḥ
RV aruṣo jātaḥ pada iḷāyāḥ purohito rājanyakṣīha devān
RV ā hi dyāvāpṛthivī agna ubhe sadā putro na mātarātatantha
RV pra yāhyachośato yaviṣṭhāthā vaha sahasyehadevān
RV piprīhi devānuśato yaviṣṭha vidvān ṛtūnrṛtupateyajeha
RV ye daivyā ṛtvijastebhiragne tvaṃ hotṝṇāmasyāyajiṣṭhaḥ
RV veṣi hotramuta potraṃ janānāṃ mandhātāsi draviṇodāṛtāvā
RV svāhā vayaṃ kṛṇavāmā havīṃṣi devo devānyajatvagnirarhan
RV ā devānāmapi panthāmaganma yacchaknavāma tadanupravoḷum
RV agnirvidvān sa yajāt sedu hotā so adhvarāṃsa ṛtūn kalpayāti
RV yad vo vayaṃ pramināma vratāni viduṣaṃ devāaviduṣṭarāsaḥ
RV agniṣ ṭad viśvamā pṛṇāti vidvānyebhirdevān ṛtubhiḥ kalpayāti
RV yat pākatrā manasā dīnadakṣā na yajñasya manvatemartyāsaḥ
RV agniṣ ṭad dhotā kratuvid vijānanyajiṣṭho devān ṛtuśo yajāti
RV viśveṣāṃ hyadhvarāṇāmanīkaṃ citraṃ ketuṃ janitātvā jajāna
RV sa ā yajasva nṛvatīranu kṣā spārhāiṣaḥ kṣumatīrviśvajanyāḥ
RV yaṃ tvā dyāvāpṛthivī yaṃ tvāpastvaṣṭā yaṃ tvāsujanimā jajāna
RV panthāmanu pravidvānpitṛyāṇaṃ dyumadagne samidhāno vi bhāhi
RV ino rājannaratiḥ samiddho raudro dakṣāya suṣumānadarśi
RV cikid vi bhāti bhāsā bṛhatāsiknīmeti ruśatīmapājan
RV kṛṣṇāṃ yadenīmabhi varpasā bhūjjanayan yoṣāmbṛhataḥ piturjām
RV ūrdhvaṃ bhānuṃ sūryasya stabhāyandivo vasubhiraratirvi bhāti
RV bhadro bhadrayā sacamāna āgāt svasāraṃ jāro abhyetipaścāt
RV supraketairdyubhiragnirvitiṣṭhan ruśadbhirvarṇairabhi rāmamasthāt
RV asya yāmāso bṛhato na vagnūnindhānā agneḥ sakhyuḥśivasya
RV iḍyasya vṛṣṇo bṛhataḥ svāso bhāmāso yāmannaktavaścikitre
RV svanā na yasya bhāmāsaḥ pavante rocamānasya bṛhataḥsudivaḥ
RV jyeṣṭhebhiryastejiṣṭhaiḥ krīḷumadbhirvarṣiṣṭhebhirbhānubhirnakṣati dyām
RV asya śuṣmāso dadṛśānapaverjehamānasya svanayan niyudbhiḥ
RV pratnebhiryo ruśadbhirdevatamo vi rebhadbhiraratirbhāti vibhvā
RV sa ā vakṣi mahi na ā ca satsi divaspṛthivyoraratiryuvatyoḥ
RV agniḥ sutukaḥ sutukebhiraśvai rabhasvadbhīrabhasvāneha gamyāḥ
RV pra te yakṣi pra ta iyarmi manma bhuvo yathā vandyo nohaveṣu
RV dhanvanniva prapā asi tvamagna iyakṣave pūravepratna rājan
RV yaṃ tvā janāso abhi saṃcaranti gāva uṣṇamiva vrajaṃyaviṣṭha
RV dūto devānāmasi martyānāmantarmahāṃścarasi rocanena
RV śiśuṃ na tvā jenyaṃ vardhayantī mātā bibhartisacanasyamānā
RV dhanoradhi pravatā yāsi haryañ jigīṣasepaśurivāvasṛṣṭaḥ
RV mūrā amūra na vayaṃ cikitvo mahitvamagne tvamaṅga vitse
RV śaye vavriścarati jihvayādan rerihyate yuvatiṃviśpatiḥ san
RV kūcijjāyate sanayāsu navyo vane tasthau palito dhūmaketuḥ
RV asnātāpo vṛṣabho na pra veti sacetaso yaṃ parṇayantamartāḥ
RV tanūtyajeva taskarā vanargu raśanābhirdaśabhirabhyadhītām
RV iyaṃ te agne navyasī manīṣā yukṣvā rathaṃna śucayadbhiraṅgaiḥ
RV brahma ca te jātavedo namaśceyaṃ ca gīḥ sadamidvardhanī bhūt
RV rakṣā ṇo agne tanayāni tokā rakṣota nastanvo aprayuchan
RV ekaḥ samudro dharuṇo rayīṇāmasmad dhṛdo bhūrijanmā vicaṣṭe
RV siṣaktyūdharniṇyorupastha utsasya madhyenihitaṃ padaṃ veḥ
RV samānaṃ nīḷaṃ vṛṣaṇo vasānāḥ saṃ jagmire mahiṣāarvatībhiḥ
RV ṛtasya padaṃ kavayo ni pānti guhā nāmānidadhire parāṇi
RV ṛtāyinī māyinī saṃ dadhāte mitvā śiśuṃ jajñaturvardhayantī
RV viśvasya nābhiṃ carato dhruvasya kaveścittantuṃ manasā viyantaḥ
RV ṛtasya hi vartanayaḥ sujātamiṣo vājāya pradivaḥsacante
RV adhīvāsaṃ rodasī vāvasāne ghṛtairannairvāvṛdhāte madhūnām
RV sapta svasṝraruṣīrvāvaśāno vidvān madhva ujjabhārādṛśe kam
RV antaryeme antarikṣe purājā ichan vavrimavidatpūṣaṇasya
RV sapta maryādāḥ kavayastatakṣustāsāmekāmidabhyaṃhuro gāt
RV āyorha skambha upamasya nīḷe pathāṃvisarge dharuṇeṣu tasthau
RV asacca sacca parame vyoman dakṣasya janmannaditerupasthe
RV agnirha naḥ pra thamajā ṛtasya pūrva āyuni vṛṣabhaścadhenuḥ
RV ayaṃ sa yasya śarmannavobhiragneredhate jaritābhiṣṭau
RV jyeṣṭhebhiryo bhānubhirṛṣūṇāṃ paryeti parivītovibhāvā
RV yo bhanubhirvibhāvā vibhātyagnirdevebhirṛtāvājasraḥ
RV ā yo vivāya sakhyā sakhibhyo 'parihvṛto atyo na saptiḥ
RV īśe yo viśvasyā devavīterīśe viśvāyuruṣasovyuṣṭau
RV ā yasmin manā havīṃṣyagnāvariṣṭarathaskabhnāti śūṣaiḥ
RV śūṣebhirvṛdho juṣāṇo arkairdevānachā raghupatvājigāti
RV mandro hotā sa juhvā yajiṣṭhaḥ sammiślo agnirā jigharti devān
RV tamusrāmindraṃ na rejamānamagniṃ gīrbhirnamobhirākṛṇudhvam
RV ā yaṃ viprāso matibhirgṛṇanti jātavedasaṃjuhvaṃ sahānām
RV saṃ yasmin viśvā vasūni jagmurvāje nāśvāḥsaptīvanta evaiḥ
RV asme ūtīrindravātatamā arvācīnāagna ā kṛṇuṣva
RV adhā hyagne mahnā niṣadyā sadyo jajñāno havyo babhūtha
RV taṃ te devāso anu ketamāyannadhāvardhanta prathamāsaūmāḥ
RV svasti no divo agne pṛthivyā viśvāyurdhehi yajathāya deva
RV sacemahi tava dasma praketairuruṣyā ṇa urubhirdevaśaṃsaiḥ
RV imā agne matayastubhyaṃ jātā gobhiraśvairabhi gṛṇantiradhaḥ
RV yadā te marto anu bhogamānaḍ vaso dadhānomatibhiḥ sujāta
RV agniṃ manye pitaramagnimāpimagniṃ bhrātaraṃ sadamitsakhāyam
RV agneranīkaṃ bṛhataḥ saparyaṃ divi śukraṃyajataṃ sūryasya
RV sidhrā agne dhiyo asme sanutrīryaṃ trāyase dama ānityahotā
RV ṛtavā sa rohidaśvaḥ purukṣurdyubhirasmāahabhirvāmamastu
RV dyubhirhitaṃ mitramiva prayogaṃ pratnam ṛtvijamadhvarasyajāram
RV bāhubhyāmagnimāyavo 'jananta vikṣu hotāraṃ nyasādayanta
RV svayaṃ yajasva divi deva devān kiṃ te pākaḥ kṛṇavadapracetāḥ
RV yathāyaja ṛtubhirdeva devānevā yajasvatanvaṃ sujāta
RV bhavā no agne 'vitota gopā bhavā vayaskṛduta novayodhāḥ
RV rāsvā ca naḥ sumaho havyadātiṃ trāsvota nastanvo aprayuchan
RV pra ketunā bṛhatā yātyagnirā rodasī vṛṣabho roravīti
RV divaścidantānupamānudānaḷ apāmupasthe mahiṣovavardha
RV mumoda garbho vṛṣabhaḥ kakudmānasremā vatsaḥ śimīvānarāvīt
RV sa devatātyudyatāni kṛṇvan sveṣu kṣayeṣuprathamo jigāti
RV ā yo mūrdhānaṃ pitrorarabdha nyadhvare dadhire sūroarṇaḥ
RV asya patmannaruṣīraśvabhudhnā ṛtasya yonautanvo juṣanta
RV uṣauṣo hi vaso agrameṣi tvaṃ yamayorabhavo vibhāvā
RV ṛtāya sapta dadhiṣe padāni janayan mitraṃ tanve svāyai
RV bhuvaścakṣurmaha ṛtasya gopā bhuvo varuṇo yad ṛtāyaveṣi
RV bhuvo apāṃ napājjātavedo bhuvo dūto yasyahavyaṃ jujoṣaḥ
RV bhuvo yajñasya rajasaśca netā yatrā niyudbhiḥ sacaseśivābhiḥ
RV divi mūrdhānaṃ dadhiṣe svarṣāṃ jihvāmagnecakṛṣe havyavāham
RV asya tritaḥ kratunā vavre antarichan dhītiṃ piturevaiḥparasya
RV sacasyamānaḥ pitrorupasthe jāmi bruvāṇaāyudhāni veti
RV sa pitryāṇyāyudhani vidvanindreṣita āptyo abhyayudhyat
RV triśīrṣāṇaṃ saptaraśmiṃ jaghanvān tvāṣṭrasya cinniḥ sasṛje trito gāḥ
RV bhūrīdindra udinakṣantamojo 'vābhinat satpatirmanyamānam
RV tvāṣṭrasya cid viśvarūpasya gonāmācakraṇastrīṇi śīrṣā parā vark
RV āpo hi ṣṭhā mayobhuvastā na ūrje dadhātana
RV maheraṇāya cakṣase
RV yo vaḥ śivatamo rasastasya bhajayateha naḥ
RV uśatīrivamātaraḥ
RV tasmā araṃ gamāma vo yasya kṣayāya jinvatha
RV āpojanayathā ca naḥ
RV śaṃ no devīrabhiṣṭaya āpo bhavantu pītaye
RV śaṃ yorabhi sravantu naḥ
RV īśānā vāryāṇāṃ kṣayantīścarṣaṇīnām
RV apoyācāmi bheṣajam
RV apsu me somo abravīdantarviśvāni bheṣajā
RV agniṃ caviśvaśambhuvam
RV āpaḥ pṛṇīta bheṣajāṃ varūthaṃ tanve mama
RV jyok casūryaṃ dṛśe
RV idamāpaḥ pra vahata yat kiṃ ca duritaṃ mayi
RV yad vāhamabhidudroha yad va śepa utānṛtam
RV āpo adyānvacāriṣaṃ rasena samagasmahi
RV payasvānagnaā gahi taṃ mā saṃ sṛja varcasā
RV o cit sakhāyaṃ sakhyā vavṛtyāṃ tiraḥ purū cidarṇavaṃjaganvan
RV piturnapātamā dadhīta vedhā adhi kṣamiprataraṃ didhyānaḥ
RV na te sakhā sakhyaṃ vaṣṭyetat salakṣmā yad viṣurūpābhavāti
RV mahas putraso asurasya vīrā divo dhartāraurviyā pari khyan
RV uśanti ghā te amṛtāsa etadekasya cit tyajasaṃ martyasya
RV ni te mano manasi dhāyyasme janyuḥ patistanvamāviviśyāḥ
RV na yat purā cakṛmā kad dha nūnam ṛtā vadanto anṛtaṃrapema
RV gandharvo apsvapyā ca yoṣā sā no nābhiḥparamaṃ jāmi tan nau
RV garbhe nu nau janitā dampatī kardevāstvaṣṭā savitāviśvarūpaḥ
RV nākirasya pra minanti vratāni veda nāvasyapṛthivi uta dyauḥ
RV ko asya veda prathamasyāhnaḥ ka īṃ dadarśa ka iha pravocat
RV bṛhan mitrasya varuṇasya dhāma kadu brava āhanovīcyā nṝn
RV yamasya mā yamyaṃ kāma āgan samāne yonau sahaśeyyāya
RV jāyeva patye tanvaṃ riricyāṃ vi cid vṛheva rathyeva cakrā
RV na tiṣṭhanti na ni miṣantyete devānāṃ spaśa iha yecaranti
RV anyena madāhano yāhi tuyaṃ tena vi vṛha rathyevacakrā
RV rātrībhirasmā ahabhirdaśasyet sūryasya cakṣurmuhurunmimīyāt
RV divā pṛthivyā mithunā sabandhū yamīryamasyabibhṛyādajāmi
RV ā ghā tā gachānuttarā yugāni yatra jāmayaḥ kṛṇavannajāmi
RV upa barbṛhi vṛṣabhāya bāhumanyamichasva subhagepatiṃ mat
RV kiṃ bhratāsad yadanāthaṃ bhavāti kimu svasā yan nirṛtirnigachat
RV kāmamūtā bahvetad rapāmi tanvā me tanvaṃ sampipṛgdhi
RV na vā u te tanvā tanvaṃ saṃ papṛcyāṃ pāpamāhuryaḥsvasāraṃ nigachāt
RV anyena mat pramudaḥ kalpayasva na tebhrāta subhage vaṣṭyetat
RV bato batasi yama naiva te mano hṛdayaṃ cāvidāma
RV anyā kilatvāṃ kakṣyeva yuktaṃ pari ṣvajāte libujeva vṛkṣam
RV anyamū ṣu tvaṃ yamyanya u tvāṃ pari ṣvajāte libujevavṛkṣam
RV tasya vā tvaṃ mana ichā sa vā tavādhā kṛṇuṣvasaṃvidaṃ subhadrām
RV vṛṣā vṛṣṇe duduhe dohasā divaḥ payāṃsi yahvo aditeradābhyaḥ
RV viśvaṃ sa veda varuṇo yathā dhiyā sayajñiyo yajatu yajñiyān ṛtūn
RV rapad gandharvīrapyā ca yoṣaṇā nadasya nāde pari pātume manaḥ
RV iṣṭasya madhye aditirni dhātu no bhrātā nojyeṣṭhaḥ prathamo vi vocati
RV so cin nu bhadrā kṣumatī yaśasvatyuṣā uvāsa manavesvarvatī
RV yadīmuśantamuśatāmanu kratumagniṃhotāraṃ vidathāya jījanan
RV adha tyaṃ drapsaṃ vibhvaṃ vicakṣaṇaṃ virābharadiṣitaḥ śyeno adhvare
RV yadī viśo vṛṇate dasmamāryāagniṃ hotāramadha dhīrajāyata
RV sadāsi raṇvo yavaseva puṣyate hotrābhiragne manuṣaḥsvadhvaraḥ
RV viprasya vā yacchaśamāna ukthyaṃ vājaṃsasavānupayāsi bhūribhiḥ
RV udīraya pitarā jāra ā bhagamiyakṣati haryato hṛttaiṣyati
RV vivakti vahniḥ svapasyate makhastaviṣyate asurovepate matī
RV yaste agne sumatiṃ marto akṣat sahasaḥ sūno ati sa praśṛṇve
RV iṣaṃ dadhāno vahamāno aśvairā sa dyumānamavān bhūṣati dyūn
RV yadagna eṣā samitirbhavāti devī deveṣu yajatā yajatra
RV ratnā ca yad vibhajāsi svadhāvo bhāgaṃ no atra vasumantaṃvītāt
RV śrudhī no agne sadane sadhasthe yukṣvā rathamamṛtasyadravitnum
RV ā no vaha rodasī devaputre mākirdevānāmapabhūriha syāḥ
RV dyāvā ha kṣāmā prathame ṛtenābhiśrāve bhavataḥsatyavācā
RV devo yan martān yajathāya kṛṇvan sīdaddhotā pratyaṃ svamasuṃ yan
RV devo devān paribhūrṛtena vahā no havyaṃ prathamaścikitvān
RV dhūmaketuḥ samidhā bhāṛjīko mandro hotā nityovācā yajīyān
RV svāvṛg devasyāmṛtaṃ yadī gorato jātāso dhārayantaurvī
RV viśve devā anu tat te yajurgurduhe yadenīdivyaṃ ghṛtaṃ vāḥ
RV arcāmi vāṃ vardhāyāpo ghṛtasnū dyāvābhūmī śṛṇutaṃrodasī me
RV ahā yad dyāvo 'sunītimayan madhvā no atrapitarā śiśītām
RV kiṃ svin no rājā jagṛhe kadasyāti vrataṃ cakṛmā ko viveda
RV mitraścid dhi ṣmā juhurāṇo devāñchloko nayātāmapi vājo asti
RV durmantvatrāmṛtasya nāma salakṣmā yad viṣurūpābhavāti
RV yamasya yo manavate sumantvagne tam ṛṣva pāhyaprayuchan
RV yasmin devā vidathe mādayante vivasvataḥ sadane dhārayante
RV sūrye jyotiradadhurmāsyaktūn pari dyotaniṃ caratoajasrā
RV yasmin devā manmani saṃcarantyapīcye na vayamasya vidma
RV mitro no atrāditiranāgān savitā devo varuṇāya vocat
RV śrudhī no agne sadane sadhasthe yukṣvā 
RV yuje vāṃ brahma pūrvyaṃ namobhirvi śloka etu pathyevasūreḥ
RV śṛṇvantu viśve amṛtasya putrā ā ye dhāmānidivyāni tasthuḥ
RV yame iva yatamāne yadaitaṃ pra vāṃ bharan mānuṣādevayantaḥ
RV ā sīdataṃ svamu lokaṃ vidāne svāsasthebhavatamindave naḥ
RV pañca padāni rupo anvarohaṃ catuṣpadīmanvemi vratena
RV akṣareṇa prati mima etām ṛtasya nābhāvadhi saṃ punāmi
RV devebhyaḥ kamavṛṇīta mṛtyuṃ prajāyai kamamṛtaṃnāvṛṇīta
RV bṛhaspatiṃ yajñamakṛṇvata ṛṣiṃ priyāṃyamastanvaṃ prārirecīt
RV sapta kṣaranti śiśave marutvate pitre putrāso apyavīvatannṛtam
RV ubhe idasyobhayasya rājata ubhe yatete ubhayasyapuṣyataḥ
RV pareyivāṃsaṃ pravato mahīranu bahubhyaḥ panthāmanupaspaśanam
RV vaivasvataṃ saṃgamanaṃ janānāṃ yamaṃrājānaṃ haviṣā duvasya
RV yamo no gātuṃ prathamo viveda naiṣa gavyūtirapabhartavā u
RV yatrā naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ pareyurenā jajñānāḥpathyā anu svāḥ
RV mātalī kavyairyamo aṅgirobhirbṛhaspatirṛkvabhirvāvṛdhānaḥ
RV yāṃśca devā vāvṛdhurye ca devāṃsvāhānye svadhayānye madanti
RV imaṃ yama prastaramā hi sīdāṅgirobhiḥ pitṛbhiḥsaṃvidānaḥ
RV ā tvā mantrāḥ kaviśastā vahantvenā rājanhaviṣā mādayasva
RV aṅgirobhirā gahi yajñiyebhiryama vairūpairiha mādayasva
RV vivasvantaṃ huve yaḥ pitā te 'smin yajñe barhiṣyāniṣadya
RV aṅgiraso naḥ pitaro navagvā atharvāṇo bhṛgavaḥ somyāsaḥ
RV teṣāṃ vayaṃ sumatau yajñiyānāmapi bhadre saumanasesyāma
RV prehi prehi pathibhiḥ pūrvyebhiryatrā naḥ pūrve pitaraḥpareyuḥ
RV ubhā rājānā svadhayā madantā yamaṃ paśyāsivaruṇaṃ ca devam
RV saṃ gachasva pitṛbhiḥ saṃ yameneṣṭāpūrtena paramevyoman
RV hitvāyāvadyaṃ punarastamehi saṃ gachasva tanvāsuvarcāḥ
RV apeta vīta vi ca sarpatāto 'smā etaṃ pitaro lokamakran
RV ahobhiradbhiraktubhirvyaktaṃ yamo dadātyavasānamasmai
RV ati drava sārameyau śvānau caturakṣau śabalau sādhunāpathā
RV athā pitṝn suvidatrānupehi yamena ye sadhamādammadanti
RV yau te śvānau yama rakṣitārau caturakṣau pathirakṣīnṛcakṣasau
RV tābhyāmenaṃ pari dehi rājan svasti cāsmāanamīvaṃ ca dhehi
RV urūṇasāvasutṛpā udumbalau yamasya dūtau carato janānanu
RV tāvasmabhyaṃ dṛśaye sūryāya punardātāmasumadyeha bhadram
RV yamāya somaṃ sunuta yamaya juhutā haviḥ
RV yamaṃ ha yajñogachatyagnidūto araṃkṛtaḥ
RV yamāya ghṛtavad dhavirjuhota pra ca tiṣṭhata
RV sa nodeveṣvā yamad dīrghamāyuḥ pra jīvase
RV yamāya madhumattamaṃ rājñe havyaṃ juhotana
RV idaṃ namaṛṣibhyaḥ pūrvajebhyaḥ pūrvebhyaḥ pathikṛdbhyaḥ
RV trikadrukebhiḥ patati ṣaḷ urvīrekamid bṛhat
RV triṣṭubgāyatrī chandāṃsi sarvā tā yama āhitā
RV udīratāmavara ut parāsa un madhyamāḥ pitaraḥsomyāsaḥ
RV asuṃ ya īyuravṛkā ṛtajñāste no 'vantupitaro haveṣu
RV idaṃ pitṛbhyo namo astvadya ye pūrvāso ya uparāsa īyuḥ
RV ye pārthive rajasyā niṣattā ye vā nūnaṃ suvṛjanāsuvikṣu
RV āhaṃ pitṝn suvidatrānavitsi napātaṃ ca vikramaṇaṃ caviṣṇoḥ
RV barhiṣado ye svadhayā sutasya bhajanta pitvastaihāgamiṣṭhāḥ
RV barhiṣadaḥ pitara ūtyarvāgimā vo havyā cakṛmā juṣadhvam
RV ta ā gatāvasā śantamenāthā naḥ śaṃ yorarapodadhāta
RV upahūtāḥ pitaraḥ somyāso barhiṣyeṣu nidhiṣu priyeṣu
RV ta ā gamantu ta iha śruvantvadhi bruvantu te 'vantvasmān
RV ācyā jānu dakṣiṇato niṣadyemaṃ yajñamabhi gṛṇītaviśve
RV mā hiṃsiṣṭa pitaraḥ kena cin no yad va āgaḥpuruṣatā karāma
RV āsīnāso aruṇīnāmupasthe rayiṃ dhatta dāśuṣe martyāya
RV putrebhyaḥ pitarastasya vasvaḥ pra yachata ta ihorjandadhāta
RV ye naḥ pūrve pitaraḥ somyāso 'nūhire somapīthaṃvasiṣṭhāḥ
RV tebhiryamaḥ saṃrarāṇo havīṃṣyuśannuśadbhiḥ pratikāmamattu
RV ye tātṛṣurdevatrā jehamānā hotrāvida stomataṣṭāsoarkaiḥ
RV āgne yāhi suvidatrebhirarvāṃ satyaiḥ kavyaiḥpitṛbhirgharmasadbhiḥ
RV ye satyāso havirado haviṣpā idreṇa devaiḥ sarathandadhānāḥ
RV āgne yāhi sahasraṃ devavandaiḥ paraiḥpūrvaiḥ pitṛbhirgharmasadbhiḥ
RV agniṣvāttāḥ pitara eha gachata sadaḥsadaḥ sadatasupraṇītayaḥ
RV attā havīṃṣi prayatāni barhiṣyathārayiṃ sarvavīraṃ dadhātana
RV tvamagna īḷito jātavedo 'vāḍ ḍhavyāni surabhīṇikṛtvī
RV prādāḥ pitṛbhyaḥ svadhayā te akṣannaddhi tvandeva prayatā havīṃṣi
RV ye ceha pitaro ye ca neha yāṃśca vidma yānu ca napravidma
RV tvaṃ vettha yati te jātavedaḥ svadhābhiryajñaṃ sukṛtaṃ juṣasva
RV ye agnidagdhā ye anagnidagdhā madhye divaḥ svadhayāmādayante
RV tebhiḥ svarāḷ asunītimetāṃ yathāvaśantanvaṃ kalpayasva
RV mainamagne vi daho mābhi śoco māsya tvacaṃ cikṣipo māśarīram
RV yadā śṛtaṃ kṛṇavo jātavedo 'themenaṃ prahiṇutāt pitṛbhyaḥ
RV śṛtaṃ yadā karasi jātavedo 'theme
naṃ pari dattātpitṛbhyaḥ
RV yadā gachātyasunītimetāmathā devānāṃvaśanīrbhavāti
RV sūryaṃ cakṣurgachatu vātamātmā dyāṃ ca gachapṛthivīṃ ca dharmaṇā
RV apo vā gacha yadi tatra te hitamoṣadhīṣu prati tiṣṭhā śarīraiḥ
RV ajo bhāgastapasā taṃ tapasva taṃ te śocistapatu taṃ tearciḥ
RV yāste śivāstanvo jātavedastābhirvahainaṃsukṛtāmu lokam
RV ava sṛja punaragne pitṛbhyo yasta āhutaścaratisvadhābhiḥ
RV ayurvasāna upa vetu śeṣaḥ saṃ gachatāntanvā jātavedaḥ
RV yat te kṛṣṇaḥ śakuna ātutoda pipīlaḥ sarpa uta vāśvāpadaḥ
RV agniṣ ṭad viśvādagadaṃ kṛṇotu somaśca yobrāhmaṇānāviveśa
RV agnervarma pari gobhirvyayasva saṃ prorṇuṣva pīvasāmedasā ca
RV net tvā dhṛṣṇurharasā jarhṛṣāṇo dadhṛgvidhakṣyan paryaṅkhayāte
RV imamagne camasaṃ mā vi jihvaraḥ priyo devānāmutasomyānām
RV eṣa yaścamaso devapānastasmin devā amṛtāmādayante
RV kravyādamagniṃ pra hiṇomi dūraṃ yamarājño gachaturipravāhaḥ
RV ihaivāyamitaro jātavedā devebhyo havyaṃvahatu prajānan
RV yo agniḥ kravyāt praviveśa vo gṛhamimaṃ paśyannitaraṃjātavedasam
RV taṃ harāmi pitṛyajñāya devaṃ sa gharmaminvāt parame sadhasthe
RV yo agniḥ kravyavāhanaḥ pitṝn yakṣad ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
RV preduhavyāni vocati devebhyaśca pitṛbhya ā
RV uśantastvā ni dhīmahyuśantaḥ samidhīmahi
RV uśannuśata ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave
RV yaṃ tvamagne samadahastamu nirvāpayā punaḥ
RV kiyāmbvatra rohatu pākadūrvā vyalkaśā
RV śītike śītikāvati hlādike hlādikāvati
RV maṇḍūkyā susaṃ gama imaṃ svagniṃ harṣaya
RV tvaṣṭā duhitre vahatuṃ kṛṇotītīdaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃsameti
RV yamasya mātā paryuhyamānā maho jāyā vivasvatonanāśa
RV apāgūhannamṛtāṃ martyebhyaḥ kṛtvī savarṇāmadadurvivasvate
RV utāśvināvabharad yat tadasīdajahādu dvāmithunā saraṇyūḥ
RV pūṣā tvetaścyāvayatu pra vidvānanaṣṭapaśurbhuvanasya gopāḥ
RV sa tvaitebhyaḥ pari dadat pitṛbhyo 'gnirdevebhyaḥ suvidatriyebhyaḥ
RV āyurviśvāyuḥ pari pāsati tvā pūṣā tvā pātu prapathepurastāt
RV yatrasate sukṛto yatra te yayustatra tvādevaḥ savitā dadhātu
RV pūṣemā āśā anu veda sarvāḥ so asmānabhayatamenaneṣat
RV svastidā āghṛṇiḥ sarvavīro 'prayuchan pura etuprajānan
RV prapathe pathamajaniṣṭa pūṣā prapathe divaḥ prapathepṛthivyāḥ
RV ubhe abhi priyatame sadhasthe ā ca parā cacarati prajānan
RV sarasvatīṃ devayanto havante sarasvatīmadhvare tāyamāne
RV sarasvatīṃ sukṛto ahvayanta sarasvatī dāśuṣe vāryaṃ dāt
RV sarasvati yā sarathaṃ yayatha svadhābhirdevi pitṛbhirmadantī
RV āsadyāsmin barhiṣi mādayasvānamīvā iṣa ādhehyasme
RV sarasvatīṃ yāṃ pitaro havante dakṣiṇā yajñamabhinakṣamāṇāḥ
RV sahasrārghamiḷo atra bhāgaṃ rāyaspoṣaṃ yajamāneṣu dhehi
RV apo asmān mātaraḥ śundhayantu ghṛtena no ghṛtapvaḥ punantu
RV viśvaṃ hi ripraṃ pravahanti devirudidābhyaḥ śucirāpūta emi
RV drapsaścaskanda prathamānanu dyūnimaṃ ca yonimanu yaśca purvaḥ
RV samānaṃ yonimanu saṃcarantaṃ drapsaṃ juhomyanu sapta hotrāḥ
RV yaste drapsa skandati yaste aṃśurbāhucyuto dhiṣaṇāyāupasthāt
RV adhvaryorvā pari vā yaḥ pavitrāt taṃ te juhomimanasā vaṣaṭkṛtam
RV yaste drapsa skanno yaste aṃśuravaśca yaḥ paraḥsrucā
RV ayaṃ devo bṛhaspatiḥ saṃ taṃ siñcatu rādhase
RV payasvatīroṣadhayaḥ payasvan māmakaṃ vacaḥ
RV apāmpayasvadit payastena mā saha śundhata
RV paraṃ mṛtyo anu parehi panthāṃ yaste sva itaro devayānāt
RV cakṣuṣmate śṛṇvate te bravīmi mā naḥ prajāṃ rīriṣomota vīrān
RV mṛtyoḥ padaṃ yopayanto yadaita drāghīya āyuḥ pratarandadhānāḥ
RV āpyāyamānāḥ prajayā dhanena śuddhāḥpūtā bhavata yajñiyāsaḥ
RV ime jīvā vi mṛtairāvavṛtrannabhūd bhadrā devahūtirnoadya
RV prāñco agāma nṛtaye hasāya drāghīya āyuḥprataraṃ dadhānāḥ
RV imaṃ jīvebhyaḥ paridhiṃ dadhāmi maiṣāṃ nu gādaparoarthametam
RV śataṃ jīvantu śaradaḥ purūcīrantarmṛtyuṃ dadhatāṃ parvatena
RV yathāhānyanupūrvaṃ bhavanti yatha ṛtava ṛtubhiryantisādhu
RV yathā na pūrvamaparo jahātyevā dhātarāyūṃṣi kalpayaiṣām
RV ā rohatāyurjarasaṃ vṛṇānā anupūrvaṃ yatamānā yatiṣṭha
RV iha tvaṣṭā sujanimā sajoṣā dīrghamāyuḥkarati jīvase vaḥ
RV imā nārīravidhavāḥ supatnīrāñjanena sarpiṣā saṃviśantu
RV anaśravo 'namīvāḥ suratnā ā rohantu janayoyonimagre
RV udīrṣva nāryabhi jīvalokaṃ gatāsumetamupa śeṣa ehi
RV hastagrābhasya didhiṣostavedaṃ patyurjanitvamabhi sambabhūtha
RV dhanurhastādādadāno mṛtasyāsme kṣatrāya varcasebalāya
RV atraiva tvamiha vayaṃ suvīrā viśvā spṛdhoabhimātīrjayema
RV upa sarpa mātaraṃ bhūmimetāmuruvyacasaṃ pṛthivīṃsuśevām
RV ūrṇamradā yuvatirdakṣiṇāvata eṣā tvā pātunirṛterupasthāt
RV ucchvañcasva pṛthivi mā ni bādhathāḥ sūpāyanāsmai bhavasūpavañcanā
RV mātā putraṃ yathā sicābhyenaṃ bhūmaūrṇuhi
RV ucchvañcamānā pṛthivī su tiṣṭhatu sahasraṃ mita upa hiśrayantām
RV te gṛhāso ghṛtaścuto bhavantu viśvāhāsmaiśaraṇāḥ santvatra
RV ut te stabhnāmi pṛthivīṃ tvat parīmaṃ logaṃ nidadhan moahaṃ riṣam
RV etāṃ sthūṇāṃ pitaro dhārayantu te 'trāyamaḥ sādanā te minotu
RV pratīcīne māmahanīṣvāḥ parṇamivā dadhuḥ
RV pratīcīṃ jagrabhā vācamaśvaṃ raśanayā yathā
RV ni vartadhvaṃ mānu gātāsmān siṣakta revatīḥ
RV agnīṣomāpunarvasū asme dhārayataṃ rayim
RV punarenā ni vartaya punarenā nyā kuru
RV indra eṇā niyachatvagnirenā upājatu
RV punaretā ni vartantāmasmin puṣyantu gopatau
RV ihaivāgneni dhārayeha tiṣṭhatu yā rayiḥ
RV yan niyānaṃ nyayanaṃ saṃjñānaṃ yat parāyaṇam
RV āvartanaṃ nivartanaṃ yo gopā api taṃ huve
RV ya udānaḍ vyayanaṃ ya udānaṭ parāyaṇam
RV āvartanaṃnivartanamapi gopā ni vartatām
RV ā nivarta ni vartaya punarna indra gā dehi
RV jīvābhirbhunajāmahai
RV pari vo viśvato dadha ūrjā ghṛtena payasā
RV ye devāḥ keca yajñiyāste rayyā saṃ sṛjantu naḥ
RV ā nivartana vartaya ni nivartana vartaya
RV bhūmyāścatasraḥpradiśastābhya enā ni vartaya
RV bhadraṃ no api vātaya manaḥ
RV agnimīḷe bhujāṃ yaviṣṭhaṃ śāsā mitraṃ durdharītum
RV yasya dharman svarenīḥ saparyanti māturūdhaḥ
RV yamāsā kṛpanīḷaṃ bhāsāketuṃ vardhayanti
RV bhrājateśreṇidan
RV aryo viśāṃ gātureti pra yadānaḍ divo antān
RV kavirabhraṃ didyānaḥ
RV juṣad dhavyā mānuṣasyordhvastasthāv ṛbhvā yajñe
RV minvan sadma pura eti
RV sa hi kṣemo haviryajñaḥ śruṣṭīdasya gātureti
RV agniṃ devā vāśīmantam
RV yajñāsāhaṃ duva iṣe 'gniṃ pūrvasya śevasya
RV adreḥsūnumāyumāhuḥ
RV naro ye ke cāsmadā viśvet te vāma ā syuḥ
RV agniṃhaviṣā vardhantaḥ
RV kṛṣṇaḥ śveto 'ruṣo yāmo asya bradhna ṛjra uta śoṇoyaśasvān
RV hiraṇyarūpaṃ janitā jajāna
RV evā te agne vimado manīṣāmūrjo napādamṛtebhiḥsajoṣāḥ
RV gira ā vakṣat sumatīriyāna iṣamūrjaṃsukṣitiṃ viśvamābhāḥ
RV āgniṃ na svavṛktibhirhotāraṃ tvā vṛṇīmahe
RV yajñāyastīrṇabarhiṣe vi vo made śīraṃ pāvakaśociṣaṃvivakṣase
RV tvāmu te svābhuvaḥ śumbhantyaśvarādhasaḥ
RV veti tvāmupasecanī vi vo mada ṛjītiragna āhutirvivakṣase
RV tve dharmāṇa āsate juhūbhiḥ siñcatīriva
RV kṛṣṇārūpāṇyarjunā vi vo made viśvā adhi śriyo dhiṣevivakṣase
RV yamagne manyase rayiṃ sahasāvannamartya
RV tamā novājasātaye vi vo made yajñeṣu citramā bharā vivakṣase
RV agnirjāto atharvaṇā vidad viśvāni kāvyā
RV bhuvad dūtovivasvato vi vo made priyo yamasya kāmyo vivakṣase
RV tvāṃ yajñeṣvīḷate 'gne prayatyadhvare
RV tvaṃ vasūnikāmyā vi vo made viśvā dadhāsi dāśuṣe vivakṣase
RV tvāṃ yajñeṣv ṛtvijaṃ cārumagne ni ṣedire
RV ghṛtapratīkaṃ manuṣo vi vo made śukraṃ cetiṣṭhamakṣabhirvivakṣase
RV agne śukreṇa śociṣoru prathayase bṛhat
RV abhikrandanvṛṣāyase vi vo made garbhaṃ dadhāsi jāmiṣu vivakṣase
RV kuha śruta indraḥ kasminnadya jane mitro na śruyate
RV ṛṣīṇāṃ vā yaḥ kṣaye guhā va carkṛṣe gira
RV iha śruta indro asme adya stave vajry ṛcīṣamaḥ
RV mitro nayo janeṣvā yaśaścakre asāmyā
RV maho yas patiḥ śavaso asāmyā maho nṛmṇasya tūtujiḥ
RV bhartā vajrasya dhṛṣṇoḥ pitā putramiva priyam
RV yujāno aśva vātasya dhunī devo devasya vajrivaḥ
RV syantapathā virukmatā sṛjāna stoṣyadhvanaḥ
RV tvaṃ tyā cid vātasyāśvāgā ṛjrā tmanā vahadhyai
RV yayordevo na martyo yantā nakirvidāyyaḥ
RV adha gmantośanā pṛchate vāṃ kadarthā na ā gṛham
RV ājagmathuḥ parākād divaśca gmaśca martyam
RV ā na indra pṛkṣase 'smākaṃ brahmodyatam
RV tat tvāyācāmahe 'vaḥ śuṣṇaṃ yad dhannamānuṣam
RV akarmā dasyurabhi no amanturanyavrato amānuṣaḥ
RV tvantasyāmitrahan vadhardāsasya dambhaya
RV tvaṃ na indra śūra śūrairuta tvotāso barhaṇā
RV purutrāte vi pūrtayo navanta kṣoṇayo yathā
RV tvaṃ tān vṛtrahatye codayo nṝn kārpāṇe śūra vajrivaḥ
RV guhā yadī kavīnāṃ viśāṃ nakṣatraśavasām
RV makṣū tā ta indra dānāpnasa ākṣāṇe śūra vajrivaḥ
RV yad dha śuṣṇasya dambhayo jātaṃ viśvaṃ sayāvabhiḥ
RV mākudhryagindra śūra vasvīrasme bhūvannabhiṣṭayaḥ
RV vayaṃvayaṃ ta āsāṃ sumne syāma vajrivaḥ
RV asme tā ta indra santu satyāhiṃsantīrupaspṛśaḥ
RV vidyāmayāsāṃ bhujo dhenūnāṃ na vajrivaḥ
RV ahastā yadapadī vardhata kṣāḥ śacībhirvedyānām
RV śuṣṇaṃ pari pradakṣiṇid viśvāyave ni śiśnathaḥ
RV pibāpibedindra śūra somaṃ mā riṣaṇyo vasavāna vasuḥsan
RV uta trāyasva gṛṇato maghono mahaśca rāyo revataskṛdhī naḥ
RV yajāmaha indraṃ vajradakṣiṇaṃ harīṇāṃ rathyaṃvivratānām
RV pra śmaśru dodhuvadūrdhvathā bhūd visenābhirdayamāno vi rādhasā
RV harī nvasya yā vane vide vasvindro maghairmaghavāvṛtrahā bhuvat
RV ṛbhurvāja ṛbhukṣāḥ patyate śavo 'vakṣṇaumi dāsasya nāma cit
RV yadā vajraṃ hiraṇyamidathā rathaṃ harī yamasyavahato vi sūribhiḥ
RV ā tiṣṭhati maghavā sanaśruta indrovājasya dīrghaśravasas patiḥ
RV so cin nu vṛṣṭiryūthyā svā sacānindraḥ śmaśrūṇiharitābhi pruṣṇute
RV ava veti sukṣayaṃ sute madhūdiddhūnoti vāto yathā vanam
RV yo vācā vivāco mṛdhravācaḥ purū sahasrāśivā jaghāna
RV tattadidasya pauṃsyaṃ gṛṇīmasi piteva yastaviṣīṃvāvṛdhe śavaḥ
RV stomaṃ ta indra vimadā ajījanannapūrvyaṃ purutamaṃsudānave
RV vidmā hyasya bhojanaminasya yadā paśuṃ nagopāḥ karāmahe
RV mākirna enā sakhyā vi yauśustava cendra vimadasya caṛśeḥ
RV vidmā hi te pramatiṃ deva jāmivadasme te santusakhyā śivāni
RV indra somamimaṃ piba madhumantaṃ camū sutam
RV asme rayiṃni dhāraya vi vo made sahasriṇaṃ purūvaso vivakṣase
RV tvāṃ yajñebhirukthairupa havyebhirīmahe
RV śacīpateśacīnāṃ vi vo made śreṣṭhaṃ no dhehi vāryaṃ vivakṣase
RV yas patirvāryāṇāmasi radhrasya coditā
RV indrastotṝṇāmavitā vi vo made dviṣo naḥ pāhyaṃhasovivakṣase
RV yuvaṃ śakrā māyāvinā samīcī nīramanthatam
RV vimadenayadiḷita nasatya niramanthatam
RV viśve devā akṛpanta samicyorniṣpatantyoḥ
RV nasatyavabruvandevaḥ punarā vahataditi
RV madhuman me parāyaṇaṃ madhumat punarayanam
RV ta no devadevataya yuvaṃ madhumatas kṛtam
RV bhadraṃ no api vātaya mano dakṣamuta kratum
RV adhā tesakhye andhaso vi vo made raṇan gavo na yavase vivakṣase
RV hṛdispṛśasta asate viśveṣu soma dha masu
RV adhā kāmā imemama vi vo made vi tiṣṭhante vasūyavo vivakṣase
RV uta vratani soma te prahaṃ mināmi pākyā
RV adhā pitevasūnave vi vo made mṛḷa no abhi cid vadhād vivakṣase
RV samu pra yanti dhītayaḥ sargāso 'vatāniva
RV kratuṃ naḥsoma jivase vi vo made dharayā camasāniva vivakṣase
RV tava tye soma śaktibhirnikāmāso vy ṛṇvire
RV gṛtsasyadhirastavaso vi vo made vrajaṃ gomantamaśvinaṃ vivakṣase
RV paśuṃ naḥ soma rakṣasi purutra viṣṭhitaṃ jagat
RV samākṛṇoṣi jīvase vi vo made viśvā sampaśyan bhuvanavivakṣase
RV tvaṃ naḥ soma viśvato gopa adabhyo bhava
RV sedha rājannapasridho vi vo made ma no duḥ śaṃsa īśatā vivakṣase
RV tvaṃ naḥ soma sukraturva yodheyāya jāgṛhi
RV kṣetravittaromanuṣo vi vo made druho naḥ pāhyaṃhaso vivakṣase
RV tvaṃ no vṛtra hantamendrasyendo śivaḥ sakhā
RV yat siṃhavante samithe vi vo made yudhyamanastokasātauvivakṣase
RV ayaṃ gha sa turo mada indrasya vardhata priyaḥ
RV ayaṃkakṣīvato maho vi vo made matiṃ viprasya vardhayadvivakṣase
RV ayaṃ vipraya daśuṣe vajaniyarti gomataḥ
RV ayaṃsaptabhya ā varaṃ vi vo made prandhaṃ śroṇaṃ catariṣad vivakṣase
RV pra hyachā manīṣā spārha yanti niyutaḥ
RV pra dasrāniyudrathaḥ pūṣā aviṣṭu māhinaḥ
RV yasya tyan mahitvaṃ vatāpyamayaṃ janaḥ
RV vipra ā vaṃsaddhītibhiściketa suṣṭutīnām
RV sa veda suṣṭutīnāmindurna pūṣa vṛṣā
RV abhi psuraḥpruṣāyati vrajaṃ na ā pruṣāyati
RV maṃsīmahi tvā vayamasmākaṃ deva pūṣan
RV matmāṃ casādhanaṃ viprāṇāṃ cādhavam
RV pratyardhiryajñanāmaśvahayo rathānām
RV ṛṣiḥ sa yomanurhito viprasya yāvayatsakhaḥ
RV adhīṣamāṇāyāḥ patiḥ śucāyāśca śucasya ca
RV vāsovayo 'vīnāmā vāsāṃsi marmṛjat
RV ino vājānāṃ patirinaḥ puṣṭīnaṃ sakha
RV pra śmaśruharyato dūdhod vi vṛtha yo adābhyaḥ
RV ā te rathasya pūṣannajā dhuraṃ vavṛtyuḥ
RV viśvasyārthinaḥ sakhā sanojā anapacyutaḥ
RV asmakamurjā rathaṃ pūṣā aviṣṭu māhinaḥ
RV bhuvadvajanāṃ vṛdha imaṃ naḥ śṛṇavad dhavam
RV asat su me jaritaḥ sābhivego yat sunvate yajamanaya śikṣam
RV anāśīrdāmahamasmi prahantā satyadhvṛtaṃ vṛjināyantamābhum
RV yadīdahaṃ yudhaye saṃnayānyadevayūn tanvāśūśujānān
RV amā te tumraṃ vṛṣabhaṃ pacāni tīvraṃsutaṃ pañcadaśaṃ ni ṣiñcam
RV nāhaṃ taṃ veda ya iti bravītyadevayūn samaraṇejaghanvān
RV yadāvākhyat samaraṇam ṛghāvadādid dha mevṛṣabhā pra bruvanti
RV yadajñāteṣu vṛjaneṣvāsaṃ viśve sato maghavāno maāsan
RV jināmi vet kṣema ā santamābhuṃ pra taṃkṣiṇāṃ parvate pādagṛhya
RV na vā u māṃ vṛjane vārayante na parvatāso yadahammanasye
RV mama svanāt kṛdhukarṇo bhayāta evedanu dyūnkiraṇaḥ samejāt
RV darśan nvatra śṛtapānanindrān bāhukṣadaḥ śaravepatyamānān
RV ghṛṣuṃ vā ye niniduḥ sakhāyamadhyū nveṣu pavayo vavṛtyuḥ
RV abhūrvaukṣīrvyu āyurānaḍ darṣan nu pūrvo aparonu darṣat
RV dve pavaste pari taṃ na bhūto yo asya pārerajaso viveṣa
RV gāvo yavaṃ prayutā aryo akṣan tā apaśyaṃ sahagopāścarantīḥ
RV havā idaryo abhitaḥ samāyan kiyadāsusvapatiśchandayāte
RV saṃ yad vayaṃ yavasādo janānāmahaṃ yavāda urvajreantaḥ
RV atrā yukto 'vasātāramichādatho ayuktaṃ yunajadvavanvān
RV atredu me maṃsase satyamuktaṃ dvipācca yaccatuṣpātsaṃsṛjāni
RV strībhiryo atra vṛṣaṇaṃ pṛtanyādayuddhoasya vi bhajāni vedaḥ
RV yasyānakṣā duhitā jātvāsa kastāṃ vidvānabhimanyāte andhām
RV kataro meniṃ prati taṃ mucāte ya īṃvahāte ya īṃ vā vareyāt
RV kiyatī yoṣā maryato vadhūyoḥ pariprītā panyasāvāryeṇa
RV bhadrā vadhūrbhavati yat supeśāḥ svayaṃ sāmitraṃ vanute jane cit
RV patto jagāra pratyañcamatti śīrṣṇā śiraḥ prati dadhauvarūtham
RV āsīna ūrdhvāmupasi kṣiṇāti nyaṃṃ uttānāmanveti bhūmim
RV bṛhannachāyo apalāśo arvā tasthau mātā viṣito attigarbhaḥ
RV anyasyā vatsaṃ rihatī mimāya kayā bhuvā nidadhe dhenurūdhaḥ
RV sapta vīrāso adharādudāyannaṣṭottarāttāt samajagmiran te
RV nava paścātāt sthivimanta āyan daśa prāksānu vi tirantyaśnaḥ
RV daśānāmekaṃ kapilaṃ samānaṃ taṃ hinvanti kratavepāryāya
RV garbhaṃ mātā sudhitaṃ vakṣaṇāsvavenantantuṣayantī bibharti
RV pīvānaṃ meṣamapacanta vīrā nyuptā akṣā anu dīvaāsan
RV dvā dhanuṃ bṛhatīmapsvantaḥ pavitravantā carataḥpunantā
RV vi krośanāso viṣvañca āyan pacāti nemo nahi pakṣadardhaḥ
RV ayaṃ me devaḥ savitā tadāha drvanna id vanavatsarpirannaḥ
RV apaśyaṃ grāmaṃ vahamānamārādacakrayā svadhayāvartamānam
RV siṣaktyaryaḥ pra yugā janānāṃ sadyaḥśiśnā pramināno navīyān
RV etau me gāvau pramarasya yuktau mo ṣu pra sedhīrmuhurinmamandhi
RV āpaścidasya vi naśantyarthaṃ sūraśca markauparo babhūvān
RV ayaṃ yo vajraḥ purudhā vivṛtto 'vaḥ sūryasya bṛhataḥpurīṣāt
RV śrava idenā paro anyadasti tadavyathījarimāṇastaranti
RV vṛkṣevṛkṣe niyatā mīmayad gaustato vayaḥ pra patānpuruṣādaḥ
RV athedaṃ viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ bhayāta idrāyasunvad ṛṣaye ca śikṣat
RV devānāṃ māne prathamā atiṣṭhan kṛntatradeṣamupara udāyan
RV trayastapanti pṛthivimanūpa dva bṛbūkaṃ vahataḥpurīṣam
RV sā te jīvāturuta tasya viddhi ma smaitādṛgapa gūhaḥsamarye
RV aviḥ svaḥ kṛṇute gūhate busaṃ sa pādurasyanirṇijo na mucyate
RV viśvo hyanyo arirājagāma mamedaha śvaśuro na jagāma
RV jakṣīyād dhanā uta somaṃ papīyāt svāśitaḥ punarastaṃ jagāyāt
RV sa roruvad vṛṣabhastigmaśṛngo varṣman tasthāu varimannāpṛthivyāḥ
RV viśveṣvenaṃ vṛjaneṣu pāmi yo me kukṣisutasomaḥ pṛṇāti
RV adriṇā te mandina indra tūyān sunvanti somān pibasi tvameśām
RV pacanti te vṛṣabhānatsi teṣāṃ pṛkṣeṇa yanmaghavan hūyamānaḥ
RV idaṃ su me jaritarā cikiddhi pratīpaṃ śāpaṃ nadyovahanti
RV lopāśaḥ siṃhaṃ pratyañcamatsāḥ kroṣṭāvarāhaṃ niratakta kakṣāt
RV katha ta etadahamā ciketaṃ gṛtsasya pākastavasomanīṣām
RV tvaṃ no vidvān ṛtuthā vi voco yamardhaṃ temaghavan kṣemyā dhūḥ
RV evā hi māṃ tavasaṃ vardhayanti divaścin me bṛhatauttarā dhuḥ
RV purū sahasrā ni śiśāmi sākamaśatruṃhi ma janitā jajāna
RV evā hi māṃ tavasaṃ jajñurugraṃ karmankarman vṛṣaṇamindra devāḥ
RV vadhīṃ vṛtraṃ vajreṇa mandasano 'pa vrajammahinā dāśuṣe vam
RV devāsa āyan paraśūnrabibhran vanā vṛścanto abhi viḍbhirāyan
RV ni sudrvaṃ dadhato vakṣaṇāsu yatrā kṛpīṭamanutad dahanti
RV śaśaḥ kṣuraṃ pratyañcaṃ jagārādriṃ logena vyabhedamārāt
RV bṛhantaṃ cid ṛhate randhayāni vayad vatso vṛṣabhaṃśūśuvānaḥ
RV suparṇa itthā nakhamā siṣāyāvaruddhaḥ paripadaṃ nasiṃhaḥ
RV niruddhaścin mahiṣastarṣyāvān godhā tasmāayathaṃ karṣadetat
RV tebhyo godhā ayathaṃ karṣadetad ye brahmaṇaḥ pratipiyantyannaiḥ
RV sima ukṣṇo 'vasṛṣṭānadanti svayaṃ balānitanvaḥ śṛṇānāḥ
RV ete śamībhiḥ suśamī abhūvan ye hinvire tanvaḥ somaukthaiḥ
RV nṛvad vadannupa no māhi vājān divi śravodadhiṣe nāma vīraḥ
RV vane na vā yo nyadhāyi cākañchucirvāṃ stomo bhuraṇāvajīgaḥ
RV yasyedindraḥ purudineṣu hotā nṛṇāṃ naryonṛtamaḥ kṣapāvān
RV pra te asyā uṣasaḥ prāparasyā nṛtau syāma nṛtamasyanṛṇām
RV anu triśokaḥ śatamāvahan nṝn kutsena ratho yoasat sasavān
RV kaste mada indra rantyo bhūd duro giro abhyugro vi dhāva
RV kad vāho arvāgupa mā manīṣā ā tvā śakyamupamaṃrādho annaiḥ
RV kadu dyumnamindra tvāvato nṝn kayā dhiyā karase kan naāgan
RV mitro na satya urugāya bhṛtyā anne samasya yadasanmanīṣāḥ
RV preraya sūro arthaṃ na pāraṃ ye asya kāmaṃ janidhā ivagman
RV giraśca ye te tuvijāta pūrvīrnara indrapratiśikṣantyannaiḥ
RV mātre nu te sumite indra pūrvī dyaurmajmanā pṛthivīkāvyena
RV varāya te ghṛtavantaḥ sutāsaḥ svādman bhavantupītaye madhūni
RV ā madhvo asmā asicannamatramindrāya pūrṇaṃ sa hisatyarādhāḥ
RV sa vāvṛdhe varimannā pṛthivyā abhi kratvānaryaḥ pauṃsyaiśca
RV vyānaḷ indraḥ pṛtanāḥ svojā āsmai yatante sakhyāyapūrvīḥ
RV ā smā rathaṃ na pṛtanāsu tiṣṭha yaṃ bhadrayāsumatyā codayāse
RV pra devatrā brāhmaṇe gāturetvapo achā manaso naprayukti
RV mahīṃ mitrasya varuṇasya dhāsiṃ pṛthujrayaserīradhā suvṛktim
RV adhvaryavo haviṣmanto hi bhūtāchāpa itośatīruśantaḥ
RV ava yāścaṣṭe aruṇaḥ suparṇastamāsyadhvamūrmimadyā suhastāḥ
RV adhvaryavo 'pa itā samudramapāṃ napātaṃ haviṣā yajadhvam
RV sa vo dadadūrmimadyā supūtaṃ tasmai somaṃ madhumantaṃsunota
RV yo anidhmo dīdayadapsvantaryaṃ viprāsa īḷateadhvareṣu
RV apāṃ napān madhumatīrapo dā yābhirindrovāvṛdhe vīryāya
RV yābhiḥ somo modate harṣate ca kalyāṇībhiryuvatibhirnamaryaḥ
RV tā adhvaryo apo achā parehi yadāsiñcāoṣadhībhiḥ punītāt
RV eved yūne yuvatayo namanta yadīmuśannuśatīretyacha
RV saṃ jānate manasā saṃ cikitre 'dhvaryavo dhiṣaṇāpaścadevīḥ
RV yo vo vṛtābhyo akṛṇodu lokaṃ yo vo mahyā abhiśasteramuñcat
RV tasmā indrāya madhumantamūrmiṃ devamādanampra hiṇotanāpaḥ
RV prāsmai hinota madhumantamūrmiṃ garbho yo vaḥ sindhavomadhva utsaḥ
RV ghṛtapṛṣṭhamīḍyamadhvareṣvāpo revatīḥśṛṇutā havaṃ me
RV taṃ sindhavo matsaramindrapānamūrmiṃ pra heta ya ubheiyarti
RV madacyutamauśānaṃ nabhojāṃ pari tritantuṃvicarantamutsam
RV āvarvṛtatīradha nu dvidhārā goṣuyudho na niyavaṃcarantīḥ
RV ṛṣe janitrīrbhuvanasya patnīrapo vandasvasavṛdhaḥ sayonīḥ
RV hinotā no adhvaraṃ devayajyā hinota brahma sanayedhanānām
RV ṛtasya yoge vi śyadhvamūdhaḥ śruṣṭīvarīrbhūtanāsmabhyamāpaḥ
RV āpo revatīḥ kṣayathā hi vasvaḥ kratuṃ ca bhadrambibhṛthāmṛtaṃ ca
RV rāyaśca stha svapatyasya patnīḥsarasvatī tad gṛṇate vayo dhāt
RV prati yadāpo adṛśramāyatīrghṛtaṃ payāṃsi bibhratīrmadhūni
RV adhvaryubhirmanasā saṃvidānā indrāya somaṃsuṣutaṃ bharantīḥ
RV emā agman revatīrjīvadhanyā adhvaryavaḥ sādayatāsakhāyaḥ
RV ni barhiṣi dhattana somyāso 'pāṃ naptrāsaṃvidānāsa enāḥ
RV āgmannāpa uśatīrbarhiredaṃ nyadhvare asadandevayantīḥ
RV adhvaryavaḥ sunutendrāya somamabhūdu vaḥsuśakā devayajyā
RV ā no devānāmupa vetu śaṃso viśvebhisturairavaseyajatraḥ
RV tebhirvayaṃ suṣakhāyo bhavema taranto viśvāduritā syāma
RV pari cin marto draviṇaṃ mamanyād ṛtasya pathā namasāvivāset
RV ata svena kratunā saṃ vadeta śreyāṃsandakṣaṃ manasā jagṛbhyāt
RV adhāyi dhītirasasṛgramaṃśāstīrthe
na dasmamupayantyumāḥ
RV abhyānaśma suvitasya śūṣaṃ navedasoamṛtānāmabhūma
RV nityaścākanyāt svapatirdāmūnā yasmā u devaḥ savitajajāna
RV bhago vā gobhiraryamemanajyāt so asmai caruśchadayaduta syāt
RV iyaṃ sā bhūyā uṣasāmiva kṣa yad dha kṣumantaḥśavasā samāyan
RV asya stutiṃ jariturbhikṣamāṇā ānaḥ śagmāsa upa yantu vājāḥ
RV asyedeṣā sumatiḥ paprathānābhavat pūrvyā bhumanāgauḥ
RV asya sanīḷā asurasya yonau samāna ā bharaṇebibhramāṇāḥ
RV kiṃ svid vanaṃ ka u sa vṛkṣa āsa yato dyāvāpṛthivīniṣṭatakṣuḥ
RV santasthāne ajare itaūtī ahāni pūrvīruṣaso jaranta
RV naitāvadenā paro anyadastyukṣā sa dyāvāpṛthivībibharti
RV tvadaṃ pavitraṃ kṛṇuta svadhāvān yadīṃsūryaṃ na harito vahanti
RV stego na kṣāmatyeti pṛthvīṃ mihaṃ na vāto vi havāti bhūma
RV mitro yatra varuṇo ajyamāno 'gnirvane na vyasṛṣṭa śokam
RV starīryat sūta sadyo ajyamānā vyathiravyathiḥ kṛṇutasvagopā
RV putro yat purvaḥ pitrorjaniṣṭa śamyāṃ gaurjagāra yad dha pṛchān
RV uta kaṇvaṃ nṛṣadaḥ putramāhuruta śyāvo dhanamādattavāji
RV pra kṛṣṇāya ruśadapinvatodharṛtamatra nakirasmā apīpet
RV pra su gmantā dhiyasānasya sakṣaṇi varebhirvarānabhiṣu prasīdataḥ
RV asmākamindra ubhayaṃ jujoṣati yatsomyasyāndhaso bubodhati
RV vīndra yāsi divyāni rocanā vi pārthivāni rajasāpuruṣṭuta
RV ye tvā vahanti muhuradhvarānupa te suvanvantu vagyanānarādhasaḥ
RV tadin me chantsat vapuṣo vapuṣṭaraṃ putro yajjānampitroradhīyati
RV jāyā patiṃ vahati vagnunā sumat puṃsaid bhadro vahatuḥ pariṣkṛtaḥ
RV tadit sadhasthamabhi cāru dīdhaya gāvo yacchāsanvahatuṃ na dhenavaḥ
RV mātā yan manturyūthasyapūrvyābhi vāṇasya saptadhāturijjanaḥ
RV pra vo 'chā ririce devayuṣ padameko rudrebhiryātiturvaṇiḥ
RV jarā vā yeṣvamṛteṣu dāvane pari vaūmebhyaḥ siñcatā madhu
RV nidhīyamānamapagūḷamapsu pra me devānāṃ vratapāuvāca
RV indro vidvānanu hi tvā cacakṣa tenāhamagneanuśiṣṭa āgām
RV akṣetravit kṣetravidaṃ hyaprāṭ sa praitikṣetravidānuśiṣṭaḥ
RV etad vai bhadramanuśāsanosyotasrutiṃ vindatyañjasīnām
RV adyedu prāṇīdamamannimāhāpīvṛto adhayan māturūdhaḥ
RV emenamāpa jarimā yuvānamaheḷan vasuḥ sumanābabhūva
RV etāni bhadrā kalaśa kriyāma kuruśravaṇa dadato maghāni
RV dāna id vo maghavānaḥ so astvayaṃ ca somo hṛdi yambibharmi
RV pra mā yuyujre prayujo janānāṃ vahāmi sma puṣaṇamantareṇa
RV viśve devāso adha māmarakṣan duḥśāsurāgāditi ghoṣa āsīt
RV saṃ mā tapantyabhitaḥ sapatnīriva parśavaḥ
RV ni bādhateamatirnagnatā jasurverna vevīyate matiḥ
RV mūṣo na śiśnā vyadanti mādhya stotāraṃ te śatakrato
RV sakṛt su no maghavannindra mṛḷayādhā piteva no bhava
RV kuruśravaṇamāvṛṇi rājānaṃ trāsadasyavam
RV maṃhiṣṭhaṃvāghatām ṛṣiḥ
RV yasya mā harito rathe tisro vahanti sādhuyā
RV stavaisahasradakṣiṇe
RV yasya prasvādaso gira upamaśravasaḥ pituḥ
RV kṣetraṃ naraṇvamūcuṣe
RV adhi putropamaśravo napān mitrātitherihi
RV pituṣ ṭe asmivanditā
RV yadīśīyāmṛtānāmuta vā martyānām
RV jīvedinmaghavā mama
RV na devānāmati vrataṃ śatātmā cana jīvati
RV tathāyujā vi vāvṛte
RV prāvepā mā bṛhato mādayanti pravātejā iriṇe varvṛtānāḥ
RV somasyeva maujavatasya bhakṣo vibhīdako jāgṛvirmahyamachān
RV na mā mimetha na jihīḷa eṣā śivā sakhibhya uta mahyamāsīt
RV akṣasyāhamekaparasya hetoranuvratāmapa jāyāmarodham
RV dveṣṭi śvaśrūrapa jāyā ruṇaddhi na nāthito vindatemarḍitāram
RV aśvasyeva jarato vasnyasya nāhaṃ vindāmikitavasya bhogam
RV anye jāyāṃ pari mṛśantyasya yasyāgṛdhad vedane vājyakṣaḥ
RV pitā matā bhrātara enamāhurna jānīmo nayatābaddhametam
RV yadādīdhye na daviṣāṇyebhiḥ parāyadbhyo 'va hīyesakhibhyaḥ
RV nyuptāśca babhravo vācamakratanemīdeṣāṃ niṣkṛtaṃ jāriṇīva
RV sabhāmeti kitavaḥ pṛchamāno jeṣyāmīti tanvāśūśujānaḥ
RV akṣāso asya vi tiranti kāmaṃ pratidīvnedadhata ā kṛtāni
RV akṣāsa idan
kuśino nitodino nikṛtvānastapanāstāpayiṣṇavaḥ
RV kumāradeṣṇā jayataḥ punarhaṇo madhvāsampṛktāḥ kitavasya barhaṇā
RV tripañcāśaḥ krīḷati vrāta eṣāṃ deva iva savitāsatyadharmā
RV ugrasya cin manyave nā namante rājā cidebhyonama it kṛṇoti
RV nīcā vartanta upari sphurantyahastāso hastavantaṃ sahante
RV divyā aṅgārā iriṇe nyuptāḥ śītāḥ santo hṛdayaṃnirdahanti
RV jāyā tapyate kitavasya hīnā mātā putrasya carataḥ kvasvit
RV ṛṇāvā bibhyad dhanamichamāno 'nyeṣāmastamupanaktameti
RV striyaṃ dṛṣṭvāya kitavaṃ tatāpānyeṣāṃ jāyāṃsukṛtaṃ ca yonim
RV pūrvāhṇe aśvān yuyuje hi babhrūn soagnerante vṛṣalaḥ papāda
RV yo vaḥ senānīrmahato gaṇasya rājā vrātasya prathamobabhūva
RV tasmai kṛṇomi na dhanā ruṇadhmi daśāhamprācīstad ṛtaṃ vadāmi
RV akṣairmā dīvyaḥ kṛṣimit kṛṣasva vitte ramasva bahumanyamānaḥ
RV tatra gāvaḥ kitava tatra jāyā tan me vicaṣṭe savitāyamaryaḥ
RV mitraṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ khalu mṛlatā no mā no ghoreṇa caratābhidhṛṣṇu
RV ni vo nu manyurviśatāmarātiranyo babhrūṇāmprasitau nvastu
RV abudhramu tya indravanto agnayo jyotirbharanta uṣasovyuṣṭiṣu
RV mahī dyāvāpṛthivī cetatāmapo 'dyādevānāmava ā vṛṇīmahe
RV divaspṛthivyorava ā vṛṇīmahe mātṝn sindhūn parvatāñcharyaṇāvataḥ
RV anāgāstvaṃ sūryamuṣāsamīmahe bhadraṃsomaḥ suvāno adyā kṛṇotu naḥ
RV dyāvā no adya pṛthivī anāgaso mahī trāyetāṃ suvitāyamātarā
RV uṣā uchantyapa bādhatāmaghaṃ svastyagniṃsamidhānamīmahe
RV iyaṃ na usrā prathamā sudevyaṃ revat sanibhyo revatī vyuchatu
RV āre manyuṃ durvidatrasya dhīmahi svastyagniṃsamidhānamīmahe
RV pra yāḥ sisrate sūryasya raśmibhirjyotirbharantīruṣaso vyuṣṭiṣu
RV bhadrā no adya śravase vyuchata svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV anamīvā uṣasa ā carantu na udagnayo jihatāṃ jyotiṣābṛhat
RV āyukṣātāmaśvinā tūtujiṃ rathaṃ svastyagniṃsamidhānamīmahe
RV śreṣṭhaṃ no adya savitarvareṇyaṃ bhāgamā suva sa hiratnadhā asi
RV rāyo janitrīṃ dhiṣaṇāmupa bruve svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV pipartu mā tad ṛtasya pravācanaṃ devānāṃ yan manuṣyāamanmahi
RV viśvā idusrā spaḷ udeti sūryaḥ svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV adveṣo adya barhiṣa starīmaṇi grāvṇāṃ yoge manmanaḥsādha īmahe
RV ādityānāṃ śarmaṇi sthā bhuraṇyasi svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV ā no barhiḥ sadhamāde bṛhad divi devānīḷe sādayāsapta hotṝn
RV indraṃ mitraṃ varuṇaṃ sātaye bhagaṃ svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV ta ādityā ā gatā sarvatātaye vṛdhe no yajñamavatāsajoṣasaḥ
RV bṛhaspatiṃ pūṣaṇamaśvinā bhagaṃ svastyagniṃ samidhānamīmahe
RV tan no devā yachata supravācanaṃ chardirādityāḥ subharaṃnṛpāyyam
RV paśve tokāya tanayāya jīvase svastyagniṃsamidhānamīmahe
RV viśve adya maruto viśva ūtī viśve bhavantvagnayaḥsamiddhāḥ
RV viśve no devā avasā gamantu viśvamastudraviṇaṃ vājo asme
RV yaṃ devāso 'vatha vājasātau yaṃ trāyadhve yaṃ pipṛthātyaṃhaḥ
RV yo vo gopīthe na bhayasya veda te syāmadevavītaye turāsaḥ
RV uṣāsānaktā bṛhatī supeśasā dyāvākṣāmā varuṇomitro aryamā
RV indraṃ huve marutaḥ parvatānapa ādityāndyāvāpṛthivī apaḥ svaḥ
RV dyauśca naḥ pṛthivī ca pracetasa ṛtāvarī rakṣatāmaṃhasoriṣaḥ
RV mā durvidatrā nirṛtirna īśata tad devānāmavoadyā vṛṇīmahe
RV viśvasmān no aditiḥ pātvaṃhaso mātā mitrasya varuṇasyarevataḥ
RV svarvajjyotiravṛkaṃ naśīmahi tad devānāṃ 
RV grāvā vadannapa rakṣāṃsi sedhatu duṣvapnyaṃ nirṛtiṃviśvamatriṇam
RV ādityaṃ śarma marutāmaśīmahi taddevānāṃ 
RV endro barhiḥ sīdatu pinvatāmiḷā bṛhaspatiḥ sāmabhirṛkvo arcatu
RV supraketaṃ jīvase manma dhīmahi taddevānāṃ 
RV divispṛśaṃ yajñamasmākamaśvinā jīrādhvaraṃ kṛṇutaṃsumnamiṣṭaye
RV prācīnaraśmimāhutaṃ ghṛtena taddevānāṃ 
RV upa hvaye suhavaṃ mārutaṃ gaṇaṃ pāvakam ṛṣvaṃ sakhyāyaśambhuvam
RV rāyas poṣaṃ sauśravasāya dhīmahi taddevānāṃ 
RV apāṃ peruṃ jīvadhanyaṃ bharāmahe devāvyaṃ suhavamadhvaraśriyam
RV suraśmiṃ somamindriyaṃ yamīmahi taddevānāṃ 
RV sanema tat susanitā sanitvabhirvayaṃ jīvā jīvaputrāanāgasaḥ
RV brahmadviṣo viṣvageno bharerata taddevānāṃ 
RV ye sthā manoryajñiyāste śṛṇotana yad vo devā īmahetad dadātana
RV jaitraṃ kratuṃ rayimad vīravad yaśastaddevānāṃ 
RV mahadadya mahatāmā vṛṇīmahe 'vo devānāṃ bṛhatāmanarvaṇām
RV yathā vasu vīrajātaṃ naśāmahai taddevānāṃ 
RV maho agneḥ samidhānasya śarmaṇyanāgā mitre varuṇesvastaye
RV śreṣṭhe syāma savituḥ savīmani taddevānāṃ 
RV ye savituḥ satyasavasya viśve mitrasya vrate varuṇasyadevāḥ
RV te saubhagaṃ vīravad gomadapno dadhātanadraviṇaṃ citramasme
RV savitā paścātāt savitā purastāt savitottarāttātsavitādharāttāt
RV savitā naḥ suvatu sarvatātiṃ savitā norāsatāṃ dīrghamayuḥ
RV namo mitrasya varuṇasya cakṣase maho devāya tad ṛtaṃsaparyata
RV dūredṛśe devajātāya ketave divas putrāyasūryāya śaṃsata
RV sā mā satyoktiḥ pari pātu viśvato dyāvā ca yatratatanannahāni ca
RV viśvamanyan ni viśate yadejativiśvāhāpo viśvāhodeti sūryaḥ
RV na te adevaḥ pradivo ni vāsate yadetaśebhiḥ patarairatharyasi
RV prācīnamanyadanu vartate raja udanyenajyotiṣā yāsi sūrya
RV yena sūrya jyotiṣā bādhase tamo jagacca viśvamudiyarṣibhānunā
RV tenāsmad viśvāmanirāmanāhutimapāmīvāmapa duṣvapnyaṃ suva
RV viśvasya hi preṣito rakṣasi vratamaheḷayannuccarasisvadhā anu
RV yadadya tvā sūryopabravāmahai taṃ no devāanu maṃsīrata kratum
RV taṃ no dyāvāpṛthivī tan na āpa indraḥ śṛṇvantu marutohavaṃ vacaḥ
RV mā śūne bhūma sūryasya sandṛśibhadraṃ jīvanto jaraṇāmaśīmahi
RV viśvāhā tvā sumanasaḥ sucakṣasaḥ prajāvanto anamīvāanāgasaḥ
RV udyantaṃ tvā mitramaho divedive jyog jīvāḥprati paśyema sūrya
RV mahi jyotirbibhrataṃ tvā vicakṣaṇa bhāsvantaṃ cakṣuṣe cakṣuṣe mayaḥ
RV ārohantaṃ bṛhataḥ pājasas pari vayaṃjīvāḥ prati paśyema sūrya
RV yasya te viśvā bhuvanāni ketunā pra cerate ni ca viśanteaktubhiḥ
RV anāgāstvena harikeśa sūryāhnāhnā novasyasāvasyasodihi
RV śaṃ no bhava cakṣasā śaṃ no ahnā śaṃ bhānunā śaṃhimā śaṃ ghṛṇena
RV yathā śamadhvañchamasad duroṇetat sūrya draviṇaṃ dhehi citram
RV asmākaṃ devā ubhayāya janmane śarma yachata dvipadecatuṣpade
RV adat pibadūrjayamānamāśitaṃ tadasmeśaṃ yorarapo dadhātana
RV yad vo devāścakṛma jihvayā guru manaso vā prayutīdevaheḷanam
RV arāvā yo no abhi duchunāyate tasmin tadenovasavo ni dhetana
RV asmin na indra pṛtsutau yaśasvati śimīvati krandasi prāvasātaye
RV yatra goṣātā dhṛṣiteṣu khādiṣu viṣvakpatanti didyavo nṛṣāhye
RV sa naḥ kṣumantaṃ sadane vyūrṇuhi goarṇasaṃ rayimindraśravāyyam
RV syāma te jayataḥ śakra medino yathā vayamuśmasi tad vaso kṛdhi
RV yo no dāsa āryo vā puruṣṭutādeva indra yudhaye ciketati
RV asmābhiṣ ṭe suṣahāḥ santu śatravastvayā vayaṃ tānvanuyāma saṃgame
RV yo dabhrebhirhavyo yaśca bhūribhiryo abhīke varivovinnṛṣāhye
RV taṃ vikhāde sasnimadya śrutaṃ naramarvāñcamindramavase karāmahe
RV svavṛjaṃ hi tvāmahamindra śuśravānānudaṃ vṛṣabharadhracodanam
RV pra muñcasva pari kutsādihā gahi kimutvāvān muṣkayorbaddha āsate
RV yo vāṃ parijmā suvṛdaśvinā ratho doṣāmuṣāso havyohaviṣmatā
RV śaśvattamāsastamu vāmidaṃ vayaṃ piturnanāma suhavaṃ havāmahe
RV codayataṃ sūnṛtāḥ pinvataṃ dhiya ut purandhīrīrayatantaduśmasi
RV yaśasaṃ bhāgaṃ kṛṇutaṃ no aśvinā somaṃ nacāruṃ maghavatsu nas kṛtam
RV amājuraścid bhavatho yuvaṃ bhago 'nāśościdavitārāpamasya cit
RV andhasya cin nāsatyā kṛśasya cid yuvāmidāhurbhiṣajā rutasya cit
RV yuvaṃ cyavānaṃ sanayaṃ yathā rathaṃ punaryuvānaṃcarathāya takṣathuḥ
RV niṣ ṭaugryamūhathuradbhyas pariviśvet tā vāṃ savaneṣu pravācyā
RV purāṇā vāṃ vīryā pra bravā jane 'tho hāsathurbhiṣajāmayobhuvā
RV tā vāṃ nu navyāvavase karāmahe 'yaṃnāsatyā śradariryathā dadhat
RV iyaṃ vāmahve śṛṇutaṃ me aśvinā putrāyeva pitarā mahyaṃśikṣatam
RV anāpirajñā asajātyāmatiḥ purā tasyāabhiśasterava spṛtam
RV yuvaṃ rathena vimadāya śundhyuvaṃ nyūhathuḥ purumitrasyayoṣaṇām
RV yuvaṃ havaṃ vadhrimatyā agachataṃ yuvaṃsuṣutiṃ cakrathuḥ purandhaye
RV yuvaṃ viprasya jaraṇāmupeyuṣaḥ punaḥ kalerakṛṇutaṃyuvad vayaḥ
RV yuvaṃ vandanam ṛśyadādudūpathuryuvaṃsadyo viśpalāmetave kṛthaḥ
RV yuvaṃ ha rebhaṃ vṛṣaṇā guhā hitamudairayatammamṛvāṃsamaśvinā
RV yuvam ṛbīsamuta taptamatrayaomanvantaṃ cakrathuḥ saptavadhraye
RV yuvaṃ śvetaṃ pedave 'śvināśvaṃ navabhirvājairnavatīca vājinam
RV carkṛtyaṃ dadathurdrāvayatsakhaṃ bhagaṃ nanṛbhyo havyaṃ mayobhubam
RV na taṃ rājānāvadite kutaścana nāṃho aśnoti duritaṃnakirbhayam
RV yamaśvinā suhavā rudravartanī purorathaṃkṛṇuthaḥ patnyā saha
RV ā tena yātaṃ manaso javīyasā rathaṃ yaṃ vām ṛbhavaścakruraśvinā
RV yasya yoge duhitā jāyate diva ubhe ahanīsudine vivasvataḥ
RV tā vartiryātaṃ jayuṣā vi parvatamapinvataṃ śayavedhenumaśvinā
RV vṛkasya cid vartikāmantarāsyād yuvaṃśacībhirgrasitāmamuñcatam
RV etaṃ vāṃ stomamaśvināvakarmātakṣāma bhṛgavo na ratham
RV nyamṛkṣāma yoṣaṇāṃ na marye nityaṃ na sūnuntanayaṃ dadhānāḥ
RV rathaṃ yāntaṃ kuha ko ha vāṃ narā prati dyumantaṃsuvitāya bhūṣati
RV prātaryāvāṇaṃ vibhvaṃ viśeviśevastor vastorvahamānaṃ dhiyā śami
RV kuha svid doṣā kuha vastoraśvinā kuhābhipitvaṃ karataḥkuhoṣatuḥ
RV ko vāṃ śayutrā vidhaveva devaraṃ maryaṃ nayoṣā kṛṇute sadhastha ā
RV prātarjarethe jaraṇeva kāpayā vastorvastoryajatā gachathogṛham
RV kasya dhvasrā bhavathaḥ kasya vā narā rājaputrevasavanāva gachathaḥ
RV yuvāṃ mṛgeva vāraṇā mṛgaṇyavo doṣā vastorhaviṣā nihvayāmahe
RV yuvaṃ hotrām ṛtuthā juhvate nareṣaṃ janāyavahathaḥ śubhas patī
RV yuvāṃ ha ghoṣā paryaśvinā yatī rājña ūce duhitāpṛche vāṃ narā
RV bhūtaṃ me ahna uta bhūtamaktave'śvāvate rathine śaktamarvate
RV yuvaṃ kavī ṣṭhaḥ paryaśvinā rathaṃ viśo na kutsojariturnaśāyathaḥ
RV yuvorha makṣā paryaśvinā madhvāsā bharata niṣkṛtaṃ na yoṣaṇā
RV yuvaṃ ha bhujyuṃ yuvamaśvinā vaśaṃ yuvaṃ śiñjāramuśanāmupārathuḥ
RV yuvo rarāvā pari sakhyamāsate yuvorahamavasā sumnamā cake
RV yuvaṃ ha kṛśaṃ yuvamaśvinā śayuṃ yuvaṃ vidhantaṃvidhavāmuruṣyathaḥ
RV yuvaṃ sanibhya stanayantamaśvināpavrajamūrṇuthaḥ saptāsyam
RV janiṣṭa yoṣā patayat kanīnako vi cāruhan vīrudhodaṃsanā anu
RV āsmai rīyante nivaneva sindhavo 'smā ahnebhavati tat patitvanam
RV jīvaṃ rudanti vi mayante adhvare dīrghāmanu prasitindīdhiyurnaraḥ
RV vāmaṃ pitṛbhyo ya idaṃ samerire mayaḥpatibhyo janayaḥ pariṣvaje
RV na tasya vidma tadu ṣu pra vocata yuvā ha yad yuvatyāḥkṣeti yoniṣu
RV priyosriyasya vṛṣabhasya retino gṛhaṃgamemāśvinā taduśmasi
RV ā vāmagan sumatirvājinīvasū nyaśvinā hṛtsu kāmāayaṃsata
RV abhūtaṃ gopā mithunā śubhas patī priyāaryamṇo duryānaśīmahi
RV tā mandasānā manuṣo duroṇa ā dhattaṃ rayiṃ sahavīraṃvacasyave
RV kṛtaṃ tīrthaṃ suprapāṇaṃ śubhas patīsthāṇuṃ patheṣṭhāmapa durmatiṃ hatam
RV kva svidadya katamāsvaśvinā vikṣu dasrā mādayeteśubhas patī
RV ka īṃ ni yeme katamasya jagmaturviprasya vāyajamānasya vā gṛham
RV samānamu tyaṃ puruhūtamukthyaṃ rathaṃ tricakraṃ savanāganigmatam
RV parijmānaṃ vidathyaṃ suvṛktibhirvayaṃvyuṣṭā uṣaso havāmahe
RV prātaryujaṃ nāsatyādhi tiṣṭhathaḥ prātaryāvāṇammadhuvāhanaṃ ratham
RV viśo yena gachatho yajvarīrnarākīreścid yajñaṃ hotṛmantamaśvinā
RV adhvaryuṃ vā madhupāṇiṃ suhastyamagnidhaṃ vādhṛtadakṣaṃ damūnasam
RV viprasya vā yat savanani gachatho'ta ā yātaṃ madhupeyamaśvinā
RV asteva su prataraṃ lāyamasyan bhūṣanniva pra bharāstomamasmai
RV vācā viprāstarata vācamaryo ni rāmayajaritaḥ soma indram
RV dohena gāmupa śikṣā sakhāyaṃ pra bodhaya jaritarjāramindram
RV kośaṃ na pūrṇaṃ vasunā nyṛṣṭamā cyāvayamaghadeyāya śūram
RV kimaṅga tvā maghavan bhojamāhuḥ śiśīhi mā śiśayantvā śṛṇomi
RV apnasvatī mama dhīrastu śakra vasuvidambhagamindrā bharā naḥ
RV tvāṃ janā mamasatyeṣvindra santasthānā vi hvayantesamīke
RV atrā yujaṃ kṛṇute yo haviṣmān nāsunvatāsakhyaṃ vaṣṭi śūraḥ
RV dhanaṃ na syandraṃ bahulaṃ yo asmai tīvrān somānāsunotiprayasvān
RV tasmai śatrūn sutukān prātarahno nisvaṣṭrān yuvati hanti vṛtram
RV yasmin vayaṃ dadhimā śaṃsamindre yaḥ śiśrāya maghavākāmamasme
RV ārāccit san bhayatāmasya śatrurnyasmaidyumnā janyā namantām
RV ārācchatrumapa bādhasva dūramugro yaḥ śambaḥpuruhūta tena
RV asme dhehi yavamad gomadindra kṛdhī dhiyaṃjaritre vājaratnām
RV pra yamantarvṛṣasavāso agman tīvrāḥ somā bahulāntāsaindram
RV nāha dāmānaṃ maghavā ni yaṃsan ni sunvate vahatibhūri vāmam
RV uta prahāmatidīvyā jayāti kṛtaṃ yacchvaghnī vicinotikāle
RV yo devakāmo na dhanā ruṇaddhi samit taṃ rāyāsṛjati svadhāvān
RV gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ durevāṃ yavena kṣudhaṃ puruhūtaviśvām
RV vayaṃ rājabhiḥ prathamā dhanānyasmākenavṛjanenā jayema
RV bṛhaspatirnaḥ pari pātu paścādutottarasmādadharādaghāyoḥ
RV idraḥ purastāduta madhyato naḥ sakhā sakhibhyovarivaḥ kṛṇotu
RV achā ma indraṃ matayaḥ svarvidaḥ sadhrīcīrviśvāuśatīranūṣata
RV pari ṣvajante janayo yathā patiṃ maryaṃna śundhyuṃ maghavānamūtaye
RV na ghā tvadrigapa veti me manastve it kāmaṃ puruhūtaśiśraya
RV rājeva dasma ni ṣado 'dhi barhiṣyasmin su some'vapānamastu te
RV viṣūvṛdindro amateruta kṣudhaḥ sa id rāyo maghavāvasva īśate
RV tasyedime pravaṇe sapta sindhavo vayovardhanti vṛṣabhasya śuṣmiṇaḥ
RV vayo na vṛkṣaṃ supalāśamāsadan somāsa indraṃ mandinaścamūṣadaḥ
RV praiṣāmanīkaṃ śavasā davidyutad vidatsvarmanave jyotirāryam
RV kṛtaṃ na śvaghnī vi cinoti devane saṃvargaṃ yan maghavāsūryaṃ jayat
RV na tat te anyo anu vīryaṃ śakan napurāṇo maghavan nota nūtanaḥ
RV viśaṃviśaṃ maghavā paryaśāyata janānāṃ dhenāavacākaśad vṛṣā
RV yasyāha śakraḥ savaneṣu raṇyati satīvraiḥ somaiḥ sahate pṛtanyataḥ
RV āpo na sindhumabhi yat samakṣaran somāsa indraṃ kulyāiva hradam
RV vardhanti viprā maho asya sādane yavaṃ navṛṣṭirdivyena dānunā
RV vṛṣā na kruddhaḥ patayad rajassvā yo aryapatnīrakṛṇodimā apaḥ
RV sa sunvate maghavā jīradānave 'vindajjyotirmanave haviṣmate
RV ujjāyatāṃ paraśurjyotiṣā saha bhūyā ṛtasya sudughāpurāṇavat
RV vi rocatāmaruṣo bhānunā śuciḥ svarṇaśukraṃ śuśucīta satpatiḥ
RV gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ 
RV bṛhaspatirnaḥ pari 
RV ā yātvindraḥ svapatirmadāya yo dharmaṇā tūtujānastuviṣmān
RV pratvakṣāṇo ati viśvā sahāṃsyapāreṇamahatā vṛṣṇyena
RV suṣṭhāmā rathaḥ suyamā harī te mimyakṣa vajro nṛpategabhastau
RV śībhaṃ rājan supathā yāhyarvāṃ vardhāmate papuṣo vṛṣṇyāni
RV endravāho nṛpatiṃ vajrabāhumugramugrāsastaviṣāsa enam
RV pratvakṣasaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ satyaśuṣmamemasmatrā sadhamādovahantu
RV evā patiṃ droṇasācaṃ sacetasamūrja skambhaṃ dharuṇaā vṛṣāyase
RV ojaḥ kṛṣva saṃ gṛbhāya tve apyaso yathākenipānāmino vṛdhe
RV gamannasme vasūnyā hi śaṃsiṣaṃ svāśiṣaṃ bharamāyāhi sominaḥ
RV tvamīśiṣe sāsminnā satsi barhiṣyanādhṛṣyā tava pātrāṇi dharmaṇā
RV pṛthak prāyan prathamā devahūtayo 'kṛṇvata śravasyāniduṣṭarā
RV na ye śekuryajñiyāṃ nāvamāruhamīrmaivate nyaviśanta kepayaḥ
RV evaivāpāgapare santu dūḍhyo 'śvā yeṣāṃ duryujaāyuyujre
RV itthā ye prāgupare santi dāvane purūṇiyatra vayunāni bhojanā
RV girīnrajrān rejamānānadhārayad dyauḥ krandadantarikṣāṇi kopayat
RV samīcīne dhiṣaṇe vi ṣkabhāyativṛṣṇaḥ pītvā mada ukthāni śaṃsati
RV imaṃ bibharmi sukṛtaṃ te aṅkuśaṃ yenārujāsi maghavañchaphārujaḥ
RV asmin su te savane astvokyaṃ suta iṣṭaumaghavan bodhyābhagaḥ
RV gobhiṣ ṭaremāmatiṃ 
RV bṛhaspatirnaḥ pari 
RV divas pari prathamaṃ jajñe agnirasmad dvitīyaṃ parijātavedāḥ
RV tṛtīyamapsu nṛmaṇā ajasramindhāna enaṃjarate svādhīḥ
RV vidmā te agne tredhā trayāṇi vidmā te dhāma vibhṛtāpurutrā
RV vidmā te nāma paramaṃ guhā yad vidmā tamutsaṃ yata ājagantha
RV samudre tvā nṛmaṇā apsvantarnṛcakṣā īdhe divo agnaūdhan
RV tṛtīye tvā rajasi tasthivāṃsamapāmupasthemahiṣā avardhan
RV akrandadagni stanayanniva dyauḥ kṣāmā rerihad vīrudhaḥsamañjan
RV sadyo jajñāno vi hīmiddho akhyadā rodasībhānunā bhātyantaḥ
RV śrīṇāmudāro dharuṇo rayīṇāṃ manīṣāṇāmprārpaṇaḥ somagopāḥ
RV vasuḥ sūnuḥ sahaso apsu rājāvi bhātyagra uṣasāmidhānaḥ
RV viśvasya keturbhuvanasya garbha ā rodasī apṛṇājjāyamānaḥ
RV vīḷuṃ cidadrimabhinat parāyañ janā yadagnimayajanta pañca
RV uśik pāvako aratiḥ sumedhā marteṣvagniramṛto ni dhāyi
RV iyarti dhūmamaruṣaṃ bharibhraducchukreṇa śociṣādyā inakṣan
RV dṛśāno rukma urviyā vyadyaud durmarṣamāyuḥ śriyerucānaḥ
RV agniramṛto abhavad vayobhiryadenaṃ dyaurjanayat suretāḥ
RV yaste adya kṛṇavad bhadraśoce 'pūpaṃ deva ghṛtavantamagne
RV pra taṃ naya prataraṃ vasyo achābhi sumnaṃ devabhaktaṃyaviṣṭha
RV ā taṃ bhaja sauśravaseṣvagna ukthauktha ā bhaja śasyamāne
RV priyaḥ sūrye priyo agnā bhavātyujjātena bhinadadujjanitvaiḥ
RV tvāmagne yajamānā anu dyūn viśvā vasu dadhire vāryāṇi
RV tvayā saha draviṇamichamānā vrajaṃ gomantamuśijo vivavruḥ
RV astāvyagnirnarāṃ suśevo vaiśvānara ṛṣibhiḥsomagopāḥ
RV adveṣe dyāvāpṛthivī huvema devā dhatta rayimasme suvīram
RV pra hotā jāto mahān nabhovin nṛṣadvā sīdadapāmupasthe
RV dadhiryo dhāyi sa te vayāṃsi yantā vasūni vidhatetanūpāḥ
RV imaṃ vidhanto apāṃ sadhasthe paśuṃ na naṣṭaṃ padairanu gman
RV guhā catantamuśijo namobhirichanto dhīrābhṛgavo 'vindan
RV imaṃ trito bhūryavindadichan vaibhūvaso mūrdhanyaghnyāyāḥ
RV sa śevṛdho jāta ā harmyeṣu nābhiryuvābhavati rocanasya
RV mandraṃ hotāramuśijo namobhiḥ prāñcaṃ yajñaṃ netāramadhvarāṇām
RV viśāmakṛṇvannaratiṃ pāvakaṃ havyavāhandadhato mānuṣeṣu
RV pra bhūrjayantaṃ mahāṃ vipodhāṃ mūrā amūraṃ purāndarmāṇam
RV nayanto garbhaṃ vanāṃ dhiyaṃ dhurhiriśmaśruṃ nārvāṇaṃ dhanarcam
RV ni pastyāsu trita stabhūyan parivīto yonau sīdadantaḥ
RV ataḥ saṃgṛbhyā viśāṃ damūnā vidharmaṇāyantrairīyatenṝn
RV asyājarāso damāmaritrā arcaddhūmāso agnayaḥ pāvakāḥ
RV śvitīcayaḥ śvātrāso bhuraṇyavo vanarṣado vāyavo nasomāḥ
RV pra jihvayā bharate vepo agniḥ pra vayunāni cetasāpṛthivyāḥ
RV tamāyavaḥ śucayantaṃ pāvakaṃ mandraṃhotāraṃ dadhire yajiṣṭham
RV dyāvā yamagniṃ pṛthivī janiṣṭāmāpastvaṣṭā bhṛgavoyaṃ sahobhiḥ
RV īḷenyaṃ prathamaṃ mātariśvā devāstatakṣurmanave yajatram
RV yaṃ tvā devā dadhire havyavāhaṃ puruspṛho mānuṣāsoyajatram
RV sa yāmannagne stuvate vayo dhāḥ pra devayanyaśasaḥ saṃ hi pūrvīḥ
RV jagṛbhmā te dakṣiṇamindra hastaṃ vasūyavo vasupatevasūnām
RV vidmā hi tvā gopatiṃ śūra gonāmasmabhyaṃcitraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV svāyudhaṃ svavasaṃ sunīthaṃ catuḥsamudraṃ dharunaṃrayīṇām
RV carkṛtyaṃ śaṃsyaṃ bhūrivāramasmabhyaṃcitraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV subrahmāṇaṃ devavantaṃ bṛhantamuruṃ gabhīraṃ pṛthubudhnamindra
RV śrutaṛṣimugramabhimātiṣāhamasmabhyaṃ citraṃvṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV sanadvājaṃ vipravīraṃ tarutraṃ dhanaspṛtaṃ śūśuvāṃsaṃsudakṣam
RV dasyuhanaṃ pūrbhidamindra satyamasmabhyaṃcitraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV aśvāvantaṃ rathinaṃ vīravantaṃ sahasriṇaṃ śatinaṃvājamindra
RV bhadravrātaṃ vipravīraṃ svarṣāmasmabhyaṃcitraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV pra saptagum ṛtadhītiṃ sumedhāṃ bṛhaspatiṃ matirachājigāti
RV ya āṅgiraso namasopasadyo 'smabhyaṃ citraṃvṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV vanīvāno mama dūtāsa indraṃ stomāścaranti sumatīriyānāḥ
RV hṛdispṛśo manasā vacyamānā asmabhyaṃ citraṃvṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV yat tvā yāmi daddhi tan na indra bṛhantaṃ kṣayamasamaṃjanānām
RV abhi tad dyāvāpṛthivī gṛṇītāmasmabhyaṃcitraṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ rayiṃ dāḥ
RV ahaṃ bhuvaṃ vasunaḥ pūrvyas patirahaṃ dhanāni saṃjayāmi śaśvataḥ
RV māṃ havante pitaraṃ na jantavo 'handāśuṣe vi bhajāmi bhojanam
RV ahamindro rodho vakṣo atharvaṇastritāya gā ajanayamaheradhi
RV ahaṃ dasyubhyaḥ pari nṛmṇamā dade gotrā śikṣandadhīce mātariśvane
RV mahyaṃ tvaṣṭā vajramatakṣadāyasaṃ mayi devāso 'vṛjannapi kratum
RV mamānīkaṃ sūryasyeva duṣṭaraṃ māmāryantikṛtena kartvena ca
RV ahametaṃ gavyayamaśvyaṃ paśuṃ purīṣiṇaṃ sāyakenāhiraṇyayam
RV purū sahasrā ni śiśāmi dāśuṣe yan māsomāsa ukthino amandiṣuḥ
RV ahamindro na parā jigya id dhanaṃ na mṛtyave 'va tasthekadā cana
RV somamin mā sunvanto yācatā vasu na mepūravaḥ sakhye riṣāthana
RV ahametāñchāśvasato dvādvendraṃ ye vajraṃ yudhaye'kṛṇvata
RV āhvayamānānava hanmanāhanaṃ dṛḷā vadannanamasyurnamasvinaḥ
RV abhīdamekameko asmi niṣṣāḷ abhī dvā kimu trayaḥkaranti
RV khale na parṣān prati hanmi bhūri kiṃ mā nindantiśatravo 'nindrāḥ
RV ahaṃ guṅgubhyo atithigvamiṣkaramiṣaṃ na vṛtraturaṃvikṣu dhārayam
RV yat parṇayaghna uta vā karañjahe prāhammahe vṛtrahatye aśuśravi
RV pra me namī sāpya iṣe bhuje bhūd gavāmeṣe sakhyākṛṇuta dvitā
RV didyuṃ yadasya samitheṣu maṃhayamādidenaṃ śaṃsyamukthyaṃ karam
RV pra nemasmin dadṛśe somo antargopā nemamāvirasthākṛṇoti
RV sa tigmaśṛṅgaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ yuyutsan druhastasthaubahule baddho antaḥ
RV ādityānāṃ vasūnāṃ rudriyāṇāṃ devo devānāṃ namināmi dhāma
RV te mā bhadrāya śavase tatakṣuraparājitamastṛtamaṣāḷam
RV ahaṃ dāṃ gṛṇate pūrvyaṃ vasvahaṃ brahma kṛṇavaṃ mahyaṃvardhanam
RV ahaṃ bhuvaṃ yajamānasya coditāyajvanaḥ sākṣiviśvasmin bhare
RV māṃ dhurindraṃ nāma devatā divaśca gmaścāpāṃ cajantavaḥ
RV ahaṃ harī vṛṣaṇā vivratā raghū ahaṃvajraṃ śavase dhṛṣṇvā dade
RV ahamatkaṃ kavaye śiśnathaṃ hathairahaṃ kutsamāvamābhirūtibhiḥ
RV ahaṃ śuṣṇasya śnathitā vadharyamaṃna yo rara āryaṃ nāma dasyave
RV ahaṃ piteva vetasūnrabhiṣṭaye tugraṃ kutsāya smadibhaṃca randhayam
RV ahaṃ bhuvaṃ yajamānasya rājani pra yad bharetujaye na priyādhṛṣe
RV ahaṃ randhayaṃ mṛgayaṃ śrutarvaṇe yan mājihīta vayunācanānuṣak
RV ahaṃ veśaṃ namramāyave 'karamahaṃsavyāya paḍgṛbhimarandhayam
RV ahaṃ sa yo navavāstvaṃ bṛhadrathaṃ saṃ vṛtreva dāsaṃvṛtrahārujam
RV yad vardhayantaṃ prathayantamānuṣag dūrepāre rajaso rocanākaram
RV ahaṃ sūryasya pari yāmyāśubhiḥ praitaśebhirvahamānaojasā
RV yan mā sāvo manuṣa āha nirṇija ṛdhak kṛṣedāsaṃ kṛtvyaṃ hathaiḥ
RV ahaṃ saptahā nahuṣo nahuṣṭaraḥ prāśrāva yaṃ śavasāturvaśaṃ yadum
RV ahaṃ nyanyaṃ sahasā sahas karaṃ navavrādhato navatiṃ ca vakṣayam
RV ahaṃ sapta sravato dhārayaṃ vṛṣā dravitnvaḥ pṛthivyāṃsīrā adhi
RV ahamarṇāṃsi vi tirāmi sukraturyudhā vidammanave gātumiṣṭaye
RV ahaṃ tadāsu dhārayaṃ yadāsu na devaścanatvaṣṭādhārayad ruśat
RV spārhaṃ gavāmūdhassuvakṣaṇāsvā madhormadhu śvātryaṃ somamāśiram
RV evā devānindro vivye nṝn pra cyautnena maghavāsatyarādhāḥ
RV viśvet tā te harivaḥ śacīvo 'bhiturāsaḥ svayaśo gṛṇanti
RV pra vo mahe mandamānāyāndhaso 'rcā viśvānarāyaviśvābhuve
RV indrasya yasya sumakhaṃ saho mahi śravonṛmṇaṃ ca rodasī saparyataḥ
RV so cin nu sakhyā narya ina stutaścarkṛtya indro māvatenare
RV viśvāsu dhūrṣu vājakṛtyeṣu satpate vṛtre vāpsvabhi śūra mandase
RV ke te nara indra ye ta iṣe ye te sumnaṃ sadhanyamiyakṣān
RV ke te vājāyāsuryāya hinvire ke apsu svāsūrvarāsupauṃsye
RV bhuvastvamindra brahmaṇā mahān bhuvo viśveṣu savaneṣuyajñiyaḥ
RV bhuvo nṝṃścyautno viśvasmin bharejyeṣṭhaśca mantro viśvacarṣaṇe
RV avā nu kaṃ jyāyān yajñavanaso mahīṃ ta omātrāṃkṛṣṭayo viduḥ
RV aso nu kamajaro vardhāśca viśvedetāsavanā tūtumā kṛṣe
RV etā viśvā savanā tūtumākṛṣe svayaṃ sūno sahaso yānidadhiṣe
RV varāya te pātraṃ dharmaṇe tanā yajño mantrobrahmodyataṃ vacaḥ
RV ye te vipra brahmakṛtaḥ sute sacā vasūnāṃ ca vasunaścadāvane
RV pra te sumnasya manasā pathā bhuvan made sutasyasomyasyāndhasaḥ
RV mahat tadulbaṃ sthaviraṃ tadāsīd yenāviṣṭitaḥpraviveśithāpaḥ
RV viśvā apaśyad bahudhā te agne jātavedastanvo deva ekaḥ
RV ko mā dadarśa katamaḥ sa devo yo me tanvo bahudhāparyapaśyat
RV kvāha mitrāvaruṇā kṣiyantyagnervisvāḥsamidho devayānīḥ
RV aichāma tvā bahudhā jātavedaḥ praviṣṭamagne apsvoṣadhīṣu
RV taṃ tvā yamo acikeccitrabhāno daśāntaruṣyādatirocamānam
RV hotrādahaṃ varuṇa bibhyadāyaṃ nedeva mā yunajannatradevāḥ
RV tasya me tanvo bahudhā niviṣṭā etamarthaṃ naciketāhamagniḥ
RV ehi manurdevayuryajñakāmo 'raṃkṛtyā tamasi kṣeṣyagne
RV sugān pathaḥ kṛṇuhi devayānān vaha havyānisumanasyamānaḥ
RV agneḥ pūrve bhrātaro arthametaṃ rathīvādhvānamanvāvarīvuḥ
RV tasmād bhiyā varuṇa dūramāyaṃ gauro nakṣepnoravije jyāyāḥ
RV kurmasta āyurajaraṃ yadagne yathā yukto jātavedo nariṣyāḥ
RV athā vahāsi sumanasyamāno bhāgaṃ devebhyohaviṣaḥ sujāta
RV prayājān me anuyājāṃśca kevalānūrjasvantaṃ haviṣodatta bhāgam
RV ghṛtaṃ cāpāṃ puruṣaṃ cauṣadhīnāmagneśca dīrghamāyurastu devāḥ
RV tava prayājā anuyājāśca kevala ūrjasvanto haviṣaḥ santubhāgāḥ
RV tavāgne yajño 'yamastu sarvastubhyaṃ namantāmpradiśaścatasraḥ
RV viśve devāḥ śāstana mā yatheha hotā vṛto manavai yanniṣadya
RV pra me brūta bhāgadheyaṃ yathā vo yena pathāhavyamā vo vahāni
RV ahaṃ hotā nyasīdaṃ yajīyān viśve devā maruto mājunanti
RV aharaharaśvinādhvaryavaṃ vāṃ brahmā samid bhavatisāhutirvām
RV ayaṃ yo hotā kiru sa yamasya kamapyūhe yat samañjantidevāḥ
RV aharaharjāyate māsimāsyathā devā dadhirehavyavāham
RV māṃ devā dadhire havyavāhamapamluktaṃ bahu kṛchrācarantam
RV agnirvidvān yajñaṃ naḥ kalpayāti pañcayāmantrivṛtaṃ saptatantum
RV ā vo yakṣyamṛtatvaṃ suvīraṃ yathā vo devā varivaḥkarāṇi
RV ā bāhvorvajramindrasya dheyāmathemāviśvāḥ pṛtanā jayāti
RV trīṇi śatā trī sahasrāṇyagniṃ triṃśacca devā navacāsaparyan
RV aukṣan ghṛtairastṛṇan barhirasmā ādiddhotāraṃ nyasādayanta
RV yamaichāma manasā so 'yamāgād yajñasya vidvānparuṣaścikitvān
RV sa no yakṣad devatātā yajīyān ni hiṣatsadantaraḥ pūrvo asmat
RV arādhi hotā niṣadā yajīyanabhi prayāṃsi sudhitāni hikhyat
RV yajāmahai yajñiyān hanta devānīḷāmahāīḍyānājyena
RV sādhvīmakardevavītiṃ no adya yajñasya jihvāmavidāmaguhyām
RV sa āyurāgāt surabhirvasāno bhadrāmakardevahūtiṃ no adya
RV tadadya vācaḥ prathamaṃ masīya yenāsurānabhi devāasāma
RV ūrjāda uta yajñiyasaḥ pañca janā mama hotraṃjuṣadhvam
RV pañca janā mama hotraṃ juṣantāṃ gojātā uta yeyajñiyāsaḥ
RV pṛthivī naḥ pārthivāt pātvaṃ
aso'ntarikṣaṃ divyāt pātvasmān
RV tantuṃ tanvan rajaso bhānumanvihi jyotiṣmataḥ pathorakṣa dhiyā kṛtān
RV anulbaṇaṃ vayata joguvāmapo manurbhava janayā daivyaṃ janam
RV akṣānaho nahyatanota somyā iṣkṛṇudhvaṃ raśanā otapiṃśata
RV aṣṭāvandhuraṃ vahatābhito rathaṃ yena devāsoanayannabhi priyam
RV aśmanvatī rīyate saṃ rabhadhvamut tiṣṭhata pra taratāsakhāyaḥ
RV atrā jahāma ye asannaśevāḥ śivān vayamuttaremābhi vājān
RV tvaṣṭā māyā vedapasāmapastamo bibhrat pātrādevapānāni śantamā
RV śiśīte nūnaṃ paraśuṃ svāyasaṃyena vṛścādetaśo brahmaṇas patiḥ
RV sato nūnaṃ kavayaḥ saṃ śiśīta vāśībhiryābhiramṛtāya takṣatha
RV vidvāṃsaḥ padā guhyāni kartana yenadevāso amṛtatvamānaśuḥ
RV garbhe yoṣāmadadhurvatsamāsanyapīcyena manasotajihvayā
RV sa viśvāhā sumanā yogyā abhi siṣāsanirvanatekāra ijjitim
RV tāṃ su te kīrtiṃ maghavan mahitvā yat tvā bhīte rodasīahvayetām
RV prāvo devānātiro dāsamojaḥ prajāyaitvasyai yadaśikṣa indra
RV yadacarastanvā vāvṛdhāno balānīndra prabruvāṇo janeṣu
RV māyet sā te yāni yuddhānyāhurnādya śatruṃ nanupurā vivitse
RV ka u nu te mahimanaḥ samasyāsmat pūrva ṛṣayo 'ntamāpuḥ
RV yan mātaraṃ ca pitaraṃ ca sākamajanayathāstanvaḥsvāyāḥ
RV catvāri te asuryāṇi nāmādābhyāni mahiṣasya santi
RV tvamaṅga tāni viśvāni vitse yebhiḥ karmāṇi maghavañcakartha
RV tvaṃ viśvā dadhiṣe kevalāni yānyāviryā ca guhāvasūni
RV kāmamin me maghavan mā vi tārīstvamājñātātvamindrāsi dātā
RV yo adadhājjyotiṣi jyotirantaryo asṛjan madhunā sammadhūni
RV adha priyaṃ śūṣamindrāya manma brahmakṛtobṛhadukthādavāci
RV dūre tan nāma guhyaṃ parācairyat tvā bhīte ahvayetāṃvayodhai
RV udastabhnāḥ pṛthivīṃ dyāmabhīke bhrātuḥputrān maghavan titviṣāṇaḥ
RV mahat tan nāma guhyaṃ puruspṛg yena bhūtaṃ janayo yenabhavyam
RV pratnaṃ jātaṃ jyotiryadasya priyaṃ priyāḥ samaviśanta pañca
RV ā rodasī apṛṇādota madhyaṃ pañca devān ṛtuśaḥ sapta sapta
RV catustriṃśatā purudhā vi caṣṭe sarūpeṇa jyotiṣāvivratena
RV yaduṣa auchaḥ prathamā vibhānāmajanayo yena puṣṭasyapuṣṭam
RV yat te jāmitvamavaraṃ parasyā mahan mahatyāasuratvamekam
RV vidhuṃ dadrāṇaṃ samane bahūnāṃ yuvānaṃ santaṃ palitojagāra
RV devasya paśya kāvyaṃ mahitvādyā mamāra sa hyaḥsamāna
RV śākmanā śāko aruṇaḥ suparṇa ā yo mahaḥ śūraḥsanādanīḷaḥ
RV yacciketa satyamit tan na moghaṃ vasuspārhamuta jetota dātā
RV aibhirdade vṛṣṇyā pauṃsyāni yebhiraukṣad vṛtrahatyāyavajrī
RV ye karmaṇaḥ kriyamāṇasya mahna ṛtekarmamudajāyanta devāḥ
RV yujā karmāṇi janayan viśvaujā aśastithā viśvamanāsturāṣāṭ
RV pītvī somasya diva ā vṛdhānaḥ śūro niryudhādhamad dasyūn
RV idaṃ ta ekaṃ para ū ta ekaṃ tṛtīyena jyotiṣā saṃviśasva
RV saṃveśane tanvaścāruredhi priyo devānāmparame janitre
RV tanūṣ ṭe vājin tanvaṃ nayantī vāmamasmabhyaṃ dhātuśarma tubhyam
RV ahruto maho dharuṇāya devān divīvajyotiḥ svamā mimīyāḥ
RV vājyasi vājinenā suvenīḥ suvita stomaṃ suvito divaṃgāḥ
RV suvito dharma prathamānu satyā suvito devān suvito'nu patma
RV mahimna eṣāṃ pitaraścaneśire devā deveṣvadadhurapikratum
RV samavivyacuruta yānyatviṣuraiṣāṃ tanūṣu niviviśuḥ punaḥ
RV sahobhirviśvaṃ pari cakramū rajaḥ pūrvā dhāmānyamitāmimānāḥ
RV tanūṣu viśvā bhuvanā ni yemire prāsārayantapurudha prajā anu
RV dvidhā sūnavo 'suraṃ svarvidamāsthāpayanta tṛtīyenakarmaṇā
RV svāṃ prajāṃ pitaraḥ pitryaṃ saha āvareṣvadadhustantumātatam
RV nāvā na kṣodaḥ pradiśaḥ pṛthivyāḥ svastibhiratidurgāṇi viśvā
RV svāṃ prajāṃ bṛhaduktho mahitvāvareṣvadadhādā pareṣu
RV mā pra gāma patho vayaṃ mā yajñādindra sominaḥ
RV mānta sthurno arātayaḥ
RV yo yajñasya prasādhanastanturdeveṣvātataḥ
RV tamāhutaṃ naśīmahi
RV mano nvā huvāmahe nārāśaṃsena somena
RV pitṝṇāṃ camanmabhiḥ
RV ā ta etu manaḥ punaḥ kratve dakṣāya jīvase
RV jyok casūryaṃ dṛśe
RV punarnaḥ pitaro mano dadātu daivyo janaḥ
RV jīvaṃ vrātaṃsacemahi
RV vayaṃ soma vrate tava manastanūṣu bibhrataḥ
RV prajāvantaḥ sacemahi
RV yat te yamaṃ vaivasvataṃ mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta āvartayāmasīha kṣayāya jīvase
RV yat te divaṃ yat pṛthivīṃ mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te bhūmiṃ caturbhṛṣṭiṃ mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta
RV yat te catasraḥ pradiśo mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te samudramarṇavaṃ mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te marīcīḥ pravato mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te apo yadoṣadhīrmano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te sūryaṃ yaduṣasaṃ mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te parvatān bṛhato mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te viśvamidaṃ jagan mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te parāḥ parāvato mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta 
RV yat te bhūtaṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca mano jagāma dūrakam
RV tat ta
RV pra tāryāyuḥ prataraṃ navīya sthātāreva kratumatārathasya
RV adha cyavāna ut tavītyarthaṃ parātaraṃ sOGām
RV sāman nu rāye nidhiman nvannaṃ karāmahe su purudhaśravāṃsi
RV tā no viśvāni jaritā mamattu parātaraṃ sunirṛtirjihītām
RV abhī ṣvaryaḥ pauṃsyairbhavema dyaurna bhūmiṃ girayonājran
RV tā no viśvāni jaritā ciketa parātaraṃ sunirṛtirjihītām
RV mo ṣu ṇaḥ soma mṛtyave parā dāḥ paśyema nu sūryamuccarantam
RV dyubhirhito jarimā sū no astu parātaraṃ sunirṛtirjihītām
RV asunīte mano asmāsu dhāraya jīvātave su pra tirā naāyuḥ
RV rārandhi naḥ sūryasya sandṛśi ghṛtena tvantanvaṃ vardhayasva
RV asunīte punarasmāsu cakṣuḥ punaḥ prāṇamiha no dhehibhogam
RV jyok paśyema sūryamuccarantamanumate mṛḷayā nahsvasti
RV punarno asuṃ pṛthivī dadātu punardyaurdevī punarantarikṣam
RV punarnaḥ somastanvaṃ dadātu punaḥ pūṣāpathyāṃ yā svastiḥ
RV śaṃ rodasī subandhave yahvī ṛtasya mātarā
RV bharatāmapa yad rapo dyauḥ pṛthivi kṣamā rapo mo ṣu te kiṃcanāmamat
RV ava dvake ava trikā divaścaranti bheṣajā
RV kṣamācariṣṇvekakaṃ bharatāmapa yad rapo dyauḥ pṛthivi kṣamārapo mo ṣu te kiṃ canāmamat
RV samindreraya gāmanaḍvāhaṃ ya āvahaduśīnarāṇyāanaḥ
RV bharatāmapa yad rapo dyauḥ pṛthivi kṣamā rapo moṣu te kiṃ canāmamat
RV ā janaṃ tveṣasandṛśaṃ māhīnānāmupastutam
RV aganmabibhrato namaḥ
RV asamātiṃ nitośanaṃ tveṣaṃ niyayinaṃ ratham
RV bhajerathasya satpatim
RV yo janān mahiṣānivātitasthau pavīravān
RV utāpavīravānyudhā
RV yasyekṣvākurupa vrate revān marāyyedhate
RV divīvapañca kṛṣṭayaḥ
RV indra kṣatrāsamātiṣu rathaproṣṭheṣu dhāraya
RV divīvasūryaṃ dṛśe
RV agastyasya nadbhyaḥ saptī yunakṣi rohitā
RV paṇīn nyakramīrabhi viśvān rājannarādhasaḥ
RV ayaṃ mātāyaṃ pitāyaṃ jīvāturāgamat
RV idaṃ tavaprasarpaṇaṃ subandhavehi nirihi
RV yathā yugaṃ varatrayā nahyanti dharuṇāya kam
RV evādādhāra te mano jīvātave na mṛtyave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye
RV yatheyaṃ pṛthivī mahī dādhāremān vanaspatīn
RV evādādhāra te mano jīvātave na mṛtyave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye
RV yamādahaṃ vaivasvatāt subandhormana ābharam
RV jīvātavena mṛtyave 'tho ariṣṭatātaye
RV nyag vāto 'va vāti nyak tapati sūryaḥ
RV nīcīnamaghnyāduhe nyag bhavatu te rapaḥ
RV ayaṃ me hasto bhagavānayaṃ me bhagavattaraḥ
RV ayaṃ meviśvabheṣajo 'yaṃ śivābhimarśanaḥ
RV idamitthā raudraṃ gūrtavacā brahma kratvā śacyāmantarājau
RV krāṇā yadasya pitarā maṃhaneṣṭhāḥ parṣatpakthe ahannā sapta hotṝn
RV sa id dānāya dabhyāya vanvañcyavānaḥ sūdairamimītavedim
RV tūrvayāṇo gūrtavacastamaḥ kṣodo na reta itaūtisiñcat
RV mano na yeṣu havaneṣu tigmaṃ vipaḥ śacyā vanuthodravantā
RV ā yaḥ śaryabhistuvinṛmṇoasyāśrīṇītādiśaṃ gabhastau
RV kṛṣṇā yad goṣvaruṇīṣu sīdad divo napātāśvināhuve vām
RV vītaṃ me yajñamā gataṃ me annaṃ vavanvāṃsāneṣamasmṛtadhrū
RV prathiṣṭa yasya vīrakarmamiṣṇadanuṣṭhitaṃ nu naryoapauhat
RV punastadā vṛhati yat kanāyā duhiturāanubhṛtamanarvā
RV madhyā yat kartvamabhavadabhīke kāmaṃ kṛṇvāṇepitari yuvatyām
RV manānag reto jahaturviyantā sānauniṣiktaṃ sukṛtasya yonau
RV pitā yat svāṃ duhitaramadhiṣkan kṣmayā retaḥsaṃjagmāno ni ṣiñcat
RV svādhyo 'janayan brahma devāvāstoṣ patiṃ vratapāṃ niratakṣan
RV sa īṃ vṛṣā na phenamasyadājau smadā paraidapadabhracetāḥ
RV sarat padā na dakṣiṇā parāvṛṃ na tā nume pṛśanyo jagṛbhre
RV makṣū na vahniḥ prajāyā upabdiragniṃ na nagna upasīdadūdhaḥ
RV sanitedhmaṃ sanitota vājaṃ sa dhartājajñe sahasā yavīyut
RV makṣū kanāyāḥ sakhyaṃ navagvā ṛtaṃ vadanta ṛtayuktimagman
RV dvibarhaso ya upa gopamāguradakṣiṇāso acyutādudukṣan
RV makṣū kanāyāḥ sakhyaṃ navīyo rādho na reta ṛtamitturaṇyan
RV śuci yat te rekṇa āyajanta sabardughāyāḥ payausriyāyāḥ
RV paśvā yat paścā viyutā budhanteti bravīti vaktarīrarāṇaḥ
RV vasorvasutvā kāravo 'nehā viśvaṃ viveṣṭidraviṇamupa kṣu
RV tadin nvasya pariṣadvāno agman purū sadanto nārṣadambibhitsan
RV vi śuṣṇasya saṃgrathitamanarvā vidatpuruprajātasya guhā yat
RV bhargo ha nāmota yasya devāḥ svarṇa ye triṣadhastheniṣeduḥ
RV agnirha nāmota jātavedāḥ śrudhī no hotarṛtasya hotādhruk
RV uta tyā me raudrāvarcimantā nāsatyāvindra gūrtayeyajadhyai
RV manuṣvad vṛktabarhiṣe rarāṇā mandūhitaprayasā vikṣu yajyū
RV ayaṃ stuto rājā vandi vedhā apaś va viprastaratisvasetuḥ
RV sa kakṣīvantaṃ rejayat so agniṃ nemiṃ nacakramarvato raghudru
RV sa dvibandhurvaitaraṇo yaṣṭā sabardhuṃ dhenumasvanduhadhyai
RV saṃ yan mitrāvaruṇā vṛñja ukthairjyeṣṭhebhiraryamaṇaṃ varūthaiḥ
RV tadbandhuḥ sūrirdivi te dhiyandhā nābhānediṣṭho rapatipra venan
RV sā no nābhiḥ paramāsya vā ghāhaṃ tatpaścā katithaścidāsa
RV iyaṃ me nābhiriha me sadhasthamime me devā ayamasmisarvaḥ
RV dvijā aha prathamajā ṛtasyedaṃ dhenuraduhajjāyamānā
RV adhāsu mandro aratirvibhāvāva syati dvivartanirvaneṣāṭ
RV ūrdhvā yacchreṇirna śiśurdan makṣū sthiraṃśevṛdhaṃ sūta mātā
RV adhā gāva upamātiṃ kanāyā anu śvāntasya kasya citpareyuḥ
RV śrudhi tvaṃ sudraviṇo nastvaṃ yāḷ āśvaghnasyavavṛdhe sūnṛtābhiḥ
RV adha tvamindra viddhyasmān maho rāye nṛpate vajrabāhuḥ
RV rakṣā ca no maghonah pāhi sūrīnanehasaste harivoabhiṣṭau
RV adha yad rājānā gaviṣṭau sarat saraṇyuḥ kāravejaraṇyuḥ
RV vipraḥ preṣṭhaḥ sa hyeṣāṃ babhūva parā cavakṣaduta parṣadenān
RV adhā nvasya jenyasya puṣṭau vṛthā rebhanta īmahe tadūnu
RV saraṇyurasya sūnuraśvo vipraścāsi śravasaścasātau
RV yuvoryadi sakhyāyāsme śardhāya stomaṃ jujuṣe namasvānviśvatra yasminnā giraḥ samīcīḥ pūrvīva gatūrdāśat sūnṛtāyai
RV sa gṛṇāno adbhirdevavāniti subandhurnamasā sūktaiḥ
RV vardhadukthairvacobhirā hi nūnaṃ vyadhvaiti payasausriyāyāḥ
RV ta ū ṣu ṇo maho yajatrā bhūta devāsa ūtaye sajoṣāḥ
RV ye vājānanayatā viyanto ye sthā nicetāro amūrāḥ
RV ye yajñena dakṣiṇayā samaktā indrasya sakhyamamṛtatvamānaśa
RV tebhyo bhadramaṅgiraso vo astu prati gṛbhṇītamānavaṃ sumedhasaḥ
RV ya udājan pitaro gomayaṃ vasv ṛtenābhindan parivatsarevalam
RV dīrghāyutvamaṅgiraso vo astu prati gṛbhṇītamānavaṃ sumedhasaḥ
RV ya ṛtena sūryamārohayan divyaprathayan pṛthivīṃ mātaraṃvi
RV suprajāstvamaṅgiraso vo astu prati gṛbhṇīta mānavaṃsumedhasaḥ
RV ayaṃ nābhā vadati valgu vo gṛhe devaputrā ṛṣayastacchṛṇotana
RV subrahmaṇyamaṅgiraso vo astu prati gṛbhṇītamānavaṃ sumedhasaḥ
RV virūpāsa id ṛṣayasta id gambhīravepasaḥ
RV te aṅgirasaḥsūnavaste agneḥ pari jajñire
RV ye agneḥ pari jajñire virūpāso divas pari
RV navagvo nudaśagvo aṅgirastamo sacā deveṣu maṃate
RV indreṇa yujā niḥ sṛjanta vāghato vrajaṃ gomantamaśvinam
RV sahasraṃ me dadato aṣṭakarṇyaḥ śravo deveṣvakrata
RV pra nūnaṃ jāyatāmayaṃ manustokmeva rohatu
RV yaḥ sahasraṃśatāśvaṃ sadyo dānāya maṃhate
RV na tamaśnoti kaścana diva iva sānvārabham
RV sāvarṇyasya dakṣiṇā vi sindhuriva paprathe
RV uta dāsā pariviṣe smaddiṣṭī goparīṇasā
RV yadusturvaśca māmahe
RV sahasradā grāmaṇīrmā riṣan manuḥ sūryeṇāsyayatamānaitu dakṣiṇā
RV sāvarṇerdevāḥ pra tirantvāyuryasminnaśrāntā asanāma vājam
RV parāvato ye didhiṣanta āpyaṃ manuprītāso janimāvivasvataḥ
RV yayāterye nahuṣyasya barhiṣi devā āsate teadhi bruvantu naḥ
RV viśvā hi vo namasyāni vandyā nāmāni devā uta yajñiyānivaḥ
RV ye stha jātā aditerabdhyas pari ye pṛthivyāstema iha śrutā havam
RV yebhyo mātā madhumat pinvate payaḥ pīyūṣaṃ dyauraditiradribarhāḥ
RV ukthaśuṣmān vṛṣabharān svapnasastānādityānanu madā svastaye
RV nṛcakṣaso animiṣanto arhaṇā bṛhad devāso amṛtatvamānaśuḥ
RV jyotīrathā ahimāyā anāgaso divo varṣmāṇaṃvasate svastaye
RV samrājo ye suvṛdho yajñamāyayuraparihvṛtā dadhire divikṣayam
RV tānā vivāsa namasā suvṛktibhirmaho ādityānaditiṃ svastaye
RV ko va stomaṃ rādhati yaṃ jujoṣatha viśve devāso manuṣoyati ṣṭhana
RV ko vo 'dhvaraṃ tuvijātā araṃ karad yo naḥparṣadatyaṃhaḥ svastaye
RV yebhyo hotrāṃ prathamāmāyeje manuḥ samiddhāgnirmanasāsapta hotṛbhiḥ
RV ta ādityā abhayaṃ śarma yachata sugā naḥkarta supathā svastaye
RV ya īśire bhuvanasya pracetaso viśvasya sthāturjagataścamantavaḥ
RV te naḥ kṛtādakṛtādenasas paryadyā devāsaḥpipṛtā svastaye
RV bhareṣvindraṃ suhavaṃ havāmahe 'ṃhomucaṃ sukṛtandaivyaṃ janam
RV agniṃ mitraṃ varuṇaṃ sātaye bhagandyāvāpṛthivī marutaḥ svastaye
RV sutrāmāṇaṃ pṛthivīṃ dyāmanehasaṃ suśarmāṇamaditiṃsupraṇītim
RV daivīṃ nāvaṃ svaritrāmanāgasamasravantīmā ruhemā svastaye
RV viśve yajatrā adhi vocatotaye trāyadhvaṃ no durevāyāabhihrutaḥ
RV satyayā vo devahūtyā huvema śṛṇvato devāavase svastaye
RV apāmīvāmapa viśvāmanāhutimapārātiṃ durvidatrāmaghāyataḥ
RV āre devā dveṣo asmad yuyotanoru ṇaḥ śarmayachatā svastaye
RV ariṣṭaḥ sa marto viśva edhate pra prajābhirjāyatedharmaṇas pari
RV yamādityāso nayathā sunītibhirativiśvāni duritā svastaye
RV yaṃ devāso 'vatha vājasātau yaṃ śūrasātā maruto hitedhane
RV prātaryāvāṇaṃ rathamindra sānasimariṣyantamāruhemā svastaye
RV svasti naḥ pathyāsu dhanvasu svastyapsu vṛjane svarvati
RV svasti naḥ putrakṛtheṣu yoniṣu svasti rāye maruto dadhātana
RV svastirid dhi prapathe śreṣṭhā rekṇasvatyabhi yāvāmameti
RV sā no amā so araṇe ni pātu svāveśā bhavatudevagopā
RV evā plateḥ sūnuravīvṛdhad vo viśva ādityā aditemanīṣī
RV īśānāso naro amartyenāstāvi jano divyogayena
RV kathā devānāṃ katamasya yāmani sumantu nāma śṛṇvatāmmanāmahe
RV ko mṛḷāti katamo no mayas karat katama ūtī abhyā vavartati
RV kratūyanti kratavo hṛtsu dhītayo venanti venāḥ patayantyā diśaḥ
RV na marḍitā vidyate anya ebhyo deveṣu me adhikāmā ayaṃsata
RV narā vā śaṃsaṃ pūṣaṇamagohyamagniṃ deveddhamabhyarcase girā
RV sūryāmāsā candramasā yamaṃ divi tritaṃvātamuṣasamaktumaśvinā
RV kathā kavistuvīravān kayā girā bṛhaspatirvāvṛdhatesuvṛktibhiḥ
RV aja ekapāt suhavebhirṛkvabhirahiḥ śṛṇotubudhnyo havīmani
RV dakṣasya vādite janmani vrate rājānā mitrāvaruṇāvivāsasi
RV atūrtapanthāḥ pururatho aryamā saptahotāviṣurūpeṣu janmasu
RV te no arvanto havanaśruto havaṃ viśve śṛṇvantu vājinomitadravaḥ
RV sahasrasā medhasātāviva tmanā maho yedhanaṃ samitheṣu jabhrire
RV pra vo vāyuṃ rathayujaṃ purandhiṃ stomaiḥ kṛṇudhvaṃsakhyāya pūṣaṇam
RV te hi devasya savituḥ savīmanikratuṃ sacante sacitaḥ sacetasaḥ
RV triḥ sapta sasrā nadyo mahīrapo vanaspatīn parvatānagnimūtaye
RV kṛśānumastṝn tiṣyaṃ sadhastha ā rudraṃrudreṣu rudriyaṃ havāmahe
RV sarasvatī sarayuḥ sindhurūrmibhirmaho mahīravasā yantuvakṣaṇīḥ
RV devīrāpo mātaraḥ sūdayitnvo ghṛtavat payomadhuman no arcata
RV uta mātā bṛhaddivā śṛṇotu nastvaṣṭā devebhirjanibhiḥpitā vacaḥ
RV ṛbhukṣā vājo rathaspatirbhago raṇvaḥśaṇsaḥ śaśamānasya pātu naḥ
RV raṇvaḥ sandṛṣṭau pitumāniva kṣayo bhadrā rudrāṇāmmarutāmupastutiḥ
RV gobhiḥ ṣyāma yaśaso janeṣvā sadādevāsa iḷayā sacemahi
RV yāṃ me dhiyaṃ maruta indra devā adadāta varuṇa mitra yūyam
RV tāṃ pīpayata payaseva dhenuṃ kuvid giro adhi rathevahātha
RV kuvidaṅga prati yathā cidasya naḥ sajātyasya marutobubodhatha
RV nābhā yatra prathamaṃ saṃnaśāmahe tatrajāmitvamaditirdadhātu naḥ
RV te hi dyāvāpṛthivī mātarā mahī devī devāñ janmanāyajñiye itaḥ
RV ubhe bibhṛta ubhayaṃ bharīmabhiḥ purūretāṃsi pitṛbhiśca siñcataḥ
RV vi ṣā hotrā viśvamaśnoti vāryaṃ bṛhaspatiraramatiḥpanīyasī
RV grāvā yatra madhuṣuducyate bṛhadavīvaśantamatibhirmanīṣiṇaḥ
RV evā kavistuvīravān ṛtajñā draviṇasyurdraviṇasaścakānaḥ
RV ukthebhiratra matibhiśca vipro 'pīpayad gayodivyāni janma
RV evā plateḥ sūnur
RV agnirindro varuṇo mitro aryamā vāyuḥ pūṣā sarasvatīsajoṣasaḥ
RV ādityā viṣṇurmarutaḥ svarbṛhat somo rudroaditirbrahmaṇas patiḥ
RV indrāgnī vṛtrahatyeṣu satpatī mitho hinvānā tanvāsamokasā
RV antarikṣaṃ mahyā paprurojasā somo ghṛtaśrīrmahimānamīrayan
RV teṣāṃ hi mahnā mahatāmanarvaṇāṃ stomāniyarmyṛtajñā ṛtāvṛdhām
RV ye apsavamarṇavaṃ citrarādhasasteno rāsantāṃ mahaye sumitryāḥ
RV svarṇaramantarikṣāṇi rocanā dyāvābhūmī pṛthivīṃskambhurojasā
RV pṛkṣā iva mahayantaḥ surātayo devāstavante manuṣāya sūrayaḥ
RV mitrāya śikṣa varuṇāya dāśuṣe yā samrājā manasā naprayuchataḥ
RV yayordhāma dharmaṇā rocate bṛhad yayorubherodasī nādhasī vṛtau
RV yā gaurvartaniṃ paryeti niṣkṛtaṃ payo duhānā vratanīravārataḥ
RV sā prabruvāṇā varuṇāya dāśuṣe devebhyodāśad dhaviṣā vivasvate
RV divakṣaso agnijihvā ṛtāvṛdha ṛtasya yoniṃ vimṛśanta āsate
RV dyāṃ skabhitvyapa ā cakrurojasā yajñaṃ janitvītanvī ni māmṛjuḥ
RV parikṣitā pitarā pūrvajāvarī ṛtasya yonā kṣayataḥsamokasā
RV dyāvāpṛthivī varuṇāya savrate ghṛtavat payomahiṣāya pinvataḥ
RV parjanyāvātā vṛṣabhā purīṣiṇendravāyū varuṇo mitroaryamā
RV devānādityānaditiṃ havāmahe ye pārthivāsodivyāso apsu ye
RV tvaṣṭāraṃ vāyum ṛbhavo ya ohate daivyā hotārā uṣasaṃsvastaye
RV bṛhaspatiṃ vṛtrakhādaṃ sumedhasamindriyaṃsomaṃ dhanasā u īmahe
RV brahma gāmaśvaṃ janayanta oṣadhīrvanaspatīn pṛthivīmparvatānapaḥ
