RV sūryaṃ divi rohayantaḥ sudānava āryāvratā visṛjanto adhi kṣami
RV bhujyumaṃhasaḥ pipṛtho niraśvinā śyāvaṃ putraṃvadhrimatyā ajinvatam
RV kamadyuvaṃ vimadāyohathuryuvaṃviṣṇāpvaṃ viśvakāyāva sṛjathaḥ
RV pāvīravī tanyaturekapādajo divo dhartā sindhurāpaḥsamudriyaḥ
RV viśve devāsaḥ śṛṇavan vacāṃsi me sarasvatīsaha dhībhiḥ purandhyā
RV viśve devāḥ saha dhībhiḥ purandhyā manoryajatrāamṛtā ṛtajñāḥ
RV rātiṣāco abhiṣācaḥ svarvidaḥ svargiro brahma sūktaṃ juṣerata
RV devān vasiṣṭho amṛtān vavande ye viśvā bhuvanābhipratasthuḥ
RV te no rāsantāmurugāyamadya yūyaṃ pātasvastibhiḥ sadā naḥ
RV devān huve bṛhacchravasaḥ svastaye jyotiṣkṛto adhvarasyapracetasaḥ
RV ye vāvṛdhuḥ prataraṃ viśvavedasaindrajyeṣṭhāso amṛtā ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
RV indraprasūtā varuṇapraśiṣṭā ye sūryasya jyotiṣo bhāgamānaśuḥ
RV marudgaṇe vṛjane manma dhīmahi māghone yajñaṃjanayanta sūrayaḥ
RV indro vasubhiḥ pari pātu no gayamādityairno aditḥ śarmayachtu
RV rudro rudrebhirdevo mṛḷayāti nastvaṣṭā nognābhiḥ suvitāya jinvatu
RV aditirdyāvāpṛthivī ṛtaṃ mahadindrāviṣṇū marutaḥsvarbṛhat
RV devānādityānavase havāmahe vasūn rudrāṃsavitāraṃ sudaṃsasam
RV sarasvān dhībhirvaruṇo dhṛtavratḥ pūṣā viṣṇurmahimāvāyuraśvinā
RV brahmakṛto amṛtā viśvavedasaḥ śarma noyaṃsan trivarūthamaṃhasaḥ
RV vṛṣā yajño vṛṣaṇaḥ santu yajñiyā vṛṣaṇo devāvṛṣaṇo haviṣkṛtaḥ
RV vṛṣaṇā dyāvāpṛthivī ṛtāvarīvṛṣā parjanyo vṛṣaṇo vṛṣastubhaḥ
RV agnīṣomā vṛṣaṇā vājasātaye purupraśastā vṛṣaṇā upabruve
RV yāvījire vṛṣaṇo devayajyayā tā naḥ śarmatrivarūthaṃ vi yaṃsataḥ
RV dhṛtavratāḥ kṣatriyā yajñaniṣkṛto bṛhaddivā adhvarāṇāmabhiśriyaḥ
RV agnihotāra ṛtasāpo adruho 'po asṛjannanuvṛtratūrye
RV dyāvāpṛthivī janayannabhi vratāpa oṣadhīrvanināniyajñiyā
RV antarikṣaṃ svarā paprurūtaye vaśaṃ devāsastanvī ni māmṛjuḥ
RV dhartāro diva ṛbhavaḥ suhastā vātāparjanyā mahiṣasyatanyatoḥ
RV āpa oṣadhīḥ pra tirantu no giro bhago rātirvājino yantu me havam
RV samudraḥ sindhū rajo antarikṣamaja ekapāt tanayitnurarṇavaḥ
RV ahirbudhnyaḥ śṛṇavad vacāṃsi me viśve devāsauta sūrayo mama
RV syāma vo manavo devavītaye prāñcaṃ no yajñaṃ pra ṇayatasādhuyā
RV ādityā rudrā vasavaḥ sudānava imā brahmaśasyamānāni jinvata
RV daivyā hotārā prathamā purohita ṛtasya panthāmanvemisādhuyā
RV kṣetrasya patiṃ prativeśamīmahe viśvān devānamṛtānaprayuchataḥ
RV vasiṣṭhāsaḥ pitṛvad vācamakrata devānīḷānā ṛṣivatsvastaye
RV prītā iva jñātayaḥ kāmametyāsme devāso 'vadhūnutā vasu
RV devān vasiṣṭho amṛtān vavande 
RV imāṃ dhiyaṃ saptaśīrṣṇīṃ pitā na ṛtaprajātāṃ bṛhatīmavindat
RV turīyaṃ svijjanayad viśvajanyo 'yāsya ukthamindrāya śaṃsan
RV ṛtaṃ śaṃsanta ṛju dīdhyānā divas putrāso asurasyavīrāḥ
RV vipraṃ padamaṅgiraso dadhānā yajñasya dhāmaprathamaṃ mananta
RV haṃsairiva sakhibhirvāvadadbhiraśmanmayāni nahanāvyasyan
RV bṛhaspatirabhikanikradad gā uta prāstauduccavidvānagāyat
RV avo dvābhyāṃ para ekayā gā guhā tiṣṭhantīranṛtasyasetau
RV bṛhaspatistamasi jyotirichannudusrā ākarvihi tisra āvaḥ
RV vibhidyā puraṃ śayāthemapācīṃ nistrīṇi sākamudadherakṛntat
RV bṛhaspatiruṣasaṃ sūryaṃ gāmarkaṃviveda stanayanniva dyauḥ
RV indro valaṃ rakṣitāraṃ dughānāṃ kareṇeva vi cakartāraveṇa
RV svedāñjibhirāśiramichamāno 'rodayat paṇimāgā amuṣṇāt
RV sa īṃ satyebhiḥ sakhibhiḥ śucadbhirgodhāyasaṃ vidhanasairadardaḥ
RV brahmaṇas patirvṛṣabhirvarāhairgharmasvedebhirdraviṇaṃ vyānaṭ
RV te satyena manasā gopatiṃ gā iyānāsa iṣaṇayantadhībhiḥ
RV bṛhaspatirmithoavadyapebhirudusriyā asṛjatasvayugbhiḥ
RV taṃ vardhayanto matibhiḥ śivābhiḥ siṃ
amiva nānadataṃsadhasthe
RV bṛhaspatiṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ śūrasātau bharebhare anumadema jiṣṇum
RV yadā vājamasanad viśvarūpamā dyāmarukṣaduttarāṇisadma
RV bṛhaspatiṃ vṛṣaṇaṃ vardhayanto nānā santobibhrato jyotirāsā
RV satyāmāśiṣaṃ kṛṇutā vayodhai kīriṃ cid dhyavathasvebhirevaiḥ
RV paścā mṛdho apa bhavantu viśvāstadrodasī śṛṇutaṃ viśvaminve
RV indro mahnā mahato arṇavasya vi mūrdhānamabhinadarbudasya
RV ahannahimariṇāt sapta sindhūn devairdyāvāpṛthivīprāvataṃ naḥ
RV udapruto na vayo rakṣamāṇā vāvadato abhriyasyeva ghoṣāḥ
RV giribhrajo normayo madanto bṛhaspatimabhyarkā anāvan
RV saṃ gobhirāṅgiraso nakṣamāṇo bhaga ivedaryamaṇaṃnināya
RV jane mitro na dampatī anakti bṛhaspatevājayāśūnrivājau
RV sādhvaryā atithinīriṣirā spārhāḥ suvarṇāanavadyarūpāḥ
RV bṛhaspatiḥ parvate bhyo vitūryā nirgāūpe yavamiva sthivibhyaḥ
RV āpruṣāyan madhuna ṛtasya yonimavakṣipannarka ulkāmivadyoḥ
RV bṛhaspatiruddharannaśmano gā bhūmyā udneva vitvacaṃ bibheda
RV apa jyotiṣā tamo antarikṣādudnaḥ śīpālamiva vātaājat
RV bṛhaspatiranumṛśyā valasyābhramiva vāta ā cakraā gāḥ
RV yadā valasya pīyato jasuṃ bhed bṛhaspatiragnitapobhirarkaiḥ
RV dadbhirna jihvā pariviṣṭamādadāvirnidhīnrakṛṇodusriyāṇām
RV bṛhaspatiramata hi tyadāsāṃ nāma svarīṇāṃ sadaneguhā yat
RV āṇḍeva bhittvā śakunasya garbhamudusriyāḥparvatasya tmanājat
RV aśnāpinaddhaṃ madhu paryapaśyan matsyaṃ na dīna udanikṣiyantam
RV niṣ ṭajjabhāra camasaṃ na vṛkṣādbṛhaspatirviraveṇā vikṛtya
RV soṣāmavindat sa svaḥ so agniṃ so arkeṇa vi babādhetamāṃsi
RV bṛhaspatirgovapuṣo valasya nirmajjānaṃ naparvaṇo jabhāra
RV himeva parṇā muṣitā vanāni bṛhaspatinākṛpayad valo gāḥ
RV anānukṛtyamapunaścakāra yāt sūryāmāsā mithauccarātaḥ
RV abhi śyāvaṃ na kṛśanebhiraśvaṃ nakṣatrebhiḥ pitarodyāmapiṃśan
RV rātryāṃ tamo adadhurjyotirahanbṛhaspatirbhinadadriṃ vidad gāḥ
RV idamakarma namo abhriyāya yaḥ pūrvīranvānonavīti
RV bṛhaspatiḥ sa hi gobhiḥ so aśvaiḥ sa vīrebhiḥ sanṛbhirno vayo dhāt
RV bhadrā agnervadhryaśvasya sandṛśo vāmī praṇītiḥsuraṇā upetayaḥ
RV yadīṃ sumitrā viśo agra indhateghṛtenāhuto jarate davidyutat
RV ghṛtamagnervadhryaśvasya vardhanaṃ ghṛtamannaṃ ghṛtaṃ vasya medanam
RV ghṛtenāhuta urviyā vi paprathe sūrya ivarocate sarpirāsutiḥ
RV yat te manuryadanīkaṃ sumitraḥ samīdhe agne tadidaṃnavīyaḥ
RV sa revacchoca sa giro juṣasva sa vājaṃ darṣisa iha śravo dhāḥ
RV yaṃ tvā pūrvamīḷito vadhryaśvaḥ samīdhe agne sa idaṃjuṣasva
RV sa na stipā uta bhavā tanūpā dātraṃ rakṣasvayadidaṃ te asme
RV bhavā dyumnī vādhryaśvota gopā mā tvā tārīdabhimātirjanānām
RV śūra iva dhṛṣṇuścyavanaḥ sumitraḥ pra nuvocaṃ vādhryaśvasya nāma
RV samajryā parvatyā vasūni dāsā vṛtrāṇyāryā jigetha
RV śūra iva dhṛṣṇuścyavano janānāṃ tvamagne pṛtanāyūnrabhi ṣyāḥ
RV dīrghatanturbṛhadukṣāyamagniḥ sahasrastarīḥ śatanīthaṛbhvā
RV dyumān dyumatsu nṛbhirmṛjyamānaḥ sumitreṣu dīdayodevayatsu
RV tve dhenuḥ sudughā jātavedo 'saścateva samanā sabardhuk
RV tvaṃ nṛbhirdakṣiṇāvadbhiragne sumitrebhiridhyasedevayadbhiḥ
RV devāścit te amṛtā jātavedo mahimānaṃ vādhryaśva pra vocan
RV yat sampṛchaṃ mānuṣīrviśa āyan tvaṃ nṛbhirajayastvāvṛdhebhiḥ
RV piteva putramabibharupasthe tvāmagne vadhryaśvaḥ saparyanjuṣāṇo asya samidhaṃ yaviṣṭhota pūrvānavanorvrādhataścit
RV śaśvadagnirvadhryaśvasya śātrūn nṛbhirjigāyasutasomavadbhiḥ
RV samanaṃ cidadahaścitrabhāno 'vavrādhantamabhinad vṛdhaścit
RV ayamagnirvadhryaśvasya vṛtrahā sanakāt preddhonamasopavākyaḥ
RV sa no ajāmīnruta vā vijāmīnabhitiṣṭha śardhato vādhryaśva
RV imāṃ me agne samidhaṃ juṣasveḷas pade prati haryāghṛtācīm
RV varṣman pṛthivyāḥ sudinatve ahnāmūrdhvobhava sukrato devayajyā
RV ā devānāmagrayāveha yātu narāśaṃso viśvarūpebhiraśvaiḥ
RV ṛtasya pathā namasā miyedho devebhyo devatamaḥsuṣūdat
RV śaśvattamamīḷate dūtyāya haviṣmanto manuṣyāso agnim
RV vahiṣṭhairaśvaiḥ suvṛtā rathenā devān vakṣi niṣadeha hotā
RV vi prathatāṃ devajuṣṭaṃ tiraścā dīrghaṃ drāghmāsurabhi bhūtvasme
RV aheḷatā manasā deva barhirindrajyeṣṭhānuśato yakṣi devān
RV divo vā sānu spṛśatā varīyaḥ pṛthivyā vā mātrayā viśrayadhvam
RV uśatīrdvāro mahinā mahadbhirdevaṃ rathaṃrathayurdhārayadhvam
RV devī divo duhitarā suśilpe uṣāsānaktā sadatāṃ niyonau
RV ā vāṃ devāsa uśatī uśanta urau sīdantu subhageupasthe
RV ūrdhvo grāvā bṛhadagniḥ samiddhaḥ priyā dhāmānyaditerupasthe
RV purohitāv ṛtvijā yajñe asmin viduṣṭarādraviṇamā yajethām
RV tisro devīrbarhiridaṃ varīya ā sīdata cakṛmā vaḥsyonam
RV manuṣvad yajñaṃ sudhitā havīṃṣīḷā devīghṛtapadī juṣanta
RV deva tvaṣṭaryad dha cārutvamānaḍ yadaṅgirasāmabhavaḥ sacābhūḥ
RV sa devānāṃ pātha upa pra vidvānuśan yakṣi draviṇodaḥ suratnaḥ
RV vanaspate raśanayā niyūyā devānāṃ pātha upa vakṣividvān
RV svadāti devaḥ kṛṇavad dhavīṃṣyavatāndyāvāpṛthivī havaṃ me
RV āgne vaha varuṇamiṣṭaye na indraṃ divo marutoantarikṣāt
RV sīdantu barhirviśva ā yajatrāḥ svāhādevā amṛtā mādayantām
RV bṛhaspate prathamaṃ vāco agraṃ yat prairata nāmadheyandadhānāḥ
RV yadeṣāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ yadaripramāsītpreṇā tadeṣāṃ nihitaṃ guhāviḥ
RV saktumivatitaunā punanto yatra dhīrā manasā vācamakrata
RV atrā sakhāyaḥ sakhyāni jānate bhadraiṣāṃlakṣmīrnihitādhi vāci
RV yajñena vācaḥ padavīyamāyan tāmanvavindannṛṣiṣupraviṣṭām
RV tāmābhṛtyā vyadadhuḥ purutrā tāṃ saptarebhā abhi saṃ navante
RV uta tvaḥ paśyan na dadarśa vācamuta tvaḥ śṛṇvan naśṛṇotyenām
RV uto tvasmai tanvaṃ vi sasre jāyeva patyauśatī suvāsāḥ
RV uta tvaṃ sakhye sthirapītamāhurnainaṃ hinvantyapivājineṣu
RV adhenvā carati māyayaiṣa vācaṃ śuśruvānaphalāmapuṣpām
RV yastityāja sacividaṃ sakhāyaṃ na tasya vācyapi bhāgoasti
RV yadīṃ śṛṇotyalakaṃ śṛṇoti nahi praveda sukṛtasyapanthām
RV akṣaṇvantaḥ karṇavantaḥ sakhāyo manojaveṣvasamābabhūvuḥ
RV ādaghnāsa upakakṣāsa u tve hradā iva snātvā utve dadṛśre
RV hṛdā taṣṭeṣu manaso javeṣu yad brāhmaṇāḥ saṃyajantesakhāyaḥ
RV atrāha tvaṃ vi jahurvedyābhirohabrahmāṇo vicarantyu tve
RV ime ye nārvāṃ na paraścaranti na brāhmaṇāso nasutekarāsaḥ
RV ta ete vācamabhipadya pāpayā sirīstantraṃ tanvate aprajajñayaḥ
RV sarve nandanti yaśasāgatena sabhāsāhena sakhyā sakhāyaḥ
RV kilbiṣaspṛt pituṣaṇirhyeṣāmaraṃ hito bhavativājināya
RV ṛcāṃ tvaḥ poṣamāste pupuṣvān gāyatraṃ tvo gāyatiśakvarīṣu
RV brahmā tvo vadati jātavidyāṃ yajñasyamātrāṃ vi mimīta u tvaḥ
RV devānāṃ nu vayaṃ jānā pra vocāma vipanyayā
RV uktheṣuśasyamāneṣu yaḥ paśyāduttare yuge
RV brahmaṇas patiretā saṃ karmāra ivādhamat
RV devānāmpūrvye yuge 'sataḥ sadajāyata
RV devānāṃ yuge prathame 'sataḥ sadajāyata
RV tadāśā anvajāyanta taduttānapadas pari
RV bhūrjajña uttānapado bhuva āśā ajāyanta
RV aditerdakṣoajāyata dakṣād vaditiḥ pari
RV aditirhyajaniṣṭa dakṣa yā duhitā tava
RV tāṃ devāanvajāyanta bhadrā amṛtabandhavaḥ
RV yad devā adaḥ salile susaṃrabdhā atiṣṭhata
RV atrā vonṛtyatāmiva tīvro reṇurapāyata
RV yad devā yatayo yathā bhuvanānyapinvata
RV atrā samudraā gūḷamā sūryamajabhartana
RV aṣṭau putrāso aditerye jātāstanvas pari
RV devānupaprait saptabhiḥ parā mārtāṇḍamāsyat
RV saptabhiḥ putrairaditirupa prait pūrvyaṃ yugam
RV prajāyai mṛtyave tvat punarmārtāṇḍamābharat
RV janiṣthā ugraḥ sahase turāya mandra ojiṣṭhobahulābhimānaḥ
RV avardhannindraṃ marutaścidatra mātāyad vīraṃ dadhanad dhaniṣṭhā
RV druho niṣattā pṛśanī cidevaiḥ purū śaṃsena vāvṛdhuṣṭa indram
RV abhīvṛteva tā mahāpadena dhvāntāt prapitvādudaranta garbhāḥ
RV ṛṣvā te pādā pra yajjigāsyavardhan vājā uta ye cidatra
RV tvamindra sālāvṛkān sahasramāsan dadhiṣe aśvināvavṛtyāḥ
RV samanā tūrṇirupa yāsi yajñamā nāsatyā sakhyāyavakṣi
RV vasāvyāmindra dhārayaḥ sahasrāśvinā śūra dadaturmaghāni
RV mandamāna ṛtādadhi prajāyai sakhibhirindra iṣirebhirartham
RV ābhirhi māyā upa dasyumāgān mihaḥ pratamrā avapat tamāṃsi
RV sanāmānā cid dhvasayo nyasmā avāhannindra uṣasoyathānaḥ ṛṣvairagachaḥ sakhibhirnikāmaiḥ sākampratiṣṭhā hṛdyā jaghantha
RV tvaṃ jaghantha namuciṃ makhasyuṃ dāsaṃ kṛṇvāna ṛṣayevimāyam
RV tvaṃ cakartha manave syonān patho devatrāñjasevayānān
RV tvametāni papriṣe vi nāmeśāna indra dadhiṣe gabhastau
RV anu tvā devāḥ śavasā madantyuparibudhnān vaninaścakartha
RV cakraṃ yadasyāpsvā niṣattamuto tadasmai madhviccachadyāt
RV pṛthivyāmatiṣitaṃ yadūdhaḥ payo goṣvadadhā oṣadhīṣu
RV aśvādiyāyeti yad vadantyojaso jātamuta manya enam
RV manyoriyāya harmyeṣu tasthau yataḥ prajajña indro asya veda
RV vayaḥ suparṇā upa sedurindraṃ priyamedhā ṛṣayonādhamānāḥ
RV apa dhvāntamūrṇuhi pūrdhi cakṣurmumugdhyasmān nidhayeva baddhān
RV vasūnāṃ vā carkṛṣa iyakṣan dhiyā vā yajñairvārodasyoḥ
RV arvanto vā ye rayimantaḥ sātau vanuṃ vā yesuśruṇaṃ suśruto dhuḥ
RV hava eṣāmasuro nakṣata dyāṃ śravasyatā manasā niṃsatakṣā
RV cakṣāṇā yatra suvitāya devā dyaurna vārebhiḥkṛṇavanta svaiḥ
RV iyameṣāmamṛtānāṃ gīḥ sarvatātā ye kṛpaṇanta ratnam
RV dhiyaṃ ca yajñaṃ ca sādhantaste no dhāntu vasavyamasāmi
RV ā tat ta indrāyavaḥ panantabhi ya ūrvaṃ gomantantitṛtsān
RV sakṛtsvaṃ ye puruputrāṃ mahīṃ sahasradhārāmbṛhatīṃ dudukṣan
RV śacīva indramavase kṛṇudhvamanānataṃ damayantaṃ pṛtanyūn
RV ṛbhukṣaṇaṃ maghavānaṃ suvṛktiṃ bhartā yo vajraṃ naryampurukṣuḥ
RV yad vāvāna purutamaṃ purāṣāḷ ā vṛtrahendro nāmānyaprāḥ
RV aceti prāsahas patistuviṣmān yadīmuśmasikartave karat tat
RV pra su va āpo mahimānamuttamaṃ kārurvocāti sadanevivasvataḥ
RV pra saptasapta tredhā hi cakramuḥ prasṛtvarīṇāmati sindhurojasā
RV pra te 'radad varuṇo yātave pathaḥ sindho yad vājānabhyadravastvam
RV bhūmyā adhi pravatā yāsi sānunā yadeṣāmagraṃ jagatāmirajyasi
RV divi svano yatate bhūmyoparyanantaṃ śuṣmamudiyartibhānunā
RV abhrādiva pra stanayanti vṛṣṭayaḥ sindhuryadeti vṛṣabho na roruvat
RV abhi tvā sindho śiśumin na mātaro vāśrā arṣantipayaseva dhenavaḥ
RV rājeva yudhvā nayasi tvamit sicau yadāsāmagraṃ pravatāminakṣasi
RV imaṃ me gaṅge yamune sarasvati śutudri stemaṃ sacatā paruṣṇyā
RV asiknyā marudvṛdhe vitastayārjīkīye śṛṇuhyāsuṣomayā
RV tṛṣṭāmayā prathamaṃ yātave sajūḥ sasartvā rasayāśvetyā tyā
RV tvaṃ sindho kubhayā gomatīṃ krumummehatnvā sarathaṃ yābhirīyase
RV ṛjītyenī ruśatī mahitvā pari jrayāṃsi bharate rajāṃsi
RV adabdhā sindhurapasāmapastamāśvā na citrāvapuṣīva darśatā
RV svaśvā sindhuḥ surathā suvāsā hiraṇyayī sukṛtāvājinīvatī
RV ūrṇāvatī yuvatiḥ sīlamāvatyutādhi vastesubhagā madhuvṛdham
RV sukhaṃ rathaṃ yuyuje sidhuraśvinaṃ tena vājaṃ saniṣadasminnājau
RV mahān hyasya mahimā panasyate 'dabdhasyasvayaśaso virapśinaḥ
RV ā va ṛñjasa ūrjāṃ vyuṣṭiṣvindraṃ maruto rodasīanaktana
RV ubhe yathā no ahanī sacābhuvā sadaḥsadovarivasyāta udbhidā
RV tadu śreṣṭhaṃ savanaṃ sunotanā
tyo na hastayato adriḥsotari
RV vidad dhyaryo abhibhūti pauṃsyaṃ maho rāye cittarute yadarvataḥ
RV tadid dhyasya savanaṃ viverapo yathā purā manavegātumaśret
RV goarṇasi tvāṣṭre aśvanirṇiji premadhvareṣvadhvarānaśiśrayuḥ
RV apa hata rakṣaso bhaṅgurāvata skabhāyata nirṛtiṃsedhatāmatim
RV ā no rayiṃ sarvavīraṃ sunotana devāvyambharata ślokamadrayaḥ
RV divaścidā vo 'mavattarebhyo vibhvanā cidāśvapastarebhyaḥ
RV vāyościda somarabhastarebhyo 'gneścidarcapitukṛttarebhyaḥ
RV bhurantu no yaśasaḥ sotvandhaso grāvāṇo vācā divitādivitmatā
RV naro yatra duhate kāmyaṃ madhvāghoṣayantoabhito mithasturaḥ
RV sunvanti somaṃ rathirāso adrayo nirasya rasaṃ gaviṣoduhanti te
RV duhantyūdharupasecanāya kaṃ naro havya nāmarjayanta āsabhiḥ
RV ete naraḥ svapaso abhūtana ya indrāya sunutha somamadrayaḥ
RV vāmaṃvāmaṃ vo divyāya dhāmne vasuvasu vaḥ pārthivayasunvate
RV abhrapruṣo na vācā pruṣā vasu haviṣmanto na yajñāvijānuṣaḥ
RV sumārutaṃ na brahmāṇamarhase gaṇamastoṣyeṣāṃ na śobhase
RV śriye maryāso añjīnrakṛṇvata sumarutaṃ na pūrviratikṣapaḥ
RV divas putrāsa etā na yetira ādityāsaste akrana vāvṛdhuḥ
RV pra ye divaḥ pṛthivya na barhaṇā tmanā riricre abhrānna sūryaḥ
RV pājasvanto na vīrāḥ panasyavo riśādaso namaryā abhidyavaḥ
RV yuṣmākaṃ budhne apāṃ na yāmani vithuryati na mahīśratharyati
RV viśvapsuryajño arvāgayaṃ su vaḥprayasvanto na satrāca ā gata
RV yūyaṃ dhūrṣu prayujo na raśmibhirjyotiṣmanto na bhāsāvyuṣṭiṣu
RV śyenāso na svayaśaso riśādasaḥ pravāsona prasitāsaḥ paripruṣaḥ
RV pra yad vahadhve marutaḥ parākād yūyaṃ mahaḥsaṃvaraṇasya vasvaḥ
RV vidānāso vasavo rādhyasyārācciddveṣaḥ sanutaryuyota
RV ya udṛci yajñe adhvareṣṭhā marudbhyo na mānuṣo dadāśat
RV revat sa vayo dadhate suvīraṃ sa devānāmapi gopītheastu
RV te hi yajñeṣu yajñiyāsa ūmā ādityena nāmnāśambhaviṣṭhāḥ
RV te no 'vantu rathatūrmanīṣāṃ mahaścayāmannadhvare cakānāḥ
RV viprāso na manmabhiḥ svādhyo devāvyo na yajñaiḥsvapnasaḥ
RV rājāno na citrāḥ susandṛśaḥ kṣitīnāṃ namaryā arepasaḥ
RV agnirna ye bhājasā rukmavakṣaso vātāso na svayujaḥsadyaūtayaḥ
RV prajñātāro na jyeṣṭhāḥ sunītayaḥsuśarmāṇo na somā ṛtaṃ yate
RV vātāso na ye dhunayo jigatnavo 'gnīnāṃ na jihvāvirokiṇaḥ
RV varmaṇvanto na yodhāḥ śimīvantaḥ pitṝṇāṃna śaṃsāḥ surātayaḥ
RV rathānāṃ na ye 'rāḥ sanābhayo jigīvāṃso na śūrāabhidyavaḥ
RV vareyavo na maryā ghṛtapruṣo 'bhisvartāroarkaṃ na suṣṭubhaḥ
RV aśvāso na ye jyeṣṭhāsa āśavo didhiṣavo na rathyaḥsudānavaḥ
RV āpo na nimnairudabhirjigatnavo viśvarūpāaṅgiraso na sāmabhiḥ
RV grāvāṇo na sūrayaḥ sindhumātara ādardirāso adrayo naviśvahā
RV śiśūlā na krīḷayaḥ sumātaro mahāgrāmo nayāmannuta tviṣā
RV uṣasāṃ na ketavo 'dhvaraśriyaḥ śubhaṃyavo nāñjibhirvyaśvitan
RV sindhavo na yayiyo bhrājadṛṣṭayaḥ parāvato nayojanāni mamire
RV subhāgān no devāḥ kṛṇutā suratnānasmān stotṝn marutovāvṛdhānāḥ
RV adhi stotrasya sakhyasya gāta sanād dhi voratnadheyāni santi
RV apaśyamasya mahato mahitvamamartyasya martyāsu vikṣu
RV nānā hanū vibhṛte saṃ bharete asinvatī bapsatī bhūryattaḥ
RV guhā śiro nihitam ṛdhagakṣī asinvannatti jihvayāvanāni
RV atrāṇyasmai paḍbhiḥ saṃ bharantyuttānahastānamasādhi vikṣu
RV pra mātuḥ prataraṃ guhyamichan kumāro na vīrudhaḥsarpadurvīḥ
RV sasaṃ na pakvamavidacchucantaṃririhvāṃsaṃ ripa upasthe antaḥ
RV tad vām ṛtaṃ rodasī pra bravīmi jāyamāno mātarā garbhoatti
RV nāhaṃ devasya martyaściketāgniraṅga vicetāḥ sapracetāḥ
RV yo asmā annaṃ tṛṣvādadhātyājyairghṛtairjuhotipuṣyati
RV tasmai sahasramakṣabhirvi cakṣe 'gne viśvataḥpratyaṃṃ asi tvam
RV kiṃ deveṣu tyaja enaścakarthāgne pṛchāmi nu tvāmavidvān
RV akrīḷan krīḷan harirattave 'dan vi parvaśaścakarta gāmivāsiḥ
RV viṣūco aśvān yuyuje vanejā ṛjītibhī raśanābhirgṛbhītān
RV cakṣade mitro vasubhiḥ sujātaḥ samānṛdheparvabhirvāvṛdhānaḥ
RV agniḥ saptiṃ vājambharaṃ dadātyagnirvīraṃ śrutyaṃkarmaniṣṭhām
RV agnī rodasī vi carat samañjannagnirnārīṃ vīrakukṣiṃ purandhim
RV agnerapnasaḥ samidastu bhadrāgnirmahī rodasī ā viveśa
RV agnirekaṃ codayat samatsvagnirvṛtrāṇi dayate purūṇi
RV agnirha tyaṃ jarataḥ karṇamāvāgniradbhyo niradahajjarūtham
RV agniratriṃ gharma uruṣyadantaragnirnṛmedhampra jayāsṛjat sam
RV agnirdād draviṇaṃ vīrapeśā agnirṛṣiṃ yaḥ sahasrāsanoti
RV agnirdivi havyamā tatānāgnerdhāmānivibhṛtā purutrā
RV agnimukthairṛṣayo vi hvayante 'gniṃ naro yāmanibādhitāsaḥ
RV agniṃ vayo antarikṣe patanto 'gniḥ sahasrāpari yāti gonām
RV agniṃ viśa īḷate mānuṣīryā agniṃ manuṣo nahuṣo vijātāḥ
RV agnirgāndharvīṃ pathyām ṛtasyāgnergavyūtirghṛta ā niṣattā
RV agnaye brahma ṛbhavastatakṣuragniṃ mahāmavocāmā suvṛktim
RV agne prāva jaritāraṃ yaviṣṭhāgne mahi draviṇamāyajasva
RV ya imā viśvā bhuvanāni juhvad ṛṣirhotā nyasīdatpitā naḥ
RV sa āśiṣā draviṇamichamānaḥ prathamachadavarānā viveśa
RV kiṃ svidāsīdadhiṣṭhanamārambhaṇaṃ katamat svitkathāsīt
RV yato bhūmiṃ janayan viśvakarma vi dyāmaurṇon mahinā viśvacakṣāḥ
RV viśvataścakṣuruta viśvatomukho viśvatobāhurutaviśvataspāt
RV saṃ bāhubhyāṃ dhamati saṃ patatrairdyāvābhūmī janayan deva ekaḥ
RV kiṃ svid vanaṃ ka u sa vṛkṣa āsa yato dyāvāpṛthivīniṣṭatakṣuḥ
RV manīṣiṇo manasā pṛchatedu tad yadadhyatiṣṭhad bhuvanāni dhārayan
RV yā te dhāmāni paramāṇi yāvamā yā madhyamāviśvakarmannutemā
RV śikṣā sakhibhyo haviṣi svadhāvaḥsvayaṃ yajasva tanvaṃ vṛdhānaḥ
RV viśvakarman haviṣā vāvṛdhānaḥ svayaṃ yajasva pṛthivīmuta dyām
RV muhyantvanye abhito janāsa ihāsmākaṃ maghavāsūrirastu
RV vācas patiṃ viśvakarmāṇamūtaye manojuvaṃ vāje adyāhuvema
RV sa no viśvāni havanāni joṣad viśvaśambhūravasesādhukarmā
RV cakṣuṣaḥ pitā manasā hi dhīro ghṛtamene ajanannannamāne
RV yadedantā adadṛhanta pūrva ādiddyāvāpṛthivī aprathetām
RV viśvakarmā vimanā ād vihāyā dhātā vidhātā paramotasandṛk
RV teṣāmiṣṭāni samiṣā madanti yatrāsaptaṛṣīn para ekamāhuḥ
RV yo naḥ pitā janitā yo vidhātā dhāmāni veda bhuvanāniviśvā
RV yo devānāṃ nāmadhā eka eva taṃ sampraśnambhuvanā yantyanyā
RV ta āyajanta draviṇaṃ samasmā ṛṣayaḥ pūrve jaritāro nabhūnā
RV asūrte sūrte rajasi niṣatte ye bhūtānisamakṛṇvannimāni
RV paro divā para enā pṛthivyā paro devebhirasurairyadasti
RV kaṃ svid garbhaṃ prathamaṃ dadhra āpo yatra devāḥsamapaśyanta viśve
RV tamid garbhaṃ prathamaṃ dadhra āpo yatra devāḥsamagachanta viśve
RV ajasya nābhāvadhyekamarpitaṃyasmin viśvāni bhuvanāni tasthuḥ
RV na taṃ vidātha ya imā jajānāyad yuṣmākamantarambabhūva
RV nīhāreṇa prāvṛtā jalpyā cāsutṛpa ukthaśāsaścaranti
RV yaste manyo 'vidhad vajra sāyaka saha ojaḥ puṣyati viśvamānuṣak
RV sāhyāma dāsamāryaṃ tvayā yujā sahaskṛtenasahasā sahasvatā
RV manyurindro manyurevāsa devo manyurhotā varuṇojātavedāḥ
RV manyuṃ viśa īḷate mānuṣīryāḥ pāhi nomanyo tapasā sajoṣāḥ
RV abhīhi manyo tavasastavīyān tapasā yujā vi jahi śatrūn
RV amitrahā vṛtrahā dasyuhā ca viśvā vasūnyā bharātvaṃ naḥ
RV tvaṃ hi manyo abhibhūtyojāḥ svayambhūrbhāmoabhimātiṣāhaḥ
RV viśvacarṣaṇiḥ sahuriḥ sahāvānasmāsvojaḥ pṛtanāsu dhehi
RV abhāgaḥ sannapa pareto asmi tava kratvā taviṣasyapracetaḥ
RV taṃ tvā manyo akraturjihīḷāhaṃ svā tanūrbaladeyāya mehi
RV ayaṃ te asmyupa mehyarvāṃ pratīcīnaḥ sahure viśvadhāyaḥ
RV manyo vajrinnabhi māmā vavṛtsva hanāva dasyūnrutabodhyāpeḥ
RV abhi prehi dakṣiṇato bhavā me 'dhā vṛtrāṇi jaṅghanāvabhūri
RV juhomi te dharuṇaṃ madhvo agramubhā upāṃśuprathamā pibāva
RV tvayā manyo sarathamārujanto harṣamāṇāso dhṛṣitāmarutvaḥ
RV tigmeṣava āyudhā saṃśiśānā abhi pra yantunaro agnirūpāḥ
RV agniriva manyo tviṣitaḥ sahasva senānīrnaḥ sahure hūtaedhi
RV hatvāya śatrūn vi bhajasva veda ojo mimāno vi mṛdhonudasva
RV sahasva manyo abhimātimasme rujan mṛṇan pramṛṇan prehiśatrūn
RV ugraṃ te pājo nanvā rurudhre vaśī vaśaṃnayasa ekaja tvam
RV eko bahūnāmasi manyavīḷito viśaṃviśaṃ yudhaye saṃśiśādhi
RV akṛttaruk tvayā yujā vayaṃ dyumantaṃ ghoṣaṃvijayāya kṛṇmahe
RV vijeṣakṛdindra ivānavabravo 'smākaṃ manyo adhipā bhaveha
RV priyaṃ te nāma sahure gṛṇīmasi vidmā tamutsaṃ yataābabhūtha
RV ābhūtyā sahajā vajra sāyaka saho bibharṣyabhibhūtauttaram
RV kratvā no manyo saha
medyedhi mahādhanasya puruhūtasaṃsṛji
RV saṃsṛṣṭaṃ dhanamubhayaṃ samākṛtamasmabhyaṃ dattāṃvaruṇaśca manyuḥ
RV bhiyaṃ dadhānā hṛdayeṣu śatravaḥparājitāso apa ni layantām
RV satyenottabhitā bhūmiḥ sūryeṇottabhitā dyauḥ
RV ṛtenādityāstiṣṭhanti divi somo adhi śritaḥ
RV somenādityā balinaḥ somena pṛthivī mahī
RV athonakṣatrāṇāmeṣāmupasthe soma āhitaḥ
RV somaṃ manyate papivan yat sampiṃṣantyoṣadhim
RV somaṃ yambrahmāṇo vidurna tasyāśnāti kaścana
RV āchadvidhānairgupito bārhataiḥ soma rakṣitaḥ
RV gravṇāmicchṛṇvan tiṣṭhasi na te aśnāti pārthivaḥ
RV yat tvā deva prapibanti tata ā pyāyase punaḥ
RV vāyuḥsomasya rakṣitā samānāṃ māsa ākṛtiḥ
RV raibhyāsīdanudeyī nārāśaṃsi nyocanī
RV sūryāyābhadramid vāso gāthayaiti pariṣkṛtam
RV cittirā upabarhaṇaṃ cakṣurā abhyañjanam
RV dyaurbhūmiḥkośa āsīd yadayāt sūryā patim
RV stomā āsan pratidhayaḥ kuriraṃ chanda opaśaḥ
RV sūryāyāaśvinā varāgnirāsīt purogavaḥ
RV somo vadhūyurabhavadaśvināstāmubhā varā
RV sūryāṃyat patye śaṃsantīṃ manasā savitādadāt
RV mano asyā ana āsīd dyaurāsīduta chadiḥ
RV śukrāvanaḍvāhavāstāṃ yadayāt sūryā bṛham
RV ṛksāmābhyāmabhihitau gāvau te sāmanāvitaḥ
RV śrotraṃ tecakre āstāṃ divi panthāścarācāraḥ
RV śucī te cakre yātyā vyāno akṣa āhataḥ
RV anomanasmayaṃ sūryārohat prayati patim
RV sūryāyā vahatuḥ prāgāt savitā yamavāsṛjat
RV aghāsuhanyante gāvo 'rjunyoḥ paryuhyate
RV yadaśvinā pṛchamānāvayātaṃ tricakreṇa vahatuṃsūryāyāḥ
RV viśve devā anu tad vāmajānan putraḥpitarāvavṛṇīta pūṣā
RV yadayātaṃ śubhas patī vareyaṃ sūryāmupa
RV kvaikaṃcakraṃ vāmāsīt kva deṣṭrāya tasthathuḥ
RV dve te cakre sūrye brahmāṇa ṛtutha viduḥ
RV athaikaṃcakraṃ yad guhā tadaddhātaya id viduḥ
RV sūryāyai devebhyo mitrāya varuṇāya ca
RV ye bhūtasyapracetasa idaṃ tebhyo 'karaṃ namaḥ
RV pūrvāparaṃ carato māyayaitau śiśū kriḷantau pari yatoadhvaram
RV viśvānyanyo bhuvanābhicaṣṭa ṛtunranyovidadhajjāyate punaḥ
RV navonavo bhavati jāyamāno 'hnāṃ keturuṣasāmetyagram
RV bhāgaṃ devebhyo vi dadhātyāyan pra candramāstiratedīrghamayuḥ
RV sukiṃśukaṃ śalmaliṃ viśvarūpaṃ hiraṇyavarṇaṃ suvṛtaṃsucakram
RV ā roha sūrye amṛtasya lokaṃ syonaṃ patye vahatuṃkṛṇuṣva
RV udīrṣvātaḥ pativatī hyeṣā viśvāvasuṃ namasāgīrbhirīḷe
RV anyāmicha pitṛṣadaṃ vyaktāṃ sa te bhāgojanuṣā tasya viddhi
RV udīrṣvāto viśvāvaso namaseḷā mahe tvā
RV anyāmichaprapharvyaṃ saṃ jāyāṃ patyā sṛja
RV anṛkṣarā ṛjavaḥ santu panthā yebhiḥ sakhāyo yanti novareyam
RV samaryamā saṃ bhago no ninīyāt saṃ jaspatyaṃsuyamamastu devāḥ
RV pra tvā muñcāmi varuṇasya pāśād yena tvābadhnāt savitāsuśevaḥ
RV ṛtasya yonau sukṛtasya loke 'riṣṭāṃ tvā sahapatyā dadhāmi
RV preto muñcāmi nāmutaḥ subaddhāmamutas karam
RV yatheyamindra mīḍhvaḥ suputrā subhagāsati
RV pūṣā tveto nayatu hastagṛhyāśvinā tvā pra vahatāṃrathena
RV gṛhān gacha gṛhapatnī yathāso vaśinī tvaṃvidathamā vadāsi
RV iha priyaṃ prajayā te sam ṛdhyatāmasmin gṛhe gārhapatyāyajāgṛhi
RV enā patyā tanvaṃ saṃ sṛjasvādhā jivrī vidathamā vadāthaḥ
RV nīlalohitaṃ bhavati kṛtyāsaktirvyajyate
RV edhante asyājñātayaḥ patirbandheṣu badhyate
RV parā dehi śāmulyaṃ brahmabhyo vi bhajā vasu
RV kṛtyaiṣāpadvatī bhūtvyā jāyā viśate patim
RV aśrīrā tanūrbhavati ruśatī pāpayāmuyā
RV patiryadvadhvo vāsasā svamaṅgamabhidhitsate
RV ye vadhvaścandraṃ vahatuṃ yakṣmā yanti janādanu
RV punastān yajñiyā devā nayantu yata āgatāḥ
RV mā vidan paripanthino ya āsīdanti dampatī
RV sugebhirdurgamatītāmapa drāntvarātayaḥ
RV sumaṅgalīriyaṃ vadhūrimāṃ sameta paśyata
RV saubhāgyamasyai dattvāyāthāstaṃ vi paretana
RV tṛṣṭametat kaṭukametadapāṣṭhavad viṣavan naitadattave
RV sūryāṃ yo brahmā vidyāt sa id vādhūyamarhati
RV āśasanaṃ viśasanamatho adhivikartanam
RV sūryāyaḥ paśyarūpāṇi tāni brahmā tu śundhati
RV gṛbhṇāmi te saubhagatvāya hastaṃ mayā patyā jaradaṣṭiryathāsaḥ
RV bhago aryamā savitā purandhirmahyaṃ tvādurgārhapatyāya devāḥ
RV tāṃ pūṣañchivatamāmerayasva yasyāṃ bījaṃ manuṣyāvapanti
RV yā na ūrū uśatī viśrayāte yasyāmuśantaḥpraharāma śepam
RV tubhyamagre paryavahan sūryāṃ vahatunā saha
RV punaḥpatibhyo jāyāṃ dā agne prajayā saha
RV punaḥ patnīmagniradādāyuṣā saha varcasā
RV dīrghāyurasyā yaḥ patirjīvāti śaradaḥ śatam
RV somaḥ prathamo vivide gandharvo vivida uttaraḥ
RV tṛtīyoagniṣ ṭe patisturīyaste manuṣyajāḥ
RV somo dadad gandharvāya gandharvo dadadagnaye
RV rayiṃ caputrāṃścādādagnirmahyamatho imām
RV ihaiva staṃ mā vi yauṣṭaṃ viśvamāyurvyaśnutam
RV kṝḷantau putrairnaptṛbhirmodamānau sve gṛhe
RV ā naḥ prajāṃ hanayatu prajāpatirājarasāya samanaktvaryamā
RV adurmaṅgalīḥ patilokamā viśa śaṃ no bhavadvipade śaṃ catuṣpade
RV aghoracakṣurapatighnyedhi śivā paśubhyaḥ sumanāḥsuvarcāḥ
RV vīrasūrdevakāmā syonā śaṃ no bhava dvipadeśaṃ catuṣpade
RV imāṃ tvamindra mīḍhvaḥ suputrāṃ subhagāṃ kṛṇu
RV daśāsyāṃ putrānā dhehi patimekādaśaṃ kṛdhi
RV samrājñī śvaśure bhava samrājñī śvaśrvāṃ bhava
RV nanāndari samrājñī bhava samrājñī adhi devṛṣu
RV samañjantu viśve devāḥ samāpo hṛdayāni nau
RV sammātariśvā saṃ dhātā samu deṣṭrī dadhātu nau
RV vi hi sotorasṛkṣata nendraṃ devamamaṃsata
RV yatrāmadadvṛṣākapiraryaḥ puṣṭeṣu matsakhā viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV parā hīndra dhāvasi vṛṣākaperati vyathiḥ
RV no aha pravindasyanyatra somapītaye viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV kimayaṃ tvāṃ vṛṣākapiścakāra harito mṛgaḥ
RV yasmāirasyasīdu nvaryo vā puṣṭimad vasu viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV yamimaṃ tvaṃ vṛṣākapiṃ priyamindrābhirakṣasi
RV śvā nvasya jambhisadapi karṇe varahayurviśvasmadindra uttaraḥ
RV priyā taṣṭāni me kapirvyaktā vyadūduṣat
RV śiro nvasya rāviṣaṃ na sugaṃ duṣkṛte bhuvaṃ viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV na mat strī subhasattarā na suyāśutarā bhuvat
RV na matpraticyavīyasī na sakthyudyamīyasī viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV uve amba sulābhike yathevāṅga bhaviṣyati
RV bhasan me ambasakthi me śiro me vīva hṛṣyati viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV kiṃ subāho svaṅgure pṛthuṣṭo pṛthujāghane
RV kiṃ śūrapatninastvamabhyamīṣi vṛṣākapiṃ viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV avīrāmiva māmayaṃ śarārurabhi manyate
RV utāhamasmivīriṇīndrapatnī marutsakhā viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV saṃhotraṃ sma purā nārī samanaṃ vāva gachati
RV vedhāṛtasya vīriṇīndrapatnī mahīyate viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV indrāṇīmāsu nāriṣu subhagāmahamaśravam
RV nahyasyāaparaṃ cana jarasā marate patirviśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV nāhamindrāṇi rāraṇa sakhyurvṛṣākaperṛte
RV yasyedamapyaṃ haviḥ priyaṃ deveṣu gachati viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV vṛṣākapāyi revati sūputra ādu susnuṣe
RV ghasat ta indraukṣaṇaḥ priyaṃ kācitkaraṃ havirviśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV ukṣṇo hi me pañcadaśa sākaṃ pacanti viṃśatim
RV utāhamadmi pīva idubhā kukṣī pṛṇanti me viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV vṛṣabho na tigmaśṛṅgo 'ntaryūtheṣu roruvat
RV manthastaindra śaṃ hṛde yaṃ te sunoti bhāvayurviśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV na seśe yasya rambate 'ntarā sakthyā kapṛt
RV sedīśeyasya romaśaṃ niṣeduṣo vijṛmbhate viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV na seśe yasya romaśaṃ niṣeduṣo vijṛmbhate
RV sedīśeyasya rambate 'ntarā sakthyā kapṛd viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV ayamindra vṛṣākapiḥ parasvantaṃ hataṃ vidat
RV asiṃsūnāṃ navaṃ carumādedhasyāna ācitaṃ viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV ayamemi vicākaśad vicinvan dāsamāryam
RV pibāmipākasutvano 'bhi dhīramacākaśaṃ viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV dhanva ca yat kṛntatraṃ ca kati svit tā vi yojanā
RV nedīyāso vṛṣākape 'stamehi gṛhānupa viśvasmādindrauttarah
RV punarehi vṛṣākape suvitā kalpayāvahai
RV ya eṣasvapnanaṃśano 'stameṣi patha punarviśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV yadudañco vṛṣākape gṛhamindrājagantana
RV kva sya pulvaghomṛgaḥ kamagañ janayopano viśvasmādindra uttaraḥ
RV parśurha nāma mānavi sākaṃ sasūva viṃśa tim
RV bhadrambhala tyasyā abhūd yasyā udaramamayad viśvasmādindrauttaraḥ
RV rakṣohaṇaṃ vājinamā jigharmi mitraṃ prathiṣṭhamupayāmi śarma
RV śiśāno agniḥ kratubhiḥ samiddhaḥ sa nodivā sa riṣaḥ pātu naktam
RV ayodaṃṣṭro arciṣā yātudhānānupa spṛśa jātavedaḥsamiddhaḥ
RV ā jihvayā muradevān rabhasva kravyādo vṛktvyapi dhatsvāsan
RV ubhobhayāvinnupa dhehi daṃṣṭrā hiṃsraḥ śiśāno 'varamparaṃ ca
RV utāntarikṣe pari yāhi rājañ jambhaiḥ sandhehyabhi yātudhānān
RV yajñairiṣūḥ saṃnamamāno agne vācā śalyānaśanibhirdihānaḥ
RV tābhirvidhya hṛdaye yātudhānān pratīco bāhūnprati bhaṃdhyeṣām
RV agne tvacaṃ yātudhānasya bhindhi hiṃsrāśanirharasāhantvenam
RV pra parvāṇi jātavedaḥ śṛṇīhi kravyātkraviṣṇurvi cinotu vṛkṇam
RV yatredānīṃ paśyasi jātavedastiṣṭhantamagna uta vācarantam
RV yad vāntarikṣe pathibhiḥ patantaṃ tamastāvidhya śarvā śiśānaḥ
RV utālabdhaṃ spṛṇuhi jātaveda ālebhānād ṛṣṭibhiryātudhānāt
RV agne pūrvo ni jahi śośucāna āmādaḥkṣviṅkāstamadantvenīḥ
RV iha pra brūhi yatamaḥ so agne yo yātudhāno ya idaṃkṛṇoti
RV tamā rabhasva samidhā yaviṣṭha nṛcakṣasaścakṣuṣe randhayainam
RV tīkṣṇenāgne cakṣuṣā rakṣa yajñaṃ prāñcaṃ vasubhyaḥpra ṇaya pracetaḥ
RV hiṃsraṃ rakṣāṃsyabhi śośucānammā tvā dabhan yātudhānā nṛcakṣaḥ
RV nṛcakṣā rakṣaḥ pari paśya vikṣu tasya trīṇi pratiśṛṇīhyagrā
RV tasyāgne pṛṣṭīrharasā śṛṇīhi tredhāmūlaṃ yātudhānasya vṛśca
RV triryātudhānaḥ prasitiṃ ta etv ṛtaṃ yo agne anṛtena hanti
RV tamarciṣā sphūrjayañ jātavedaḥ samakṣamenaṃ gṛṇateni vṛṃdhi
RV tadagne cakṣuḥ prati dhehi rebhe śaphārujaṃ yenapaśyasi yātudhānam
RV atharvavajjyotiṣā daivyena satyandhūrvantamacitaṃ nyoṣa
RV yadagne adya mithunā śapāto yad vācastṛṣṭaṃ janayantarebhāḥ
RV manyormanasaḥ śaravyā jāyate yā tayā vidhyahṛdaye yātudhānān
RV parā śṛṇīhi tapasā yātudhānān parāgne rakṣo harasāśṛṇīhi
RV parārciṣā mūradevāñchṛṇīhi parāsutṛpo abhiśośucānaḥ
RV parādya devā vṛjinaṃ śṛṇantu pratyagenaṃ śapathā yantutṛṣṭāḥ
RV vācāstenaṃ śarava ṛchantu marman viśvasyaituprasitiṃ yātudhānaḥ
RV yaḥ pauruṣeyeṇa kraviṣā samaṅkte yo aśveyena paśunāyātudhānaḥ
RV yo aghnyāyā bharati kṣīramagne teṣāṃśīrṣāṇi harasāpi vṛśca
RV saṃvatsarīṇaṃ paya usriyāyāstasya māśīd yātudhānonṛcakṣaḥ
RV pīyūṣamagne yatamastitṛpsāt taṃ pratyañcamarciṣā vidhya marman
RV viṣaṃ gavāṃ yātudhānāḥ pibantvā vṛścyantāmaditayedurevāḥ
RV parainān devaḥ savitā dadātu parā bhāgamoṣadhīnāṃ jayantām
RV sanādagne mṛṇasi yātudhānān na tvā rakṣāṃsi pṛtanāsujigyuḥ
RV anu daha sahamūrān kravyādo mā te hetyā mukṣatadaivyāyāḥ
RV tvaṃ no agne adharādudaktāt tvaṃ paścāduta rakṣāpurastāt
RV prati te te ajarāsastapiṣṭhā aghaśaṃsaṃśośucato dahantu
RV paścāt purastādadharādudaktāt kaviḥ kāvyena pari pāhirājan
RV sakhe sakhāyamajaro jarimṇe 'gne martānamartyastvaṃ naḥ
RV pari tvāgne puraṃ vayaṃ vipraṃ sahasya dhīmahi
RV dhṛṣadvarṇaṃ divedive hantāraṃ bhaṅgurāvatām
RV viṣeṇa bhaṅgurāvataḥ prati ṣma rakṣaso daha
RV agnetigmena śociṣā tapuragrābhirṛṣṭibhiḥ
RV pratyagne mithuna daha yātudhānā kimīdinā
RV saṃ tvāśiśāmi jābṛhyadabdhaṃ vipra manmabhiḥ
RV pratyagne harasā haraḥ śṛṇīhi viśvataḥ prati
RV yātudhānasya rakṣaso balaṃ vi ruja vīryam
RV haviṣ pāntamajaraṃ svarvidi divispṛśyāhutaṃ juṣṭamagnau
RV tasya bharmaṇe bhuvanāya devā dharmaṇe kaṃsvadhayā paprathanta
RV gīrṇaṃ bhuvanaṃ tamasapagūḷamāviḥ svarabhavajjāteagnau
RV tasya devāḥ pṛthivi dyaurutāpo 'raṇayannoṣadhīḥ sakhye asya
RV devebhirnviṣito yajñiyebhiragniṃ stoṣāṇyajarambṛhantam
RV yo bhānunā pṛthiviṃ dyāmutemāmātatānarodasī antarikṣam
RV yo hotāsīt prathamo devajuṣṭo yaṃ samañjannājyenāvṛṇānaḥ
RV sa patatrītvaraṃ stha jagad yacchvātramagnirakṛnojjātavedaḥ
RV yajjatavedo bhuvanasya mūrdhannatiṣṭho agne saha rocanena
RV taṃ tvahema matibhirgīrbhirukthaiḥ sa yajñiyo abhavorodasiprāḥ
RV mūrdhā bhuvo bhavati naktamagnistataḥ suryo jāyateprātarudyan
RV mayāmu tu yajñiyānāmetamapo yattūrṇiścarati prajānan
RV dṛśenyo yo mahinā samiddho 'rocata diviyonirvibhāvā
RV tasminnagnau sūktavākena devā havirviśva ajuhavustanūpāḥ
RV sūktavakaṃ prathamamādidagnimādid dhavirajanayantadevāḥ
RV sa eṣāṃ yajño abhavat tanūpastaṃ dyaurvedataṃ prithivi tamāpaḥ
RV yaṃ devāso ajanayantāgniṃ yasminnājuhavurbhuvanāniviśvā
RV so arciṣā pṛthivīṃ dyāmutemām ṛjūyamānoatapan mahitvā
RV stomena hi divi devāso agnimajījanañchaktibhīrodasiprām
RV tamū akṛṇvan tredhā bhuve kaṃ sa oṣadhīḥpacati viśvarūpāḥ
RV yadedenamadadhuryajñiyāso divi devāḥ sūryamāditeyam
RV yadā cariṣṇū mithunāvabhūtāmādit prāpaśyanbhuvanāni viśvā
RV viśvasmā agniṃ bhuvanāya devā vaiśvānaraṃ ketumahnāmakṛṇvan
RV ā yastatānoṣaso vibhātīrapo ūrṇoti tamoarciṣā yan
RV vaiśvānaraṃ kavayo yajñiyāso 'gniṃ devā ajanayannajuryam
RV nakṣatraṃ pratnamaminaccariṣṇu yakṣasyādhyakṣantaviṣaṃ bṛhantam
RV vaiśvānaraṃ viśvahā dīdivāṃsaṃ mantrairagniṃ kavimachā vadāmaḥ
RV yo mahimnā paribabhūvorvī utāvastādutadevaḥ parastāt
RV dve srutī aśṛṇavaṃ pitṝṇāmahaṃ devānāmutamartyānām
RV tābhyāmidaṃ viśvamejat sameti yadantarāpitaraṃ mātaraṃ ca
RV dve samīcī bibhṛtaścarantaṃ śīrṣato jātaṃ manasāvimṛṣṭam
RV sa pratyaṃ viśvā bhuvanāni tasthāvaprayuchantaraṇirbhrājamānaḥ
RV yatrā vadete avaraḥ paraśca yajñanyoḥ kataro nau vi veda
RV ā śekurit sadhamādaṃ sakhāyo nakṣanta yajñaṃ kaidaṃ vi vocat
RV katyagnayaḥ kati sūryāsaḥ katyuṣāsaḥ katyu svidāpaḥ
RV nopaspijaṃ vaḥ pitaro vadāmi pṛchāmi vaḥ kavayovidmane kam
RV yāvanmātramuṣaso na pratīkaṃ suparṇyo vasatemātariśvaḥ
RV tāvad dadhātyupa yajñamāyan brāhmaṇohoturavaro niṣīdan
RV indraṃ stavā nṛtamaṃ yasya mahnā vibabādhe rocanā vi jmoantān
RV ā yaḥ paprau carṣaṇīdhṛd varobhiḥ prasindhubhyo riricāno mahitvā
RV sa sūryaḥ paryurū varāṃsyendro vavṛtyād rathyevacakrā
RV atiṣṭhantamapasyaṃ na sargaṃ kṛṣṇā tamāṃsitviṣyā jaghāna
RV samānamasmā anapāvṛdarca kṣmayā divo asamaṃ brahmanavyam
RV vi yaḥ pṛṣṭheva janimānyarya indraścikāya nasakhāyamīṣe
RV indrāya giro aniśitasargā apaḥ prerayaṃ sagarasya budhnāt
RV yo akṣeṇeva cakriyā śacībhirviṣvak tastambhapṛthivīmuta dyām
RV āpāntamanyustṛpalaprabharmā dhuniḥ śimīvāñcharumānṛjīṣī
RV somo viśvānyatasā vanāni nārvāgindrampratimānāni debhuḥ
RV na yasya dyāvāpṛthivī na dhanva nāntarikṣaṃ nādrayaḥsomo akṣāḥ
RV yadasya manyuradhinīyamānaḥ sṛṇāti vīḷurujati sthirāṇi
RV jaghāna vṛtraṃ svadhitirvaneva ruroja puro aradan nasindhūn
RV bibheda giriṃ navamin na kumbhamā gā indroakṛṇuta svayugbhiḥ
RV tvaṃ ha tyad ṛṇayā indra dhīro 'sirna parva vṛjināśṛṇāsi
RV pra ye mitrasya varuṇasya dhāma yujaṃ na janāminanti mitram
RV pra ye mitraṃ prāryamaṇaṃ durevāḥ pra saṃgiraḥ pravaruṇaṃ minanti
RV nyamitreṣu vadhamindra tumraṃ vṛṣanvṛṣāṇamaruṣaṃ śiśīhi
RV indro diva indra īśe pṛthivyā indro apāmindra itparvatānām
RV indro vṛdhāmindra in medhirāṇāmindraḥkṣeme yoge havya indraḥ
RV prāktubhya indraḥ pra vṛdho ahabhyaḥ prāntarikṣāt prasamudrasya dhāseḥ
RV pra vātasya prathasaḥ pra jmo antātpra sindhubhyo ririce pra kṣitibhyaḥ
RV pra śośucatyā uṣaso na keturasinvā te vartatāmindrahetiḥ
RV aśmeva vidhya diva ā sṛjānastapiṣṭhena heṣasādroghamitrān
RV anvaha māsā anvid vanānyanvoṣadhīranu parvatāsaḥ
RV anvindraṃ rodasī vāvaśāne anvāpo ajihatajāyamānam
RV karhi svit sā ta indra cetyāsadaghasya yad bhinado rakṣaeṣat
RV mitrakruvo yacchasane na gāvaḥ pṛthivyā āpṛgamuyā śayante
RV śatrūyanto abhi ye nastatasre mahi vrādhanta ogaṇāsaindra
RV andhenāmitrāstamasā sacantāṃ sujyotiṣo aktavastānabhi ṣyuḥ
RV purūṇi hi tvā savanā janānāṃ brahmāṇi mandan gṛṇatāmṛṣīṇām
RV imāmāghoṣannavasā sahūtiṃ tiro viśvānarcato yāhyarvāṃ
RV evā te vayamindra bhuñjatīnāṃ vidyāma sumatīnāṃnavānām
RV vidyāma vastoravasā gṛṇanto viśvāmitrā utata indra nūnam
RV śunaṃ huvema maghavānaṃ 
RV sahasraśīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt
RV sabhūmiṃ viśvato vṛtvātyatiṣṭhad daśāṅgulam
RV puruṣa evedaṃ sarvaṃ yad bhūtaṃ yacca bhavyam
RV utāmṛtatvasyeśāno yadannenātirohati
RV etāvānasya mahimāto jyāyāṃśca pūruṣaḥ
RV pādo 'syaviśvā bhūtāni tripādasyāmṛtaṃ divi
RV tripādūrdhva udait puruṣaḥ pādo 'syehābhavat punaḥ
RV tato viṣvaṃ vyakrāmat sāśanānaśane abhi
RV tasmād virāḷ ajāyata virājo adhi pūruṣaḥ
RV sa jātoatyaricyata paścād bhūmimatho puraḥ
RV yat puruṣeṇa haviṣā devā yajñamatanvata
RV vasantoasyāsīdājyaṃ grīṣma idhmaḥ śarad dhaviḥ
RV taṃ yajñaṃ barhiṣi praukṣan puruṣaṃ jātamagrataḥ
RV tena devā ayajanta sādhyā ṛṣayaśca ye
RV tasmād yajñāt sarvahutaḥ sambhṛtaṃ pṛṣadājyam
RV paśūntāṃścakre vāyavyānāraṇyān grāmyāśca ye
RV tasmād yajñāt sarvahuta ṛcaḥ sāmāni jajñire
RV chandāṃsijajñire tasmād yajustasmādajāyata
RV tasmādaśvā ajāyanta ye ke cobhayādataḥ
RV gāvo hajajñire tasmāt tasmājjātā ajāvayaḥ
RV yat puruṣaṃ vyadadhuḥ katidhā vyakalpayan
RV mukhaṃ kimasya kau bāhū kā ūrū pādā ucyete
RV brāhmaṇo 'sya mukhamāsīd bāhū rājanyaḥ kṛtaḥ
RV ūrūtadasya yad vaiśyaḥ padbhyāṃ śūdro ajāyata
RV candramā manaso jātaścakṣoḥ sūryo ajāyata
RV mukhādindraścāgniśca prāṇād vāyurajāyata
RV nābhyā āsīdantarikṣaṃ śīrṣṇo dyauḥ samavartata
RV padbhyāṃ bhūmirdiśaḥ śrotrāt tathā lokānakalpayan
RV saptāsyāsan paridhayastriḥ sapta samidhaḥ kṛtāḥ
RV devāyad yajñaṃ tanvānā abadhnan puruṣaṃ paśum
RV yajñena yajñamayajanta devāstāni dharmāṇi prathamānyāsan
RV te ha nākaṃ mahimānaḥ sacanta yatra pūrve sādhyāḥsanti devāḥ
RV saṃ jāgṛvadbhirjaramāṇa idhyate dame damūnā iṣayanniḷas pade
RV viśvasya hotā haviṣo vareṇyo vibhurvibhāvāsuṣakhā sakhīyate
RV sa darśataśrīratithirgṛhegṛhe vanevane śiśriyetakvavīriva
RV janaṃjanaṃ janyo nāti manyate viśa ākṣeti viśyo viśaṃ viśam
RV sudakṣo dakṣaiḥ kratunāsi sukraturagne kaviḥ kāvyenāsiviśvavit
RV vasurvasūnāṃ kṣayasi tvameka id dyāvā cayāni pṛthivī ca puṣyataḥ
RV prajānannagne tava yonim ṛtviyamiḷāyās pade ghṛtavantamāsadaḥ
RV ā te cikitra uṣasāmivetayo 'repasaḥ sūryasyevaraśmayaḥ
RV tava śriyo varṣyasyeva vidyutaścitrāścikitra uṣasāṃna ketavaḥ
RV yadoṣadhīrabhisṛṣṭo vanāni ca parisvayaṃ cinuṣe annamāsye
RV tamoṣadhīrdadhire garbham ṛtviyaṃ tamāpo agniṃjanayanta mātaraḥ
RV tamit samānaṃ vaninaśca vīrudho'ntarvatīśca suvate ca viśvahā
RV vātopadhūta iṣito vaśānanu tṛṣu yadannā veviṣadvitiṣṭhase
RV ā te yatante rathyo yathā pṛthak chardhāṃsyagne ajarāṇi dhakṣataḥ
RV medhākāraṃ vidathasya prasādhanamagniṃ hotāramparibhūtamaṃ matim
RV tamidarbhe haviṣyā samānamittamin mahe vṛṇate nānyaṃ tvat
RV tvāmidatra vṛṇate tvāyavo hotāramagne vidatheṣuvedhasaḥ
RV yad devayanto dadhati prayāṇsi te haviṣmantomanavo vṛktabarhiṣaḥ
RV tavāgne hotraṃ tava potram ṛtviyaṃ tava neṣṭraṃ tvamagnid ṛtāyataḥ
RV tava praśāstraṃ tvamadhvarīyasi brahmācāsi gṛhapatiśca no dame
RV yastubhyamagne amṛtāya martyaḥ samidhā dāśaduta vāhaviṣkṛti
RV tasya hotā bhavasi yāsi dūtyamupa brūṣeyajasyadhvarīyasi
RV imā asmai matayo vāco asmadān ṛco giraḥ suṣṭutayaḥsamagmata
RV vasūyavo vasave jātavedase vṛddhāsu cid vardhanoyāsu cākanat
RV imāṃ pratnāya suṣṭutiṃ navīyasīṃ voceyamasmā uśateśṛṇotu naḥ
RV bhūyā antarā hṛdyasya nispṛśe jāyevapatya uśatī suvāsāḥ
RV yasminnaśvāsa ṛṣabhāsa ukṣaṇo vaśā meṣāavasṛṣṭāsa āhutāḥ
RV kīlālape somapṛṣṭhāya vedhasehṛdā matiṃ janaye cārumagnaye
RV ahāvyagne havirāsye te srucīva ghṛtaṃ camvīva somaḥ
RV vājasaniṃ rayimasme suvīraṃ praśastaṃ dhehi yaśasambṛhantam
RV yajñasya vo rathyaṃ viśpatiṃ viśāṃ hotāramaktoratithiṃ vibhāvasum
RV śocañchuṣkāsu hariṇīṣu jarbhuradvṛṣā keturyajato dyāmaśāyata
RV imamañjaspāmubhaye akṛṇvata dharmāṇamagniṃ vidathasyasādhanam
RV aktuṃ na yahvamuṣasaḥ purohitaṃ tanūnapātamaruṣasya niṃsate
RV baḷ asya nīthā vi paṇeśca manmahe vayā asya prahutāāsurattave
RV yadā ghorāso amṛtatvamāśatādijjanasyadaivyasya carkiran
RV ṛtasya hi prasitirdyaururu vyaco namo mahyaramatiḥpanīyasī
RV indro mitro varuṇaḥ saṃ cikitrire 'tho bhagaḥsavitā pūtadakṣasaḥ
RV pra rudreṇa yayinā yanti sindhavastiro mahīmaramatindadhanvire
RV yebhiḥ parijmā pariyannuru jrayo vi roruvajjaṭhare viśvamukṣate
RV krāṇā rudrā maruto viśvakṛṣṭayo divaḥ śyenāsoasurasya nīḷayaḥ
RV tebhiścaṣṭe varuṇo mitro aryamendrodevebhirarvaśebhirarvaśaḥ
RV indre bhujaṃ śaśamānāsa āśata sūro dṛśīke vṛṣaṇaśca pauṃsye
RV pra ye nvasyārhaṇā tatakṣire yujaṃ vajraṃnṛṣadaneṣu kāravaḥ
RV sūraścidā harito asya rīramadindrādā kaścid bhayatetavīyasaḥ
RV bhīmasya vṛṣṇo jaṭharādabhiśvaso divedivesahuri stannabādhitaḥ
RV stomaṃ vo adya rudrāya śikvase kṣayadvīrāya namasādidiṣṭana
RV yebhiḥ śivaḥ svavānevayāvabhirdivaḥsiṣakti svayaśā nikāmabhiḥ
RV te hi prajāyā abharanta vi śravo bṛhaspatirvṛṣabhaḥsomajāmayaḥ
RV yajñairatharvā prathamo vi dhārayad devādakṣairbhṛgavaḥ saṃ cikitrire
RV te hi dyāvāpṛthivī bhūriretasā narāśaṃsaścaturaṅgoyamo 'ditiḥ
RV devastvaṣṭā draviṇodā ṛbhukṣaṇaḥ prarodasī maruto viṣṇurarhire
RV uta sya na uśijāmurviyā kavirahiḥ śṛṇotu budhnyohavīmani
RV sūryāmāsā vicarantā divikṣitā dhiyāśamīnahuṣī asya bodhatam
RV pra naḥ pūṣā carathaṃ viśvadevyo 'pāṃ napādavatuvāyuriṣṭaye
RV ātmānaṃ vasyo abhi vātamarcata tadaśvinā suhavā yāmani śrutam
RV viśāmāsāmabhayānāmadhikṣitaṃ gīrbhiru svayaśasaṃgṛṇīmasi
RV gnābhirviśvābhiraditimanarvaṇamaktoryuvānaṃ nṛmaṇā adhā patim
RV rebhadatra januṣā pūrvo aṅgirā grāvāṇa ūrdhvā abhicakṣuradhvaram
RV yebhirvihāyā abhavad vicakṣaṇaḥpāthaḥ sumekaṃ svadhitirvananvati
RV mahi dyāvāpṛthivī bhūtamurvī nārī yahvī na rodasīsadaṃ naḥ
RV tebhirnaḥ pātaṃ sahyasa ebhirnaḥ pātaṃśūṣaṇi
RV yajñeyajñe sa martyo devān saparyati
RV yaḥ sumnairdīrghaśruttama āvivāsatyenān
RV viśveṣāmirajyavo devānāṃ vārmahaḥ
RV viśve hiviśvamahaso viśve yajñeṣu yajñiyāḥ
RV te ghā rājāno amṛtasya mandrā aryamā mitro varuṇaḥparijmā
RV kad rudro nṛṇāṃ stuto marutaḥ pūṣaṇo bhagaḥ
RV uta no naktamapāṃ vṛṣaṇvasū sūryāmāsā sadanāyasadhanyā
RV sacā yat sādyeṣāmahirbudhneṣu budhnyaḥ
RV uta no devāvaśvinā śubhas patī dhāmabhirmitrāvaruṇāuruṣyatām
RV mahaḥ sa rāya eṣate 'ti dhanveva duritā
RV uta no rudrā cin mṛḷatāmaśvinā viśve devāso rathaspatirbhagaḥ
RV ṛbhurvāja ṛbhukṣaṇaḥ parijmā viśvavedasaḥ
RV ṛbhurṛbhukṣā ṛbhurvidhato mada ā te harī jūjuvānasyavājinā
RV duṣṭaraṃ yasya sāma cid ṛdhag yajño namānuṣaḥ
RV kṛdhī no ahrayo deva savitaḥ sa ca stuṣe maghonām
RV saho naindro vahnibhirnyeṣāṃ carṣaṇīnāṃ cakraṃ raśmiṃ nayoyuve
RV aiṣu dyāvāpṛthivī dhātaṃ mahadasme vīreṣu viśvacarṣaṇiśravaḥ
RV pṛkṣaṃ vājasya sātaye pṛkṣaṃ rāyotaturvaṇe
RV etaṃ śaṃsamindrāsmayuṣ ṭvaṃ kūcit santaṃ sahasāvannabhiṣṭaye sadā pāhyabhiṣṭaye
RV medatāṃ vedatā vaso
RV etaṃ me stomaṃ tanā na sūrye dyutadyāmānaṃ vāvṛdhantanṛṇām
RV saṃvananaṃ nāśvyaṃ taṣṭevānapacyutam
RV vāvarta yeṣāṃ rāyā yuktaiṣāṃ hiraṇyayī
RV nemadhitāna pauṃsyā vṛtheva viṣṭāntā
RV pra tad duḥśīme pṛthavāne vene pra rāme vocamasuremaghavatsu
RV ye yuktvāya pañca śatāsmayu pathā viśrāvyeṣām
RV adhīn nvatra saptatiṃ ca sapta ca
RV sadyo didiṣṭa tānvaḥsadyo didiṣṭa pārthyaḥ sadyo didiṣṭa māyavaḥ
RV praite vadantu pra vayaṃ vadāma grāvabhyo vācaṃ vadatāvadadbhyaḥ
RV yadadrayaḥ parvatāḥ sākamāśavaḥ ślokaṃghoṣaṃ bharathendrāya sominaḥ
RV ete vadanti śatavat sahasravadabhi krandanti haritebhirāsabhiḥ
RV viṣṭvī grāvāṇaḥ sukṛtaḥ sukṛtyayā hotuścit pūrve haviradyamāśata
RV ete vadantyavidannanā madhu nyūṅkhayante adhi pakvaāmiṣi
RV vṛkṣasya śākhāmaruṇasya bapsataste sūbharvāvṛṣabhāḥ premarāviṣuḥ
RV bṛhad vadanti madireṇa mandinendraṃ krośanto 'vidannanāmadhu
RV saṃrabhyā dhīrāḥ svasṛbhiranartiṣurāghoṣayantaḥ pṛthivīmupabdibhiḥ
RV suparṇā vācamakratopa dyavyākhare kṛṣṇā iṣirāanartiṣuḥ
RV nyaṃ ni yantyuparasya niṣkṛtaṃ purū retodadhire sūryaśvitaḥ
RV ugrā iva pravahantaḥ samāyamuḥ sākaṃ yuktā vṛṣaṇobibhrato dhuraḥ
RV yacchvasanto jagrasānā arāviṣuḥśṛṇva eṣāṃ prothatho arvatāmiva
RV daśāvanibhyo daśakakṣyebhyo daśayoktrebhyo daśayojanebhyaḥ
RV daśābhīśubhyo arcatājarebhyo daśa dhuro daśa yuktāvahadbhyaḥ
RV te adrayo daśayantrāsa āśavasteṣāmādhānaṃ paryetiharyatam
RV ta ū sutasya somyasyāndhaso 'ṃśoḥ pīyūṣamprathamasya bhejire
RV te somādo harī indrasya niṃsate 'ṃśuṃ duhanto adhyāsategavi
RV tebhirdugdhaṃ papivān somyaṃ madhvindro vardhateprathate vṛṣāyate
RV vṛṣā vo aṃśurna kilā riṣāthanelāvantaḥ sadamitsthanāśitāḥ
RV raivatyeva mahasā cārava sthana yasyagrāvāṇo ajuṣadhvamadhvaram
RV tṛdilā atṛdilāso adrayo 'śramaṇā aśṛthitā amṛtyavaḥ
RV anāturā ajarā sthāmaviṣṇavaḥ supīvaso atṛṣitāatṛṣṇajaḥ
RV dhruvā eva vaḥ pitaro yugeyuge kṣemakāmāsaḥ sadaso nayuñjate
RV ajuryāso hariṣāco haridrava ā dyāṃ raveṇapṛthivīmaśuśravuḥ
RV tadid vadantyadrayo vimocane yāmannañjaspā iva ghedupabdibhiḥ
RV vapanto bījamiva dhānyākṛtaḥ pṛñcantisomaṃ na minanti bapsataḥ
RV sute adhvare adhi vācamakratā krīḷayo na mātarantudantaḥ
RV vi ṣū muñcā suṣuvuṣo manīṣāṃ vi vartantāmadrayaścāyamānāḥ
RV haye jāye manasā tiṣṭha ghore vacāṃsi miśrākṛṇavāvahai nu
RV na nau mantrā anuditāsa ete mayas karanparatare canāhan
RV kimetā vācā kṛṇavā tavāhaṃ prākramiṣamuṣasāmagriyeva
RV purūravaḥ punarastaṃ parehi durāpanā vātaivāhamasmi
RV iṣurna śriya iṣudherasanā goṣāḥ śatasā na raṃhiḥ
RV avīre kratau vi davidyutan norā na māyuṃ citayantadhunayaḥ
RV sā vasu dadhatī śvaśurāya vaya uṣo yadi vaṣṭyantigṛhāt
RV astaṃ nanakṣe yasmiñcākan divā naktaṃśnathitā vaitasena
RV triḥ sma māhnaḥ śnathayo vaitasenota sma me 'vyatyaipṛṇāsi
RV purūravo 'nu te ketamāyaṃ rājā me vīra tanvastadāsīḥ
RV yā sujūrṇiḥ śreṇiḥ sumnaāpirhradecakṣurna granthinīcaraṇyuḥ
RV tā añjayo 'ruṇayo na sasruḥ śriye gāvo nadhenavo 'navanta
RV samasmiñ jāyamāna āsata gnā utemavardhan nadyaḥsvagūrtāḥ
RV mahe yat tvā purūravo raṇāyāvardhayandasyuhatyāya devāḥ
RV sacā yadāsu jahatīṣvatkamamānuṣīṣu mānuṣo niṣeve
RV apa sma mat tarasantī na bhujyustā atrasan rathaspṛśonāśvāḥ
RV yadāsu marto amṛtāsu nispṛk saṃ kṣoṇībhiḥ kratubhirnapṛṅkte
RV tā ātayo na tanvaḥ śumbhata svā aśvāso nakrīḷayo dandaśānāḥ
RV vidyun na yā patantī davidyod bharantī me apyā kāmyāni
RV janiṣṭo apo naryaḥ sujātaḥ prorvaśī tirata dīrghamāyuḥ
RV jajñiṣa itthā gopīthyāya hi dadhātha tat purūravo maojaḥ
RV aśāsaṃ tvā viduṣī sasminnahan na ma āśṛṇoḥkimabhug vadāsi
RV kadā sūnuḥ pitaraṃ jāta ichāccakran nāśru vartayadvijānan
RV ko dampatī samanasā vi yūyodadha yadagniḥśvaśureṣu dīdayat
RV prati bravāṇi vartayate aśru cakran na krandadādhyeśivāyai
RV pra tat te hinavā yat te asme parehyastaṃ nahimūra māpaḥ
RV sudevo adya prapatedanāvṛt parāvataṃ paramāṃ gantavā u
RV adhā śayīta nirṛterupasthe 'dhainaṃ vṛkā rabhasāsoadyuḥ
RV purūravo mā mṛthā mā pra papto mā tvā vṛkāso aśivāsa ukṣan
RV na vai straiṇāni sakhyāni santi sālāvṛkāṇāṃhṛdayānyetā
RV yad virūpācaraṃ martyeṣvavasaṃ rātrīḥ śaradaścatasraḥ
RV ghṛtasya stokaṃ sakṛdahna āśnāṃ tādevedantātṛpāṇā carāmi
RV antarikṣaprāṃ rajaso vimānīmupa śikṣāmyurvaśīṃvasiṣṭhaḥ
RV upa tvā rātiḥ sukṛtasya tiṣṭhān ni vartasvahṛdayaṃ tapyate me
RV iti tvā devā ima āhuraiḷa yathemetad bhavasimṛtyubandhuḥ
RV prajā te devān haviṣā yajāti svarga u tvamapi mādayāse
RV pra te mahe vidathe śaṃsiṣaṃ harī pra te vanve vanuṣoharyataṃ madam
RV ghṛtaṃ na yo haribhiścāru secata ā tvāviśantu harivarpasaṃ giraḥ
RV hariṃ hi yonimabhi ye samasvaran hinvanto harī divyaṃyathā sadaḥ
RV ā yaṃ pṛṇanti haribhirna dhenava indrāyaśūṣaṃ harivantamarcata
RV so asya vajro harito ya āyaso harirnikāmo harirāgabhastyoḥ
RV dyumnī suśipro harimanyusāyaka indre ni rūpāharitā mimikṣire
RV divi na keturadhi dhāyi haryato vivyacad vajro harito naraṃhyā
RV tudadahiṃ hariśipro ya āyasaḥ sahasraśokāabhavad dharimbharaḥ
RV tvaṃtvamaharyathā upastutaḥ pūrvebhirindra harikeśayajvabhiḥ
RV tvaṃ haryasi tava viśvamukthyamasāmi rādhoharijāta haryatam
RV tā vajriṇaṃ mandinaṃ stomyaṃ mada indraṃ rathe vahatoharyatā harī
RV purūṇyasmai savanāni haryata indrāyasomā harayo dadhanvire
RV araṃ kāmāya harayo dadhanvire sthirāya hinvan harayo harīturā
RV arvadbhiryo haribhirjoṣamīyate so asya kāmaṃharivantamānaśe
RV hariśmaśārurharikeśa āyasasturaspeye yo haripāavardhata
RV arvadbhiryo haribhirvājinīvasurati viśvāduritā pāriṣad dharī
RV sruveva yasya hariṇī vipetatuḥ śipre vājāya hariṇīdavidhvataḥ
RV pra yat kṛte camase marmṛjad dharī pītvāmadasya hayatasyādhasaḥ
RV uta sma sadma haryatasya pastyoratyo na vājaṃ harivānacikradat
RV mahī cid dhi dhiṣaṇāharyadojasā bṛhad vayodadhiṣe haryataścidā
RV ā rodasī haryamāṇo mahitvā navyaṃnavyaṃ haryasi manmanu priyam
RV pra pastyamasura haryataṃ gorāviṣkṛdhi harayesūryāya
RV ā tvā haryantaṃ prayujo janānāṃ rathe vahantu hariśipramindra
RV pibā yathā pratibhṛtasya madhvo haryan yajñaṃsadhamāde daśoṇim
RV apāḥ pūrveṣāṃ harivaḥ sutānāmatho idaṃ savanaṃkevalaṃ te
RV mamaddhi somaṃ madhumantamindra satrā vṛṣañjaṭhara ā vṛṣasva
RV yā oṣadhīḥ pūrvā jātā devebhyastriyugaṃ purā
RV manainu babhrūṇāmahaṃ śataṃ dhāmāni sapta ca
RV śataṃ vo amba dhāmāni sahasramuta vo ruhaḥ
RV adhāśatakratvo yūyamimaṃ me agadaṃ kṛta
RV oṣadhīḥ prati modadhvaṃ puṣpavatīḥ prasūvarīḥ
RV aśvāiva sajitvarīrvīrudhaḥ pārayiṣṇvaḥ
RV oṣadhīriti mātarastad vo devīrupa bruve
RV saneyamaśvaṃgāṃ vāsa ātmānaṃ tava pūruṣa
RV aśvatthe vo niṣadanaṃ parṇe vo vasatiṣ kṛtā
RV gobhāja itkilāsatha yat sanavatha pūruṣam
RV yatrauṣadhīḥ samagmata rājānaḥ samitāviva
RV vipraḥ saucyate bhiṣag rakṣohāmīvacātanaḥ
RV aśvāvatīṃ somāvatīmūrjayantīmudojasam
RV āvitsisarvā oṣadhīrasmā ariṣṭatātaye
RV ucchuṣmā oṣadhīnāṃ gāvo goṣṭhādiverate
RV dhanaṃsaniṣyantīnāmātmānaṃ tava pūruṣa
RV iṣkṛtirnāma vo mātātho yūyaṃ stha niṣkṛtīḥ
RV sīrāḥpatatṛṇī sthana yadāmayati niṣ kṛtha
RV ati viśvāḥ pariṣṭhā stena iva vrajamakramuḥ
RV oṣadhīḥprācucyavuryat kiṃ ca tanvo rapaḥ
RV yadimā vājayannahamoṣadhīrhasta ādadhe
RV ātmāyakṣmasya naśyati purā jīvagṛbho yathā
RV yasyauṣadhīḥ prasarpathāṅgamañgaṃ paruṣparuḥ
RV tatoyakṣmaṃ vi bādhadhva ugro madhyamaśīriva
RV sākaṃ yakṣma pra pata cāṣeṇa kikidīvinā
RV sākaṃvātasya dhrājyā sākaṃ naśya nihākayā
RV anyā vo anyāmavatvanyānyasyā upāvata
RV tāḥ sarvāḥsaṃvidānā idaṃ me prāvatā vacaḥ
RV yāḥ phalinīryā aphalā apuṣpā yāśca puṣpiṇīḥ
RV bṛhaspatiprasūtāstā no muñcantvaṃhasaḥ
RV muñcantu mā śapathyādatho varuṇyāduta
RV atho yamasyapaḍbīśāt sarvasmād devakilbiṣāt
RV avapatantīravadan diva oṣadhayas pari
RV yaṃ jīvamaśnavāmahai na sa riṣyāti pūruṣaḥ
RV yā oṣadhīḥ somarājñīrbahvīḥ śatavicakṣaṇāḥ
RV tāsāṃ tvamasyuttamāraṃ kāmāya śaṃ hṛde
RV yā oṣadhīḥ somarājñīrviṣṭhitāḥ pṛthivīmanu
RV bṛhaspatiprasūtā asyai saṃ datta vīryam
RV mā vo riṣat khanitā yasmai cāhaṃ khanāmi vaḥ
RV dvipaccatuṣpadasmākaṃ sarvamastvanāturam
RV yāścedamupaśṛṇvanti yāśca dūraṃ parāgatāḥ
RV sarvāḥ saṃgatya vīrudho 'syai saṃ datta vīryam
RV oṣadhayaḥ saṃ vadante somena saha rājñā
RV yasmai kṛṇotibrāhmaṇastaṃ rājan pārayāmasi
RV tvamuttamāsyoṣadhe tava vṛkṣā upastayaḥ
RV upastirastuso 'smākaṃ yo asmānabhidāsati
RV bṛhaspate prati me devatāmihi mitro vā yad varuṇo vāsipūṣā
RV ādityairvā yad vasubhirmarutvān sa parjanyaṃśantanave vṛṣāya
RV ā devo dūto ajiraścikitvān tvad devāpe abhi māmagachat
RV pratīcīnaḥ prati māmā vavṛtsva dadhāmi te dyumatīṃvācamāsan
RV asme dhehi dyumatīṃ vācamāsan bṛhaspate anamīvāmiṣirām
RV yayā vṛṣṭiṃ śantanave vanāva divo drapsomadhumānā viveśa
RV ā no drapsā madhumanto viśantvindra dehyadhirathaṃsahasram
RV ni ṣīda hotram ṛtuthā yajasva devān devāpehaviṣā saparya
RV ārṣṭiṣeṇo hotram ṛṣirniṣīdan devāpirdevasumatiṃcikitvān
RV sa uttarasmādadharaṃ samudramapo divyā asṛjadvarṣyā abhi
RV asmin samudre adhyuttarasminnāpo devebhirnivṛtā atiṣṭhan
RV tā adravannārṣṭiṣeṇena sṛṣṭā devāpinā preṣitāmṛkṣiṇīṣu
RV yad devāpiḥ śantanave purohito hotrāya vṛtaḥ kṛpayannadīdhet
RV devaśrutaṃ vṛṣṭivaniṃ rarāṇo bṛhaspatirvācamasmā ayachat
RV yaṃ tvā devāpiḥ śuśucāno agna ārṣṭiṣeṇo manuṣyaḥsamīdhe
RV viśvebhirdevairanumadyamānaḥ pra parjanyamīrayā vṛṣṭimantam
RV tvāṃ pūrva ṛṣayo gīrbhirāyan tvāmadhvareṣu puruhūtaviśve
RV sahasrāṇyadhirathānyasme ā no yajñaṃrohidaśvopa yāhi
RV etānyagne navatirnava tve āhutānyadhirathā sahasra
RV tebhirvardhasva tanvaḥ śūra pūrvīrdivo no vṛṣṭimiṣitorirīhi
RV etānyagne navatiṃ sahasrā saṃ pra yacha vṛṣṇa indrāyabhāgam
RV vidvān patha ṛtuśo devayānānapyaulānaṃ divideveṣu dhehi
RV agne bādhasva vi mṛdho vi durgahāpāmīvāmaparakṣāṃsi sedha
RV asmāt samudrād bṛhato divo no 'pāmbhūmānamupa naḥ sṛjeha
RV kaṃ naścitramiṣaṇyasi cikitvān pṛthugmānaṃ vāśraṃvāvṛdhadhyai
RV kat tasya dātu śavaso vyuṣṭau takṣadvajraṃ vṛtraturamapinvat
RV sa hi dyutā vidyutā veti sāma pṛthuṃ yonimasuratvāsasāda
RV sa sanīḷebhiḥ prasahāno asya bhrāturna ṛtesaptathasya māyāḥ
RV sa vājaṃ yātāpaduṣpadā yan svarṣātā pari ṣadatsaniṣyan
RV anarvā yacchatadurasya vedo ghnañchiśnadevānabhi varpasā bhūt
RV sa yahvyo 'vanīrgoṣvarvā juhoti pradhanyāsu sasriḥ
RV apādo yatra yujyāso 'rathā droṇyaśvāsa īrate ghṛtaṃvāḥ
RV sa rudrebhiraśastavāra ṛbhvā hitvī gayamāreavadyaāgāt
RV vamrasya manye mithunā vivavrī annamabhītyārodayanmuṣāyan
RV sa id dāsaṃ tuvīravaṃ patirdan ṣaḷakṣantriśīrṣāṇaṃ damanyat
RV asya trito nvojasā vṛdhāno vipāvarāhamayoagrayā han
RV sa druhvaṇe manuṣa ūrdhvasāna ā sāviṣadarśasānāyaśarum
RV sa nṛtamo nahuṣo 'smat sujātaḥ puro 'bhinadarhandasyuhatye
RV so abhriyo na yavasa udanyan kṣayāya gātuṃ vidan no asme
RV upa yat sīdadinduṃ śarīraiḥ śyeno 'yopāṣṭirhantidasyūn
RV sa vrādhataḥ śavasānebhirasya kutsāya śuṣṇaṃ kṛpaṇeparādāt
RV ayaṃ kavimanayacchasyamānamatkaṃ vo asyasanitota nṛṇām
RV ayaṃ daśasyan naryebhirasya dasmo devebhirvaruṇo namāyī
RV ayaṃ kanīna ṛtupā avedyamimītāraruṃ yaścatuṣpāt
RV asya stomebhirauśija ṛjiśvā vrajaṃ darayad vṛṣabheṇapiproḥ
RV sutvā yad yajato dīdayad gīḥ pura iyāno abhivarpasā bhūt
RV evā maho asura vakṣathāya vamrakaḥ paḍbhirupa sarpadindram
RV sa iyānaḥ karati svastimasmā iṣamūrjaṃsukṣitiṃ viśvamābhāḥ
RV indra dṛhya maghavan tvāvadid bhuja iha stutaḥ sutapābodhi no vṛdhe
RV devebhirnaḥ savitā prāvatu śrutamāsarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV bharāya su bharata bhāgam ṛtviyaṃ pra vāyave śucipekrandadiṣṭaye
RV gaurasya yaḥ payasaḥ pītimānaśa āsarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV ā no devaḥ savitā sāviṣad vaya ṛjūyate yajamānāyasunvate
RV yathā devān pratibhūṣema pākavadā sarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV indro asme sumanā astu viśvahā rājā somaḥ suvitasyādhyetu naḥ
RV yathāyathā mitradhitāni sandadhurā sarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV indra ukthena śavasā parurdadhe bṛhaspate pratarītāsyāyuṣaḥ
RV yajño manuḥ pramatirnaḥ pitā hi kamāsarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV indrasya nu sukṛtaṃ daivyaṃ saho 'gnirgṛhe jaritāmedhiraḥ kaviḥ
RV yajñaśca bhūd vidathe cārurantama āsarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV na vo guhā cakṛma bhūri duṣkṛtaṃ nāviṣṭyaṃ vasavodevaheḷanam
RV mākirno devā anṛtasya varpasa ā sarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV apāmīvāṃ savitā sāviṣan nyag varīya idapa sedhantvadrayaḥ
RV grāvā yatra madhuṣuducyate bṛhadāsarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV ūrdhvo grāvā vasavo 'stu sotari viśvā dveṣāṃsi sanutaryuyota
RV sa no devaḥ savitā pāyurīḍya ā sarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV ūrjaṃ gāvo yavase pīvo attana ṛtasya yāḥ sadane kośeaṅgdhve
RV tanūreva tanvo astu bheṣajamā sarvatātiṃaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV kratuprāvā jaritā śaśvatāmava indra id bhadrāpramatiḥ sutāvatām
RV pūrṇamūdhardivyaṃ yasya siktayaā sarvatātimaditiṃ vṛṇīmahe
RV citraste bhānuḥ kratuprā abhiṣṭiḥ santi spṛdhojaraṇiprā adhṛṣṭāḥ
RV rajiṣṭhayā rajyā paśva ā gostūtūrṣaty paryagraṃ duvasyuḥ
RV ud budhyadhvaṃ samanasaḥ sakhāyaḥ samagnimindhvaṃ bahavaḥsanīḷāḥ
RV dadhikrāmagnimuṣasaṃ ca devīmindrāvato'vase ni hvaye vaḥ
RV mandrā kṛṇudhvaṃ dhiya ā tanudhvaṃ nāvamaritraparaṇīṃkṛṇudhvam
RV iṣkṛṇudhvamāyudhāraṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ prāñcaṃyajñaṃ pra ṇayatā sakhāyaḥ
RV yunakta sīrā vi yugā tanudhvaṃ kṛte yonau vapateha bījam
RV girā ca śruṣṭiḥ śabharā asan no nedīya it sṛṇyaḥpakvameyāt
RV sīrā yuñjanti kavayo yugā vi tanvate pṛthak
RV dhīrādeveṣu sumnayā
RV nirāhāvān kṛṇotana saṃ varatrā dadhātana
RV siñcāmahāavatamudriṇaṃ vayaṃ suṣekamanupakṣitam
RV iṣkṛtāhāvamavataṃ suvaratraṃ suṣecanam
RV udriṇaṃ siñceakṣitam
RV prīṇītāśvān hitaṃ jayātha svastivāhaṃ rathamitkṛṇudhvam
RV droṇāhāvamavatamaśmacakramaṃsatrakośaṃsiñcatā nṛpāṇam
RV vrajaṃ kṛṇudhvaṃ sa hi vo nṛpāṇo varma sīvyadhvaṃ bahulāpṛthūni
RV puraḥ kṛṇudhvamāyasīradhṛṣṭā mā vaḥ susroccamaso dṛṃhatā tam
RV ā vo dhiyaṃ yajñiyāṃ varta ūtaye devā devīṃ yajatāṃyajñiyāmiha
RV sā no duhīyad yavaseva gatvī sahasradhārāpayasā mahī gauḥ
RV ā tū ṣiñca harimīṃ drorupasthe vāśībhistakṣatāśmanmayībhiḥ
RV pari ṣvajadhvaṃ daśa kakṣyābhirubhe dhurau prati vahniṃ yunakta
RV ubhe dhurau vahnirāpibdamāno 'ntaryoneva carati dvijāniḥ
RV vanaspatiṃ vana āsthāpayadhvaṃ ni ṣū dadhidhvamakhananta utsam
RV kapṛn naraḥ kapṛthamud dadhātana codayata khudatavājasātaye
RV niṣṭigryaḥ putramā cyāvayotaya indraṃsabādha iha somapītaye
RV pra te rathaṃ mithūkṛtamindro 'vatu dhṛṣṇuyā
RV asminnājau puruhūta śravāyye dhanabhakṣeṣu no 'va
RV ut sma vāto vahati vāso 'syā adhirathaṃ yadajayat sahasram
RV rathīrabhūn mudgalānī gaviṣṭau bhare kṛtaṃ vyacedindrasenā
RV antaryacha jighāṃsato vajramindrābhidāsataḥ
RV dāsasyavā maghavannāryasya vā sanutaryavayā vadham
RV udno hradamapibajjarhṛṣāṇaḥ kūṭaṃ sma tṛṃhadabhimātimeti
RV pra muṣkabhāraḥ śrava ichamāno 'jirambāhū abharat siṣāsan
RV nyakrandayannupayanta enamamehayan vṛṣabhaṃ madhya ājeḥ
RV tena sūbharvaṃ śatavat sahasraṃ gavāṃ mudgalaḥ pradhanejigāya
RV kakardave vṛṣabho yukta āsīdavāvacīt sārathirasya keśī
RV dudheryuktasya dravataḥ sahānasa ṛchanti ṣmā niṣpadomudgalānīm
RV uta pradhimudahannasya vidvānupāyunag vaṃsagamatraśikṣan
RV indra udāvat patimaghnyānāmaraṃhatapadyābhiḥ kakudmān
RV śunamaṣtrāvyacarat kapardī varatrāyāṃ dārvānahyamānaḥ
RV nṛmṇāni kṛṇvan bahave janāya gāḥpaspaśānastaviṣīradhatta
RV imaṃ taṃ paśya vṛṣabhasya yuñjaṃ kāṣṭhāyā madhyedrughaṇaṃ śayānam
RV yena jigāya śatavat sahasraṃ gavāmmudgalaḥ pṛtanājyeṣu
RV āre aghā ko nvitthā dadarśa yaṃ yuñjanti taṃ vāsthāpayanti
RV nāsmai tṛṇaṃ nodakamā bharantyuttaro dhurovahati pradediśat
RV parivṛkteva patividyamānaṭ pīpyānā kūcakreṇeva siñcan
RV eṣaiṣyā cid rathyā jayema sumaṅgalaṃ sinavadastu sātam
RV tvaṃ viśvasya jagataścakṣurindrāsi cakṣuṣaḥ
RV vṛṣāyadājiṃ vṛṣaṇā siṣāsasi codayan vadhriṇā yujā
RV āśuḥ śiśāno vṛṣabho na bhīmo ghanāghanaḥ kṣobhaṇaścarṣaṇīnām
RV saṃkrandano 'nimiṣa ekavīraḥ śataṃ senāajayat sākamindraḥ
RV saṃkrandanenānimiṣeṇa jiṣṇunā yutkāreṇa duścyavanenadhṛṣṇunā
RV tadindreṇa jayata tat sahadhvaṃ yudho naraiṣuhastena vṛṣṇā
RV sa iṣuhastaiḥ sa niṣaṅgibhirvaśī saṃsraṣṭā sa yudhaindro gaṇena
RV saṃsṛṣṭajit somapā bāhuśardhyugradhanvāpratihitābhirastā
RV bṛhaspate pari dīyā rathena rakṣohāmitrānapabādhamānaḥ
RV prabhañjan senāḥ pramṛṇo yudhā jayannasmākamedhyavitā rathānām
RV balavijñāya sthaviraḥ pravīraḥ sahasvān vājī sahamānaugraḥ
RV abhivīro abhisatvā sahojā jaitramindra rathamātiṣṭha govit
RV gotrabhidaṃ govidaṃ vajrabāhuṃ jayantamajma pramṛṇantamojasā
RV imaṃ sajātā anu vīrayadhvamindraṃ sakhāyo anusaṃ rabhadhvam
RV abhi gotrāṇi sahasā gāhamāno 'dayo vīraḥ śatamanyurindraḥ
RV duścyavanaḥ pṛtanāṣāḷ ayudhyo 'smākaṃ senāavatu pra yutsu
RV indra āsāṃ netā bṛhaspatirdakṣiṇā yajñaḥ pura etusomaḥ
RV devasenānāmabhibhañjatīnāṃ jayantīnāṃ marutoyantvagram
RV indrasya vṛṣṇo varuṇasya rājña ādityānāṃ marutāṃśardha ugram
RV mahāmanasāṃ bhuvanacyavānāṃ ghoṣodevānāṃ jayatāmudasthāt
RV ud dharṣaya maghavannāyudhānyut satvanāṃ māmakānāmmanāṃsi
RV ud vṛtrahan vājināṃ vājinānyud rathānāṃjayatāṃ yantu ghoṣāḥ
RV asmākamindraḥ samṛteṣu dhvajeṣvasmākaṃ yā iṣavastājayantu
RV asmākaṃ vīrā uttare bhavantvasmānu devā avatāhaveṣu
RV amīṣāṃ cittaṃ pratilobhayantī gṛhāṇāṅgānyapve parehi
RV abhi prehi nirdaha hṛtsu śokairandhenāmitrāstamasāsacantām
RV pretā jayatā nara indro vaḥ śarma yachatu
RV ugrā vaḥ santubāhavo 'nādhṛṣyā yathāsatha
RV asāvi somaḥ puruhūta tubhyaṃ haribhyāṃ yajñamupa yāhitūyam
RV tubhyaṃ giro vipravīrā iyānā dadhanvira indrapibā sutasya
RV apsu dhūtasya harivaḥ pibeha nṛbhiḥ sutasya jaṭharampṛṇasva
RV mimikṣuryamadraya indra tubhyaṃ tebhirvardhasvamadamukthavāhaḥ
RV progrāṃ pītiṃ vṛṣṇa iyarmi satyāṃ prayai sutasyaharyaśva tubhyam
RV indra dhenābhiriha mādayasva dhībhirviśvābhiḥ śacyā gṛṇānaḥ
RV ūtī śacīvastava vīryeṇa vayo dadhānā uśija ṛtajñāḥ
RV prajāvadindra manuṣo duroṇe tasthurgṛṇantaḥsadhamādyāsaḥ
RV praṇītibhiṣ ṭe haryaśva suṣṭoḥ suṣumnasya pururucojanāsaḥ
RV maṃhiṣṭhāmūtiṃ vitire dadhānā stotāraindra tava sūnṛtābhiḥ
RV upa brahmāṇi harivo haribhyāṃ somasya yāhi pītaye sutasya
RV indra tvā yajñaḥ kṣamamāṇamānaḍ dāśvānasyadhvarasya praketaḥ
RV sahasravājamabhimātiṣāhaṃ suteraṇaṃ maghavānaṃ suvṛktim
RV upa bhūṣanti giro apratītamindraṃ namasyā jarituḥpananta
RV saptāpo devīḥ suraṇā amṛktā yābhiḥ sindhumatara indrapūrbhit
RV navatiṃ srotyā nava ca sravantīrdevebhyo gātummanuṣe ca vindaḥ
RV apo mahīrabhiśasteramuñco 'jāgarāsvadhi deva ekaḥ
RV indra yāstvaṃ vṛtratūrye cakartha tābhirviśvāyustanvaṃ pupuṣyāḥ
RV vīreṇyaḥ kraturindraḥ suśastirutāpi dhenā puruhūtamīṭṭe
RV ārdayad vṛtramakṛṇodu lokaṃ sasāhe śakraḥpṛtanā abhiṣṭiḥ
RV śunaṃ huvema maghavānamindraṃ 
RV kadā vaso stotraṃ haryata āva śmaśā rudhad vāḥ
RV dīrghaṃ sutaṃ vātāpyāya
RV harī yasya suyujā vivratā verarvantānu śepā
RV ubhārajī na keśinā patirdan
RV apa yorindraḥ pāpaja ā marto na śaśramāṇo bibhīvān
RV śubhe yad yuyuje taviṣīvān
RV sacāyorindraścarkṛṣa ānupānasaḥ saparyan
RV nadayorvivratayoḥ śūra indraḥ
RV adhi yastasthau keśavantā vyacasvantā na puṣṭyai
RV vanoti śiprābhyāṃ śipriṇīvān
RV prāstaud ṛṣvaujā ṛṣvebhistatakṣa śūraḥ śavasā
RV ṛbhurna kratubhirmātariśvā
RV vajraṃ yaścakre suhanāya dasyave hirīmaśo hirīmān
RV arutahanuradbhutaṃ na rajaḥ
RV ava no vṛjinā śiśīhy ṛcā vanemānṛcaḥ
RV nābrahmā yajñaṛdhag joṣati tve
RV ūrdhvā yat te tretinī bhūd yajñasya dhūrṣu sadman
RV sajūrnāvaṃ svayaśasaṃ sacāyoḥ
RV śriye te pṛśnirupasecanī bhūcchriye darvirarepāḥ
RV yayā sve pātre siñcasa ut
RV śataṃ vā yadasurya prati tvā sumitra itthāstaud durmitraitthāstau
RV āvo yad dasyuhatye kutsaputraṃ prāvo yaddasyuhatye kutsavatsam
RV ubhā u nūnaṃ tadidarthayethe vi tanvāthe dhiyovaśtrāpaseva
RV sadhrīcīnā yātave premajīgaḥ sudinevapṛkṣa ā taṃsayethe
RV uṣṭāreva pharvareṣu śrayethe prāyogeva śvātryā śāsurethaḥ
RV dūteva hi ṣṭho yaśasā janeṣu māpa sthātammahiṣevāpānāt
RV sākaṃyujā śakunasyeva pakṣā paśveva citrā yajurāgamiṣṭam
RV agniriva devayordīdivāṃsā parijmānevayajathaḥ purutrā
RV āpī vo asme pitareva putrogreva rucā nṛpatīva turyai
RV iryeva puṣṭyai kiraṇeva bhujyai śruṣṭīvāneva havamāgamiṣṭam
RV vaṃsageva pūṣaryā śimbātā mitreva ṛtā śatarāśātapantā
RV vājevoccā vayasā gharmyeṣṭhā meṣeveṣāsaparyā purīṣā
RV sṛṇyeva jarbharī turpharītū naitośeva turpharīparpharīkā
RV udanyajeva jemanā maderū tā me jarāyvajarammarāyu
RV pajreva carcaraṃ jāraṃ marāyu kṣadmevārtheṣu tartarīthaugrā
RV ṛbhū nāpat kharamajrā kharajrurvāyurna parpharatkṣayad rayīṇām
RV gharmeva madhu jaṭhare sanerū bhagevitā turpharīphārivāram
RV patareva cacarā candranirṇiṃ manaṛṅgāmananyā na jagmī
RV bṛhanteva gambhareṣu pratiṣṭhāṃ pādeva gādhaṃ taratevidāthaḥ
RV karṇeva śāsuranu hi smarātho 'ṃśeva nobhajataṃ citramapnaḥ
RV āraṅgareva madhverayethe sāragheva gavi nīcīnabāre
RV kīnāreva svedamāsiṣvidānā kṣāmevorjā sūyavasātsacethe
RV ṛdhyāma stomaṃ sanuyāma vājamā no mantraṃ sarathehopayātam
RV yaśo na pakvaṃ madhu goṣvantarā bhūtāṃśoaśvinoḥ kāmamaprāḥ
RV āvirabhūn mahi māghonameṣāṃ viśvaṃ jīvaṃ tamaso niramoci
RV mahi jyotiḥ pitṛbhirdattamāgāduruḥ panthādakṣiṇāyā adarśi
RV uccā divi dakṣiṇāvanto asthurye aśvadāḥ saha tesūryeṇa
RV hiraṇyadā amṛtatvaṃ bhajante vāsodāḥ soma pratiranta āyuḥ
RV daivī pūrtirdakṣiṇā devayajyā na kavāribhyo nahi tepṛṇanti
RV athā naraḥ prayatadakṣiṇāso 'vadyabhiyābahavaḥ pṛṇanti
RV śatadhāraṃ vāyumarkaṃ svarvidaṃ nṛcakṣasaste abhicakṣate haviḥ
RV ye pṛṇanti pra ca yachanti saṃgame tedakṣiṇāṃ duhate saptamātaram
RV dakṣiṇāvān prathamo hūta eti dakṣiṇāvān grāmaṇīragrameti
RV tameva manye nṛpatiṃ janānāṃ yaḥ prathamodakṣiṇāmāvivāya
RV tameva ṛṣiṃ tamu brahmāṇamāhuryajñanyaṃ sāmagāmukthaśāsam
RV sa śukrasya tanvo veda tisro yaḥ prathamodakṣiṇayā rarādha
RV dakṣiṇāśvaṃ dakṣiṇā gāṃ dadāti dakṣiṇā candramuta yad dhiraṇyam
RV dakṣiṇānnaṃ vanute yo na ātmādakṣiṇāṃ varma kṛṇute vijānan
RV na bhojā mamrurna nyarthamīyurna riṣyanti na vyathante habhojāḥ
RV idaṃ yad viśvaṃ bhuvanaṃ svaścaitat sarvandakṣiṇaibhyo dadāti
RV bhojā jigyuḥ surabhiṃ yonimagre bhojā jigyurvadhvaṃ yāsuvāsāḥ
RV bhojā jigyurantaḥpeyaṃ surāyā bhojā jigyurye ahūtāḥ prayanti
RV bhojāyāśvaṃ saṃ mṛjantyāśuṃ bhojāyāste kanyāśumbhamānā
RV bhojasyedaṃ puṣkariṇīva veśma pariṣkṛtandevamāneva citram
RV bhojamaśvāḥ suṣṭhuvāho vahanti suvṛd ratho vartatedakṣiṇāyāḥ
RV bhojaṃ devāso 'vatā bhareṣu bhojaḥśatrūn samanīkeṣu jetā
RV kimichantī saramā predamānaḍ dūre hyadhvā jaguriḥparācaiḥ
RV kāsmehitiḥ kā paritakmyāsīt kathaṃ rasāyāataraḥ payāṃsi
RV indrasya dūtīriṣitā carāmi maha ichantī paṇayo nidhīnvaḥ
RV atiṣkado bhiyasā tan na āvat tathā rasāyā atarampayāṃsi
RV kīdṛṃṃ indraḥ sarame kā dṛśīkā yasyedaṃ dūtīrasaraḥ parākāt
RV ā ca gachān mitramenā dadhāmāthāgavāṃ gopatirno bhavāti
RV nāhaṃ taṃ veda dabhyaṃ dabhat sa yasyedaṃ dūtīrasaraṃ parākāt
RV na taṃ gūhanti sravato gabhīrā hatāindreṇa paṇayaḥ śayadhve
RV imā gāvaḥ sarame yā aichaḥ pari divo antān subhagepatantī
RV kasta enā ava sṛjādayudhvyutāsmākamāyudhāsanti tigmā
RV asenyā vaḥ paṇayo vacāṃsyaniṣavyāstanvaḥ santu pāpīḥ
RV adhṛṣṭo va etavā astu panthā bṛhaspatirva ubhayā namṛḷāt
RV ayaṃ nidhiḥ sarame adribudhno gobhiraśvebhirvasubhirnyṛṣṭaḥ
RV rakṣanti taṃ paṇayo ye sugopā reku padamalakamā jagantha
RV eha gamannṛṣayaḥ somaśitā ayāsyo aṅgiraso navagvāḥ
RV ta etamūrvaṃ vi bhajanta gonāmathaitad vacaḥ paṇayovamannit
RV evā ca tvaṃ sarama ājagantha prabādhitā sahasā daivyena
RV svasāraṃ tvā kṛṇavai mā punargā apa te gavāṃ subhagebhajāma
RV nāhaṃ veda bhrātṛtvaṃ no svasṛtvamindro viduraṅgirasaśca ghorāḥ
RV gokāmā me achadayan yadāyamapāta ita paṇayovarīyaḥ
RV dūramita paṇayo varīya ud gāvo yantu minatīrṛtena
RV bṛhaspatiryā avindan nigūḷāḥ somo grāvāṇa ṛṣayaśca viprāḥ
RV te 'vadan prathamā brahmakilbiṣe 'kūpāraḥ salilomātariśvā
RV vīḷuharāstapa ugro mayobhūrāpo devīḥprathamajā ṛtena
RV somo rājā prathamo brahmajāyāṃ punaḥ prāyachadahṛṇīyamānaḥ
RV anvartitā varuṇo mitra āsīdagnirhotāhastagṛhyā nināya
RV hastenaiva grāhya ādhirasyā brahmajāyeyamiti cedavocan
RV na dūtāya prahye tastha eṣā tathā rāṣṭraṃ gupitaṃkṣatriyasya
RV devā etasyāmavadanta pūrve saptaṛṣayastapase ye niṣeduḥ
RV bhīmā jāyā brāhmaṇasyopanītā durdhāṃ dadhātiparame vyoman
RV brahmacārī carati veviṣad viṣaḥ sa devānāṃ bhavatyekamaṅgam
RV tena jāyāmanvavindad bṛhaspatiḥ somena nītāṃjuhvaṃ na devāḥ
RV punarvai devā adaduḥ punarmanuṣyā uta
RV rājānaḥsatyaṃ kṛṇvānā brahmajāyāṃ punardaduḥ
RV punardāya brahmajāyāṃ kṛtvī devairnikilbiṣam
RV ūrjampṛthivyā bhaktvāyorugāyamupāsate
RV samiddho adya manuṣo duroṇe devo devān yajasi jātavedaḥ
RV ā ca vaha mitramahaścikitvān tvaṃ dūtaḥ kavirasipracetāḥ
RV tanūnapāt patha ṛtasya yānān madhvā samañjan svadayāsujihva
RV manmāni dhībhiruta yajñam ṛndhan devatrā cakṛṇuhyadhvaraṃ naḥ
RV ājuhvāna īḍyo vandyaścā yāhyagne vasubhiḥ sajoṣāḥ
RV tvaṃ devānāmasi yahva hotā sa enān yakṣīṣito yajīyān
RV prācīnaṃ barhiḥ pradiśā pṛthivyā vastorasyā vṛjyateagre ahnām
RV vyu prathate vitaraṃ varīyo devebhyo aditayesyonam
RV vyacasvatīrurviyā vi śrayantāṃ patibhyo na janayaḥśumbhamānāḥ
RV devīrdvāro bṛhatīrviśvaminvā devebhyobhavata suprāyaṇāḥ
RV ā suṣvayantī yajate upāke uṣāsānaktā sadatāṃ niyonau
RV divye yoṣaṇe bṛhatī surukme adhi śriyaṃśukrapiśaṃ dadhāne
RV daivyā hotārā prathamā suvācā mimānā yajñaṃ manuṣoyajadhyai
RV pracodayantā vidatheṣu kārū prācīnaṃ jyotiḥpradiśā diśantā
RV ā no yajñaṃ bhāratī tūyametviḷā manuṣvadihacetayantī
RV tisro devīrbarhiredaṃ syonaṃ sarasvatīsvapasaḥ sadantu
RV ya ime dyāvāpṛthivī janitrī rūpairapiṃśad bhuvanāniviśvā
RV tamadya hotariṣito yajīyān devaṃ tvaṣṭāramiha yakṣi vidvān
RV upāvasṛja tmanyā samañjan devānāṃ pātha ṛtuthāhavīṃṣi
RV vanaspatiḥ śamitā devo agniḥ svadantu havyammadhunā ghṛtena
RV sadyo jāto vyamimīta yajñamagnirdevānāmabhavatpurogāḥ
RV asya hotuḥ pradiśy ṛtasya vāci svāhākṛtaṃhaviradantu devāḥ
RV manīṣiṇaḥ pra bharadhvaṃ manīṣāṃ yathāyathā matayaḥsanti nṛṇām
RV indraṃ satyairerayāmā kṛtebhiḥ sa hivīro girvaṇasyurvidānaḥ
RV ṛtasya hi sadaso dhītiradyaut saṃ gārṣṭeyo vṛṣabhogobhirānaṭ
RV udatiṣṭhat taviṣeṇā raveṇa mahānti citsaṃ vivyācā rajāṃsi
RV indraḥ kila śrutyā asya veda sa hi jiṣṇuḥ pathikṛtsūryāya
RV ān menāṃ kṛṇvannacyuto bhuvad goḥ patirdivaḥ sanajā apratītaḥ
RV indro mahnā mahato arṇavasya vratāminādaṅgirobhirgṛṇānaḥ
RV purūṇi cin ni tatānā rajāṃsi dādhāra yodharuṇaṃ satyatātā
RV indro divaḥ pratimānaṃ pṛthivyā viśvā veda savanā hantiśuṣṇam
RV mahīṃ cid dyāmātanot sūryeṇa cāskambha citkambhanena skabhīyān
RV vajreṇa hi vṛtrahā vṛtramastaradevasya śūśuvānasyamāyāḥ
RV vi dhṛṣṇo atra dhṛṣatā jaghanthāthābhavomaghavan bāhvojāḥ
RV sacanta yaduṣasaḥ sūryeṇa citrāmasya ketavo rāmavindan
RV ā yan nakṣatraṃ dadṛśe divo na punaryato nakiraddhā nu veda
RV dūraṃ kila prathamā jagmurāsāmindrasya yāḥ prasavesasrurāpaḥ
RV kva svidagraṃ kva budhna āsāmāpomadhyaṃ kva vo nūnamantaḥ
RV sṛjaḥ sindhūnrahinā jagrasānānādidetāḥ pra vivijrejavena
RV mumukṣamāṇā uta yā mumucre 'dhedetā naramante nitiktāḥ
RV sadhrīcīḥ sindhumuśatīrivāyan sanājjāra āritaḥpūrbhidāsām
RV astamā te pārthivā vasūnyasme jagmuḥsūnṛtā indra pūrvīḥ
RV indra piba pratikāmaṃ sutasya prātaḥsāvastava hipūrvapītiḥ
RV harṣasva hantave śūra śatrūnukthebhiṣ ṭevīryā pra bravāma
RV yaste ratho manaso javīyānendra tena somapeyāya yāhi
RV tūyamā te harayaḥ pra dravantu yebhiryāsi vṛṣabhirmandamānaḥ
RV haritvatā varcasā sūryasya śreṣṭhai rūpaistanvaṃsparśayasva
RV asmābhirindra sakhibhirhuvānaḥ sadhrīcīnomādayasvā niṣadya
RV yasya tyat te mahimānaṃ madeṣvime mahī rodasīnāviviktām
RV tadoka ā haribhirindra yuktaiḥ priyebhiryāhi priyamannamacha
RV yasya śaśvat papivānindra śatrūnanānukṛtyā raṇyācakartha
RV sa te purandhiṃ taviṣīmiyarti sa te madāyasuta indra somaḥ
RV idaṃ te pātraṃ sanavittamindra pibā somamenā śatakrato
RV pūrṇa āhāvo madirasya madhvo yaṃ viśva idabhiharyantidevāḥ
RV vi hi tvāmindra purudhā janāso hitaprayaso vṛṣabhahvayante
RV asmākaṃ te madhumattamānīmā bhuvan savanā teṣuharya
RV pra ta indra pūrvyāṇi pra nūnaṃ vīryā vocaṃ prathamākṛtāni
RV satīnamanyuraśrathāyo adriṃ suvedanāmakṛṇorbrahmaṇe gām
RV ni ṣu sīda gaṇapate gaṇeṣu tvāmāhurvipratamaṃkavīnām
RV na ṛte tvat kriyate kiṃ canāre mahāmarkaṃmaghavañcitramarca
RV abhikhyā no maghavan nādhamānān sakhe bodhi vasupatesakhīnām
RV raṇaṃ kṛdhi raṇakṛt satyaśuṣmābhakte cidābhajā rāye asmān
RV tamasya dyāvāpṛthivī sacetasā viśvebhirdevairanuśuṣmamāvatām
RV yadait kṛṇvāno mahimānamindriyampītvī somasya kratumānavardhata
RV tamasya viṣṇurmahimānamojasāṃśuṃ dadhanvān madhunovi rapśate
RV devebhirindro maghavā sayāvabhirvṛtraṃjaghanvānabhavad vareṇyaḥ
RV vṛtreṇa yadahinā bibhradāyudhā samasthithā yudhayeśaṃsamāvide
RV viśve te atra marutaḥ saha tmanāvardhannugra mahimānamindriyam
RV jajñāna eva vyabādhata spṛdhaḥ prāpaśyad vīro abhipauṃsyaṃ raṇam
RV avṛścadadrimava sasyadaḥ sṛjadastabhnān nākaṃ svapasyayā pṛthum
RV ādindraḥ satrā taviṣīrapatyata varīyo dyāvāpṛthivīabādhata
RV avābharad dhṛṣito vajramāyasaṃ śevaṃ mitrāyavaruṇāya dāśuṣe
RV indrasyātra taviṣībhyo virapśina ṛghāyato araṃhayantamanyave
RV vṛtraṃ yadugro vyavṛścadojasāpo bibhratantamasā parīvṛtam
RV yā vīryāṇi prathamāni kartvā mahitvebhiryatamānausamīyatuḥ
RV dhvāntaṃ tamo 'va dadhvase hata indro mahnāpūrvahūtāvapatyata
RV viśve devāso adha vṛṣṇyāni te 'vardhayan somavatyāvacasyayā
RV raddhaṃ vṛtramahimindrasya hanmanāgnirnajambhaistṛṣvannamāvayat
RV bhūri dakṣebhirvacanebhirṛkvabhiḥ sakhyebhiḥ sakhyānipra vocata
RV indro dhuniṃ ca cumuriṃ ca dambhayañchraddhāmanasyā śṛṇute dabhītaye
RV tvaṃ purūṇyā bharā svaśvyā yebhirmaṃsai nivacanāniśaṃsan
RV sugebhirviśvā duritā tarema vido ṣu ṇa urviyāgādhamadya
RV gharmā samantā trivṛtaṃ vyāpatustayorjuṣṭimmātariśvā jagāma
RV divas payo didhiṣāṇā aveṣan vidurdevāḥ sahasāmānamarkam
RV tisro deṣṭrāya nirṛtīrupāsate dīrghaśruto vi hijānanti vahnayaḥ
RV tāsāṃ ni cikyuḥ kavayo nidānampareṣu yā guhyeṣu vrateṣu
RV catuṣkapardā yuvatiḥ supeśā ghṛtapratīkā vayunāni vaste
RV tasyāṃ suparṇā vṛṣaṇā ni ṣedaturyatra devā dadhirebhāgadheyam
RV ekaḥ suparṇaḥ sa samudramā viveṣa sa idaṃ viśvambhuvanaṃ vi caṣṭe
RV taṃ pākena manasāpaśyamantitastammātā reḷi sa u reḷi mātaram
RV suparṇaṃ viprāḥ kavayo vacobhirekaṃ santaṃ bahudhākalpayanti
RV chandāṃsi ca dadhato adhvareṣu grahān somasyamimate dvādaśa
RV ṣaṭtriṃśāṃśca caturaḥ kalpayantaśchandāṃsi cadadhata ādvādaśam
RV yajñaṃ vimāya kavayo manīṣaṛksāmābhyāṃ pra rathaṃ vartayanti
RV caturdaśānye mahimāno asya taṃ dhīrā vācā pra ṇayantisapta
RV āpnānaṃ tīrthaṃ ka iha pra vocad yena pathāprapibante sutasya
RV sahasradhā pañcadaśānyukthā yāvad dyāvāpṛthivītāvadit tat
RV sahasradhā mahimānaḥ sahasraṃ yāvadbrahma viṣṭhitaṃ tāvatī vāk
RV kaśchandasāṃ yogamā veda dhīraḥ ko dhiṣṇyāṃ prativācaṃ papāda
RV kam ṛtvijāmaṣṭamaṃ śūramāhurharīindrasya ni cikāya kaḥ svit
RV bhūmyā antaṃ paryeke caranti rathasya dhūrṣu yuktāsoasthuḥ
RV śramasya dāyaṃ vi bhajantyebhyo yadā yamo bhavatiharmye hitaḥ
RV citra icchiśostaruṇasya vakṣatho na yo mātarāvapyetidhātave
RV anūdhā yadi jījanadadhā ca nu vavakṣa sadyomahi dūtyaṃ caran
RV agnirha nāma dhāyi dannapastamaḥ saṃ yo vanā yuvatebhasmanā datā
RV abhipramurā juhvā svadhvara ino naprothamāno yavase vṛṣā
RV taṃ vo viṃ na druṣadaṃ devamandhasa induṃ prothantampravapantamarṇavam
RV āsā vahniṃ na śociṣā virapśinammahivrataṃ na sarajantamadhvanaḥ
RV vi yasya te jrayasānasyājara dhakṣorna vātāḥ pari santyacyutāḥ
RV ā raṇvāso yuyudhayo na satvanaṃ tritaṃnaśanta pra śiṣanta iṣṭaye
RV sa idagniḥ kanvvatamaḥ kaṇvasakhāryaḥ parasyāntarasyataruṣaḥ
RV agniḥ pātu gṛṇato agniḥ sūrīnagnirdadātuteṣāmavo naḥ
RV vājintamāya sahyase supitrya tṛṣu cyavāno anu jātavedase
RV anudre cid yo dhṛṣatā varaṃ sate mahintamāya dhanvanedaviṣyate
RV evāgnirmartaiḥ saha sūribhirvasu ṣṭave sahasaḥ sūnaronṛbhiḥ
RV mitrāso na ye sudhitā ṛtāyavo dyāvo na dyumnairabhi santi mānuṣān
RV ūrjo napāt sahasāvanniti tvopastutasya vandate vṛṣā vāk
RV tvāṃ stoṣāma tvayā suvīrā drāghīya āyuḥ pratarandadhānāḥ
RV iti tvāgne vṛṣṭihavyasya putrā upastutāsa ṛṣayo 'vocan
RV tāṃśca pāhi gṛṇataśca sūrīn vaṣaḍ vaṣaḷ ityūrdhvāso anakṣan namo nama ityūrdhvāso anakṣan
RV pibā somaṃ mahata indriyāya pibā vṛtrāya hantaveśaviṣṭha
RV piba rāye śavase hūyamānaḥ piba madhvastṛpadindrā vṛṣasva
RV asya piba kṣumataḥ prasthitasyendra somasya varamāsutaśya
RV svastidā manasā mādayasvārvācīno revatesaubhagāya
RV mamattu tvā divyaḥ soma indra mamattu yaḥ sūyatepārthiveṣu
RV mamattu yena varivaścakartha mamattu yenaniriṇāsi śatrūn
RV ā dvibarhā amino yātvindro vṛṣā haribhyāṃ pariṣiktamandhaḥ
RV gavyā sutasya prabhṛtasya madhvaḥ satrā khedāmaruśahā vṛṣasva
RV ni tigmāni bhrāśayan bhrāśyānyava sthirā tanuhiyātujūnām
RV ugrāya te saho balaṃ dadāmi pratītyāśatrūn vigadeṣu vṛśca
RV vyarya indra tanuhi śravāṃsyoja sthireva dhanvano'bhimātīḥ
RV asmadryag vāvṛdhānaḥ sahobhiranibhṛṣṭastanvaṃ vāvṛdhasva
RV idaṃ havirmaghavan tubhyaṃ rātaṃ prati samrāḷ ahṛṇānogṛbhāya
RV tubhyaṃ suto maghavan tubhyaṃ pakvo 'ddhīndra pibaca prasthitasya
RV addhīdindra prasthitemā havīṃṣi cano dadhiṣva pacatotasomam
RV prayasvantaḥ prati haryāmasi tvā satyāḥ santuyajamānasya kāmāḥ
RV prendrāgnibhyāṃ suvacasyāmiyarmi sindhāviva prerayaṃnāvamarkaiḥ
RV ayā iva pari caranti devā ye asmabhyandhanadā udbhidaśca
RV na vā u devāḥ kṣudhamid vadhaṃ dadurutāśitamupagachanti mṛtyavaḥ
RV uto rayiḥ pṛṇato nopa dasyatyutāpṛṇanmarḍitāraṃ na vindate
RV ya ādhrāya cakamānāya pitvo 'nnavān sanraphitāyopajagmuṣe
RV sthiraṃ manaḥ kṛṇute sevate purotocit sa marḍitāraṃ na vindate
RV sa id bhojo yo gṛhave dadātyannakāmāya carate kṛśāya
RV aramasmai bhavati yāmahūtā utāparīṣu kṛṇute sakhāyam
RV na sa sakhā yo na dadāti sakhye sacābhuve sacamānāyapitvaḥ
RV apāsmāt preyān na tadoko asti pṛṇantamanyamaraṇaṃ cidicḥet
RV pṛṇīyādin nādhamānāya tavyān drāghīyāṃsamanupaśyeta panthām
RV o hi vartante rathyeva cakrānyamanyamupa tiṣṭhanta rāyaḥ
RV moghamannaṃ vindate apracetāḥ satyaṃ bravīmi vadha it satasya
RV nāryamaṇaṃ puṣyati no sakhāyaṃ kevalāgho bhavatikevalādī
RV kṛṣannit phāla āśitaṃ kṛṇoti yannadhvānamapa vṛṅktecaritraiḥ
RV vadan brahmāvadato vanīyān pṛṇannāpirapṛṇantamabhi ṣyāt
RV ekapād bhūyo dvipado vi cakrame dvipāt tripādamabhyetipaścāt
RV catuṣpādeti dvipadāmabhisvare sampaśyanpaṅktīrupatiṣṭhamānaḥ
RV samau cid dhastau na samaṃ viviṣṭaḥ sammātarā cin nasamaṃ duhāte
RV yamayościn na samā vīryāṇi jñātī citsantau na samaṃ pṛṇītaḥ
RV agne haṃsi nyatriṇaṃ dīdyan martyeṣvā
RV sve kṣayeśucivrata
RV ut tiṣṭhasi svāhuto ghṛtāni prati modase
RV yat tvā srucaḥsamasthiran
RV sa āhuto vi rocate 'gnirīḷenyo girā
RV srucā pratīkamajyate
RV ghṛtenāgniḥ samajyate madhupratīka āhutaḥ
RV rocamānovibhāvasuḥ
RV jaramāṇaḥ samidhyase devebhyo havyavāhana
RV taṃ tvā havantamartyāḥ
RV taṃ martā amartyaṃ ghṛtenāgniṃ saparyata
RV adābhyaṃgṛhapatim
RV adābhyena śociṣāgne rakṣastvaṃ daha
RV gopā ṛtasyadīdihi
RV sa tvamagne pratīkena pratyoṣa yātudhānyaḥ
RV urukṣayeṣudīdyat
RV taṃ tvā gīrbhirurukṣayā havyavāhaṃ samīdhire
RV yajiṣṭhaṃ mānuṣe jane
RV iti vā iti me mano gāmaśvaṃ sanuyāmiti
RV kuvitsomasyāpāmiti
RV pra vātā iva dodhata un mā pītā ayaṃsata
RV kuvit 
RV un mā pītā ayaṃsata rathamaśvā ivāśavaḥ
RV kuvit 
RV upa mā matirasthita vāśrā putramiva priyam
RV kuvit 
RV ahaṃ taṣṭeva vandhuraṃ paryacāmi hṛdā matim
RV kuvit 
RV nahi me akṣipaccanāchāntsuḥ pañca kṛṣṭayaḥ
RV kuvit 
RV nahi me rodasī ubhe anyaṃ pakṣaṃ cana prati
RV kuvit 
RV abhi dyāṃ mahinā bhuvamabhīmāṃ pṛthivīṃ mahīm
RV kuvit
RV hantāhaṃ pṛthivīmimāṃ ni dadhānīha veha vā
RV kuvit 
RV oṣamit pṛthivīmahaṃ jaṅghanānīha veha vā
RV kuvit 
RV divi me anyaḥ pakṣo 'dho anyamacīkṛṣam
RV kuvit 
RV ahamasmi mahāmaho 'bhinabhyamudīṣitaḥ
RV kuvit 
RV gṛho yāmyaraṃkṛto devebhyo havyavāhanaḥ
RV kuvit 
RV tadidāsa bhuvaneṣu jyeṣṭhaṃ yato jajña ugrastveṣanṛmṇaḥ
RV sadyo jajñāno ni riṇāti śatrūnanu yaṃviśve madantyūmāḥ
RV vāvṛdhānaḥ śavasā bhūryojāḥ śatrurdāsāya bhiyasandadhāti
RV avyanacca vyanacca sasni saṃ te navanta prabhṛtāmadeṣu
RV tve kratumapi vṛñjanti viśve dviryadete trirbhavantyūmāḥ
RV svādoḥ svādīyaḥ svādunā sṛjā samadaḥ sumadhu madhunābhi yodhīḥ
RV iti cid dhi tvā dhanā jayantaṃ mademade anumadanti viprāḥ
RV ojīyo dhṛṣṇo sthiramā tanuṣva mā tvā dabhanyātudhānā durevāḥ
RV tvayā vayaṃ śāśadmahe raṇeṣu prapaśyanto yudhenyānibhūri
RV codayāmi ta āyudhā vacobhiḥ saṃ te śiśāmibrahmaṇā vayāṃsi
RV stuṣeyyaṃ puruvarpasam ṛbhvaminatamamāptyamāptyānām
RV ā darṣate śavasā sapta dānūn pra sākṣate pratimānānibhūri
RV ni tad dadhiṣe 'varaṃ paraṃ ca yasminnāvithāvasā duroṇe
RV ā mātarā sthāpayase jigatnū ata inoṣi karvarā purūṇi
RV imā brahma bṛhaddivo vivaktīndrāya śūṣamagriyaḥsvarṣāḥ
RV maho gotrasya kṣayati svarājo duraśca viśvāavṛṇodapa svāḥ
RV evā mahān bṛhaddivo atharvāvocat svāṃ tanvamindrameva
RV svasāro mātaribhvarīrariprā hinvanti ca śavasāvardhayanti ca
RV hiraṇyagarbhaḥ samavartatāgre bhūtasya jātaḥ patirekaāsīt
RV sa dādhāra pṛthivīṃ dyāmutemāṃ kasmai devāyahaviṣā vidhema
RV ya ātmadā baladā yasya viśva upāsate praśiṣaṃ yasyadevāḥ
RV yasya chāyāmṛtaṃ yasya mṛtyuḥ kasmai devāyahaviṣā vidhema
RV yaḥ prāṇato nimiṣato mahitvaika id rājā jagato babhūva
RV ya īśe asya dvipadaścatuṣpadaḥ kasmai devāya haviṣāvidhema
RV yasyeme himavanto mahitvā yasya samudraṃ rasayā sahāhuḥ
RV yasyemāḥ pradiśo yasya bāhū kasmai devāya haviṣāvidhema
RV yena dyaurugrā pṛthivī ca dṛḷhā yena sva stabhitaṃ yenanākaḥ
RV yo antarikṣe rajaso vimānaḥ kasmai devāyahaviṣā vidhema
RV yaṃ krandasī avasā tastabhāne abhyaikṣetāṃ manasārejamāne
RV yatrādhi sūra udito vibhāti kasmai devāyahaviṣā vidhema
RV āpo ha yad bṛhatīrviśvamāyan garbhaṃ dadhānājanayantīragnim
RV tato devānāṃ samavartatāsurekaḥkasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema
RV yaścidāpo mahinā paryapaśyad dakṣaṃ dadhānājanayantīryajñam
RV yo deveṣvadhi deva eka āsīt kasmaidevāya haviṣā vidhema
RV mā no hiṃsījjanitā yaḥ pṛthivyā yo vā divaṃsatyadharmā jajāna
RV yaścāpaścandrā bṛhatīrjajānakasmai devāya haviṣā vidhema
RV prajāpate na tvadetānyanyo viśvā jātāni pari tābabhūva
RV yatkāmāste juhumastan no astu vayaṃ syāma patayorayīṇām
