RV vasuṃ na citramahasaṃ gṛṇīṣe vāmaṃ śevamatithimadviṣeṇyam
RV sa rāsate śurudho viśvadhāyaso 'gnirhotāgṛhapatiḥ suvīryam
RV juṣāṇo agne prati harya me vaco viśvāni vidvān vayunānisukrato
RV ghṛtanirṇig brahmaṇe gātumeraya tava devāajanayannanu vratam
RV sapta dhāmāni pariyannamartyo dāśad dāśuṣe sukṛtemāmahasva
RV suvīreṇa rayiṇāgne svābhuvā yasta ānaṭsamidhā taṃ juṣasva
RV yajñasya ketuṃ prathamaṃ purohitaṃ haviṣmanta īḷate saptavājinam
RV śṛṇvantamagniṃ ghṛtapṛṣṭhamukṣaṇampṛṇantaṃ devaṃ pṛṇate suvīryam
RV ṭvaṃ dūtaḥ prathamo vareṇyaḥ sa hūyamāno amṛtāyamatsva
RV tvāṃ marjayan maruto dāśuṣo gṛhe tvāṃ stomebhirbhṛgavo vi rurucuḥ
RV iṣaṃ duhan sudughāṃ viśvadhāyasaṃ yajñapriyeyajamānāya sukrato
RV agne ghṛtasnustrirṛtāni dīdyadvartiryajñaṃ pariyan sukratūyase
RV tvāmidasyā uṣaso vyuṣṭiṣu dūtaṃ kṛṇvānā ayajantamānuṣāḥ
RV tvāṃ devā mahayāyyāya vāvṛdhurājyamagnenimṛjanto adhvare
RV ni tvā vasiṣṭhā ahvanta vājinaṃ gṛṇanto agne vidatheṣuvedhasaḥ
RV rāyas poṣaṃ yajamāneṣu dhāraya yūyaṃ pātasvastibhiḥ sadā naḥ
RV ayaṃ venaścodayat pṛśnigarbhā jyotirjarāyū rajasovimāne
RV imamapāṃ saṃgame sūryasya śiśuṃ na viprāmatibhī rihanti
RV samudrādūrmimudiyarti veno nabhojāḥ pṛṣṭhaṃharyatasya darśi
RV ṛtasya sānāvadhi viṣṭapi bhrāṭsamānaṃ yonimabhyanūṣata vrāḥ
RV samānaṃ pūrvīrabhi vāvaśānāstiṣṭhan vatsasyamātaraḥ sanīḷāḥ
RV ṛtasya sānāvadhi cakramāṇārihanti madhvo amṛtasya vāṇīḥ
RV jānanto rūpamakṛpanta viprā mṛgasya ghoṣaṃ mahiṣasya higman
RV ṛtena yanto adhi sindhumasthurvidad gandharvoamṛtāni nāma
RV apsarā jāramupasiṣmiyāṇā yoṣā bibharti parame vyoman
RV carat priyasya yoniṣu priyaḥ san sīdat pakṣe hiraṇyayesa venaḥ
RV nāke suparṇamupa yat patantaṃ hṛdā venanto abhyacakṣatatvā
RV hiraṇyapakṣaṃ varuṇasya dūtaṃ yamasya yonauśakunaṃ bhuraṇyum
RV ūrdhvo gandharvo adhi nāke asthāt pratyaṃ citrā bibhradasyāyudhāni
RV vasāno atkaṃ surabhiṃ dṛśe kaṃ svarṇanāma janata priyāṇi
RV drapsaḥ samudramabhi yajjigāti paśyan gṛdhrasya cakṣasāvidharman
RV bhānuḥ śukreṇa śociṣā cakānastṛtīye cakrerajasi priyāṇi
RV imaṃ no agna upa yajñamehi pañcayāmaṃ trivṛtaṃsaptatantum
RV aso havyavāḷ uta naḥ purogā jyogevadīrghaṃ tama āśayiṣṭhāḥ
RV adevād devaḥ pracatā guhā yan prapaśyamāno amṛtatvamemi
RV śivaṃ yat santamaśivo jahāmi svāt sakhyādaraṇīṃnābhimemi
RV paśyannanyasyā atithiṃ vayāyā ṛtasya dhāma vi mimepurūṇi
RV śaṃsāmi pitre asurāya śevamayajñiyādyajñiyaṃ bhāgamemi
RV bahvīḥ samā akaramantarasminnindraṃ vṛṇānaḥ pitaraṃjahāmi
RV agniḥ somo varuṇaste cyavante paryāvardrāṣṭraṃ tadavāmyāyan
RV nirmāyā u tye asurā abhūvan tvaṃ ca mā varuṇa kāmayāse
RV ṛtena rājannanṛtaṃ viviñcan mama rāṣṭrasyādhipatyamehi
RV idaṃ svaridamidāsa vāmamayaṃ prakāśa urvantarikṣam
RV hanāva vṛtraṃ nirehi soma haviṣ ṭvā santaṃ haviṣāyajāma
RV kaviḥ kavitvā divi rūpamāsajadaprabhūtī varuṇo nirapaḥ sṛjat

RV bhadraṃ hi śarma trivarūthamasti ta ārehiṃsānāmapa didyumā kṛdhi
RV pravat te agne janimā pitūyataḥ sācīva viśvā bhuvanā nyṛñjase
RV pra saptayaḥ pra saniṣanta no dhiyaḥ puraścarantipaśupā iva tmanā
RV uta vā u pari vṛṇakṣi bapsad bahoragna ulapasya svadhāvaḥ
RV uta khilyā urvarāṇāṃ bhavanti mā te hetiṃ taviṣīṃcukrudhāma

RV yadā te vāto anuvāti śocirvapteva śmaśru vapasipra bhūma
RV pratyasya śreṇayo dadṛśra ekaṃ niyānaṃ bahavo rathāsaḥ
RV bāhū yadagne anumarmṛjāno nyaṃṃ uttānāmanveṣibhūmim
RV ut te śuṣmā jihatāmut te arcirut te agne śaśamānasyavājāḥ
RV ucchvañcasva ni nama vardhamāna ā tvādya viśvevasavaḥ sadantu

RV hradāścapuṇḍarīkāṇi samudrasya gṛhā ime

RV dṛḷaṃgranthiṃ na vi ṣyatamatriṃ yaviṣṭhamā rajaḥ
RV narā daṃsiṣṭhavatraye śubhrā siṣāsataṃ dhiyaḥ
RV athā hi vāṃ divo narā puna stomo na viśase

RV yātamachā patatribhirnāsatyā sātaye kṛtam

RV ayaṃ hi te amartya induratyo na patyate

RV ava dīdhedahīśuvaḥ
RV yaṃ suparṇaḥ parāvataḥ śyenasya putra ābharat
RV śatacakraṃ yo 'hyo vartaniḥ
RV yaṃ te śyenaścārumavṛkaṃ padābharadaruṇaṃ mānamandhasaḥ
RV enā vayo vi tāryāyurjīvasa enā jāgārabandhutā
RV evā tadindra indunā deveṣu cid dhārayāte mahi tyajaḥ
RV kratvā vayo vi tāryāyuḥ sukrato kratvāyamasmadāsutaḥ
RV imāṃ khanāmyoṣadhiṃ vīrudhaṃ balavattamām
RV yayāsapatnīṃ bādhate yayā saṃvindate patim
RV uttānaparṇe subhage devajūte sahasvati
RV sapatnīṃ me parādhama patiṃ me kevalaṃ kuru
RV uttarāhamuttara uttareduttarābhyaḥ
RV athā sapatnī yāmamādharā sādharābhyaḥ
RV nahyasyā nāma gṛbhṇāmi no asmin ramate jane
RV parāmevaparāvataṃ sapatnīṃ gamayāmasi
RV ahamasmi sahamānātha tvamasi sāsahiḥ
RV ubhe sahasvatībhūtvī sapatnīṃ me sahāvahai

RV māmanupra te mano vatsaṃ gauriva dhāvatu pathā vāriva dhāvatu

RV gāmaṅgaiṣa ā hvayati dārvaṅgaiṣo apāvadhīt
RV vasannaraṇyānyāṃ sāyamakrukṣaditi manyate
RV na vā araṇyānirhantyanyaścen nābhigachati
RV svādoḥphalasya jagdhvāya yathākāmaṃ ni padyate
RV āñjanagandhiṃ surabhiṃ bahvannāmakṛṣīvalām
RV prāhammṛgāṇāṃ mātaramaraṇyānimaśaṃsiṣam
RV śrat te dadhāmi prathamāya manyave 'han yad vṛtraṃ naryaṃviverapaḥ
RV ubhe yat tvā bhavato rodasī anu rejateśuṣmāt pṛthivī cidadrivaḥ
RV tvaṃ māyābhiranavadya māyinaṃ śravasyatā manasā vṛtramardayaḥ
RV tvamin naro vṛṇate gaviṣṭiṣu tvāṃ viśvāsuhavyāsviṣṭiṣu
RV aiṣu cākandhi puruhūta sūriṣu vṛdhāso ye maghavannānaśurmagham
RV arcanti toke tanaye pariṣṭiṣu medhasātā vājinamahraye dhane
RV sa in nu rāyaḥ subhṛtasya cākanan madaṃ yo asya raṃhyaṃciketati
RV tvāvṛdho maghavan dāśvadhvaro makṣū sa vājambharate dhanā nṛbhiḥ
RV tvaṃ śardhāya mahinā gṛṇāna uru kṛdhi maghavañchagdhirāyaḥ
RV tvaṃ no mitro varuṇo na māyī pitvo na dasmadayase vibhaktā
RV suṣvāṇāsa indra stumasi tvā sasavāṃsaśca tuvinṛmṇavājam
RV ā no bhara suvitaṃ yasya cākan tmanā tanāsanuyāma tvotāḥ
RV ṛṣvastvamindra śūra jāto dāsīrviśaḥ sūryeṇasahyāḥ
RV guhā hitaṃ guhyaṃ gūḷamapsu bibhṛmasiprasravaṇe na somam
RV aryo vā giro abhyarca vidvān ṛṣīṇāṃ vipraḥ sumatiṃcakānaḥ
RV te syāma ye raṇayanta somairenota tubhyaṃrathoḷa bhakṣaiḥ
RV imā brahmendra tubhyaṃ śaṃsi dā nṛbhyo nṛṇāṃ śūraśavaḥ
RV tebhirbhava sakraturyeṣu cākannuta trāyasvagṛṇata uta stīn
RV śrudhī havamindra śūra pṛthyā uta stavase venyasyārkaiḥ
RV ā yaste yoniṃ ghṛtavantamasvārūrmirna nimnairdravayanta vakvāḥ
RV savitā yantraiḥ pṛthivīmaramṇādaskambhane savitā dyāmadṛṃhat
RV aśvamivādhukṣad dhunimantarikṣamatūrtebaddhaṃ savitā samudram
RV yatrā samudra skabhito vyaunadapāṃ napāt savitā tasyaveda
RV ato bhūrata ā utthitaṃ rajo 'to dyāvāpṛthivīaprathetām
RV paścedamanyadabhavad yajatramamartyasya bhuvanasya bhūnā
RV suparṇo aṅga saviturgarutmān pūrvo jātaḥ sa u asyānudharma
RV gāva iva grāmaṃ yūyudhirivāśvān vāśreva vatsaṃsumanā duhānā
RV patiriva jāyāmabhi no nyetu dhartādivaḥ savitā viśvavāraḥ
RV hiraṇyastūpaḥ savitaryathā tvāṅgiraso juhve vāje asmin
RV evā tvārcannavase vandamānaḥ somasyevāṇśuṃ pratijāgarāham
RV samiddhaścit samidhyase devebhyo havyavāhana
RV ādityairudrairvasubhirna ā gahi mṛḷīkāya na ā gahi
RV imaṃ yajñamidaṃ vaco jujuṣāṇa upāgahi
RV martāsastvāsamidhāna havāmahe mṛḷīkāya havāmahe
RV tvāmu jātavedasaṃ viśvavāraṃ gṛṇe dhiyā
RV agne devānā vaha naḥ priyavratān mṛḷīkāya priyavratān
RV agnirdevo devānāmabhavat purohito 'gniṃ manuṣyā ṛṣayaḥsamīdhire
RV agniṃ maho dhanasātāvahaṃ huve mṛḷīkandhanasātaye
RV agniratriṃ bharadvājaṃ gaviṣṭhiraṃ prāvan naḥ kaṇvantrasadasyumāhave
RV agniṃ vasiṣṭho havate purohitomṛḷīkāya purohitaḥ
RV śraddhayāgniḥ samidhyate śraddhaya huyate haviḥ
RV śraddhāṃ bhagasya mūrdhani vacasā vedayamasi
RV priyaṃ śraddhe dadataḥ priyaṃ śraddte didāsataḥ
RV priyambhojeṣu yajvasvidaṃ ma uditaṃ kṛdhi
RV yathā deva asureṣu śraddhāmugreṣu cakrire
RV evambhojeṣu yajvasvasmākamuditaṃ kṛdhi
RV śraddhāṃ devā yajamānā vāyugopā upāsate
RV śraddhāṃhṛdayyayākūtyā śraddhayā vindate vasu
RV śraddhāṃ prātai havāmahe śraddhāṃ madhyandinaṃ pari
RV śraddhāṃ sūryasya nimruci śraddhe śrad dhāpayeha naḥ
RV śāsa itthā mahānasyamitrakhādo adbhutaḥ
RV na yasyahanyate sakhā na jīyate kadā cana
RV svastida viśas patirvṛtrahā vimṛdho vaśī
RV vṛṣendraḥpura etu naḥ somapa abhayaṃkaraḥ
RV vi rakṣo vi mṛdho jahi vi vṛtrasya hanū ruja
RV vi manyumindra vṛtrahannamitrasyābhidasataḥ
RV vi na indra mṛdho jahi nīcā yacha pṛtanyataḥ
RV yo asmānabhidāsatyadharaṃ gamayā tamaḥ
RV apendra dviṣato mano 'pa jijyāsato vadham
RV vi manyoḥśarma yacha varīyo yavayā vadham
RV īṅkhayantīrapasyuva indraṃ jātamupāsate
RV bhejānasaḥsuvīryam
RV tvamindra balādadhi sahaso jāta ojasaḥ
RV tvaṃ vṛṣanvṛṣedasi
RV tvamindrāsi vṛtrahā vyantarikṣamatiraḥ
RV ud dyāmastabhnā ojasā
RV tvamindra sajoṣasamarkaṃ bibharṣi bāhvoḥ
RV vajraṃśiśāna ojasā
RV tvamindrābhibhūrasi viśvā jātānyojasā
RV sa viśvābhuva ābhavaḥ
RV soma ekebhyaḥ pavate ghṛtameka upāsate
RV yebhyo madhupradhāvati tāṃścidevāpi gachatāt
RV tapasā ye anādhṛṣyāstapasā ye svaryayuḥ
RV tapo yecakrire mahastāṃścidevāpi gachatāt
RV ye yudhyante pradhaneṣu śūrāso ye tanūtyajaḥ
RV ye vāsahasradakṣiṇāstāṃścidevāpi gachatāt
RV ye cit pūrva ṛtasāpa ṛtāvāna ṛtāvṛdhaḥ
RV pitṝn tapasvatoyama tāṃścidevāpi gachatāt
RV sahasraṇīthāḥ kavayo ye gopāyanti sūryam
RV ṛṣīntapasvato yama tapojānapi gachatāt
RV arāyi kāṇe vikaṭe giriṃ gacha sadānve
RV śirimbiṭhasyasatvabhistebhiṣ ṭvā cātayāmasi

RV ado yad dāru plavate sindhoḥ pāre apūruṣam
RV tadārabhasva durhaṇo tena gacha parastaram
RV yad dha prācīrajagantoro maṇḍūradhāṇikīḥ
RV hatāindrasya śatravaḥ sarve budbudayāśavaḥ

RV agniṃ hinvantu no dhiyaḥ saptimāśumivājiṣu

RV yajñaṃ ca nastanvaṃ ca prajāṃ cādityairindraḥ sahacīkḷipāti

RV agnirnaḥpārthivebhyaḥ

RV pāhino didyutaḥ patantyāḥ

RV śatamindrāgnī savitā bṛhaspatiḥ śatāyuṣāhaviṣemaṃ punarduḥ
RV āhārṣaṃ tvāvidaṃ tvā punarāgāḥ punarnava

RV amīvāyaste garbhaṃ durṇāmā yonimāśaye

RV yastvā svapnena tamasā mohayitvā nipadyate
RV prajāṃ yaste jighāṃsati tamito nāśayāmasi
RV akṣībhyāṃ te nāsikābhyāṃ karṇābhyāṃ chubukādadhi

RV ṛṣabhaṃ mā samānānāṃ sapatnānāṃ viṣāsahim

RV svarjitaṃ mahi mandānamandhaso havāmahe pari śakraṃsutānupa

RV somasya rājño varuṇasya dharmaṇi bṛhaspateranumatyā uśarmaṇi
RV tavāhamadya maghavannupastutau dhātarvidhātaḥ kalaśānabhakṣayam
RV prasūto bhakṣamakaraṃ carāvapi stomaṃ cemaṃ prathamaḥsūrirun mṛje
RV sute sātena yadyāgamaṃ vāṃ prativiśvāmitrajamadagnī dame
RV vātasya nu mahimānaṃ rathasya rujanneti stanayannasyaghoṣaḥ
RV divispṛg yātyaruṇāni kṛṇvannuto eti pṛthivyāreṇumasyan
RV saṃ prerate anu vātasy viṣṭhā ainaṃ gachanti samanaṃ nayoṣāḥ
RV tābhiḥ sayuk sarathaṃ deva īyate 'sya viśvasyabhuvanasya rājā
RV antarikṣe pathibhirīyamāno na ni viśate katamaccanāhaḥ
RV apāṃ sakhā prathamajā ṛtāvā kva svijjātaḥ kuta ābabhūva
RV ātmā devānāṃ bhuvanasya garbho yathāvaśaṃ carati devaeṣaḥ
RV ghoṣā idasya śṛṇvire na rūpaṃ tasmai vātāyahaviṣā vidhema
RV mayobhūrvāto abhi vātūsrā ūrjasvatīroṣadhīrāriśantām
RV pīvasvatīrjīvadhanyāḥ pibantvavasāya padvaterudra mṛḷa
RV yāḥ sarūpā virūpā ekarūpā yāsāmagniriṣṭyānāmāni veda
RV yā aṅgirasastapaseha cakrustābhyaḥparjanya mahi śarma yacha
RV yā deveṣu tanvamairayanta yāsāṃ somo viśvā rūpāṇiveda
RV tā asmabhyaṃ payasā pinvamānāḥ prajāvatīrindragoṣṭhe rirīhi
RV prajāpatirmahyametā rarāṇo viśvairdevaiḥ pitṛbhiḥsaṃvidānaḥ
RV śivāḥ satīrupa no goṣṭhamākastāsāṃvayaṃ prajayā saṃ sadema
RV vibhrāḍ bṛhat pibatu somyaṃ madhvāyurdadhad yajñapatāvavihrutam
RV vātajūto yo abhirakṣati tmanā prajāḥ pupoṣapurudhā vi rājati
RV vibhrāḍ bṛhat subhṛtaṃ vājasātamaṃ dharman divo dharuṇesatyamarpitam
RV amitrahā vṛtrahā dasyuhantamaṃ jyotirjajñeasurahā sapatnahā
RV idaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ jyotiṣāṃ jyotiruttamaṃ viśvajiddhanajiducyate bṛhat
RV viśvabhrāḍ bhrājo mahi sūryo dṛśauru paprathe saha ojo acyutam
RV vibhrājañ jyotiṣā svaragacho rocanaṃ divaḥ
RV yenemāviśvā bhuvanānyābhṛtā viśvakarmaṇā viśvadevyāvatā
RV tvaṃ tyamiṭato rathamindra prāvaḥ sutāvataḥ
RV aśṛṇoḥ somino havam
RV tvaṃ makhasya dodhataḥ śiro 'va tvaco bharaḥ
RV agachaḥsomino gṛham
RV tvaṃ tyamindra martyamāstrabudhnāya venyam
RV muhuḥśrathnā manasyave
RV tvaṃ tyamindra sūryaṃ paścā santaṃ puras kṛdhi
RV devānāṃ cit tiro vaśam
RV ā yāhi vanasā saha gāvaḥ sacanta vartaniṃ yadūdhabhiḥ
RV ā yāhi vasvyā dhiyā maṃhiṣṭho jārayanmakhaḥsudānubhiḥ
RV pitubhṛto na tantumit sudānavaḥ prati dadhmo yajāmasi
RV uṣā apa svasustamaḥ saṃ vartayati vartaniṃ sujātatā
RV ā tvāhārṣamantaredhi dhruvastiṣṭhāvicācaliḥ
RV viśastvā sarvā vāñchantu mā tvad rāṣṭramadhi bhraśat
RV ihaivaidhi māpa cyoṣṭhāḥ parvata ivāvicācaliḥ
RV indraiveha dhruvastiṣṭheha rāṣṭramu dhāraya
RV imamindro adīdharad dhruvaṃ dhruveṇa haviṣā
RV tasmai somoadhi bravat tasmā u brahmaṇas patiḥ
RV dhruvā dyaurdhruvā pṛthivī dhruvāsaḥ parvatā ime
RV dhruvaṃ viśvamidaṃ jagad dhruvo rājā viśāmayam
RV dhruvaṃ te rājā varuṇo dhruvaṃ devo bṛhaspatiḥ
RV dhruvaṃ ta indraścāgniśca rāṣṭraṃ dhārayatāṃ dhruvam
RV dhruvaṃ dhruveṇa haviṣābhi somaṃ mṛśāmasi
RV atho taindraḥ kevalīrviśo balihṛtas karat
RV abhīvartena haviṣā yenendro abhivāvṛte
RV tenāsmānbrahmaṇas pate 'bhi rāṣṭrāya vartaya
RV abhivṛtya sapatnānabhi yā no arātayaḥ
RV abhi pṛtanyantantiṣṭhābhi yo na irasyati
RV abhi tvā devaḥ savitābhi somo avīvṛtat
RV abhi tvā viśvābhūtānyabhīvarto yathāsasi
RV yenendro haviṣā kṛtvyabhavad dyumnyuttamaḥ
RV idaṃ tadakri devā asapatnaḥ kilābhuvam
RV asapatnaḥ sapatnahābhirāṣṭro viṣāsahiḥ
RV yathāhameṣāṃ bhūtānāṃ virājāni janasya ca
RV pra vo grāvāṇaḥ savitā devaḥ suvatu dharmaṇā
RV dhūrṣuyujyadhvaṃ sunuta
RV grāvāṇo apa duchunāmapa sedhata durmatim
RV usrāḥ kartanabheṣajam
RV grāvāṇa upareṣvā mahīyante sajoṣasaḥ
RV vṛṣṇedadhato vṛṣṇyam
RV grāvāṇaḥ savitā nu vo devaḥ suvatu dharmaṇā
RV yajamānāya sunvate
RV pra sūnava ṛbhūṇāṃ bṛhan navanta vṛjanā
RV kṣāmā yeviśvadhāyaso 'śnan dhenuṃ na mātaram
RV pra devaṃ devyā dhiyā bharatā jātavedasam
RV havyā novakṣadānuṣak
RV ayamu ṣya pra devayurhotā yajñāya nīyate
RV ratho nayorabhīvṛto ghṛṇīvāñcetati tmanā
RV ayamagniruruṣyatyamṛtādiva janmanaḥ
RV sahasaścidsahīyān devo jīvātave kṛtaḥ
RV pataṃgamaktamasurasya māyayā hṛdā paśyanti manasāvipaścitaḥ
RV samudre antaḥ kavayo vi cakṣate marīcīnāmpadamichanti vedhasaḥ
RV pataṃgo vācaṃ manasā bibharti tāṃ gandharvo 'vadad garbheantaḥ
RV tāṃ dyotamānāṃ svaryaṃ manīṣām ṛtasya padekavayo ni pānti
RV apaśyaṃ gopāmanipadyamānamā ca parā ca pathibhiścarantam
RV sa sadhrīcīḥ sa viṣūcīrvasāna ā varīvartibhuvaneṣvantaḥ
RV tyamū ṣu vājinaṃ devajūtaṃ sahāvānaṃ tarutāraṃrathānām
RV ariṣṭanemiṃ pṛtanājamāśuṃ svastayetārkṣyamihā huvema
RV indrasyeva rātimājohuvānāḥ svastaye nāvamivā ruhema
RV urvī na pṛthvī bahule gabhīre mā vāmetau mā paretauriṣāma
RV sadyaścid yaḥ śavasā pañca kṛṣṭīḥ sūrya ivajyotiṣāpastatāna
RV sahasrasāḥ śatasā asya raṃhirnasmā varante yuvatiṃ na śaryām
RV ut tiṣṭhatāva paśyatendrasya bhāgam ṛtviyam
RV yadi śrātojuhotana yadyaśrāto mamattana
RV śrātaṃ haviro ṣvindra pra yāhi jagāma sūro adhvanovimadhyam
RV pari tvāsate nidhibhiḥ sakhāyaḥ kulapā navrājapatiṃ carantam
RV śrātaṃ manya ūdhani śrātamagnau suśrātaṃ manye tadṛtaṃ navīyaḥ
RV mādhyandinasya savanasya dadhnaḥ pibendravajrin purukṛjjuṣāṇaḥ
RV pra sasāhiṣe puruhūta śatrūñ jyeṣṭhaste śuṣma iharātirastu
RV indrā bhara dakṣiṇenā vasūni patiḥsindhūnāmasi revatīnām
RV mṛgo na bhīmaḥ kucaro giriṣṭhāḥ parāvata ā jaganthāparasyāḥ
RV sṛkaṃ saṃśāya pavimindra tigmaṃ vi śatrūntāḷi vi mṛdho nudasva
RV indra kṣatramabhi vāmamojo 'jāyathā vṛṣabhacarṣaṇīnām
RV apānudo janamamitrayantamuruṃ devebhyoakṛṇoru lokam
RV prathaśca yasya saprathaśca namānuṣṭubhasya haviṣohaviryat
RV dhāturdyutānāt savituśca viṣṇo rathantaramā jabhārā vasiṣṭhaḥ
RV avindan te atihitaṃ yadāsīd yajñasya dhāma paramaṃguhā yat
RV dhāturdyutānāt savituśca viṣṇorbharadvājo bṛhadā cakre agneḥ
RV te 'vindan manasā dīdhyānā yaju ṣkannaṃ prathamandevayānam
RV dhāturdyutānāt savituśca viṣṇorāsūryādabharan gharmamete
RV bṛhaspatirnayatu durgahā tiraḥ punarneṣadaghaśaṃsāyamanma
RV kṣipadaśastimapa durmatiṃ hannathā karadyajamānāya śaṃ yoḥ
RV narāśaṃso no 'vatu prayāje śaṃ no astvanuyājo haveṣu
RV kṣipadaśastimapa durmatiṃ hannathā karad yajamānāyaśaṃ yoḥ
RV tapurmūrdhā tapatu rakṣaso ye brahmadviṣaḥ śaravehantavā u
RV kṣipadaśastimapa durmatiṃ hannathā karadyajamānāya śaṃ yoḥ
RV apaśyaṃ tvā manasā cekitānaṃ tapaso jātaṃ tapasovibhūtam
RV iha prajāmiha rayiṃ rarāṇaḥ pra jāyasvaprajayā putrakāma
RV apaśyaṃ tvā manasā dīdhyānāṃ svāyāṃ tanū ṛtvyenādhamānām
RV upa māmuccā yuvatirbabhūyāḥ pra jāyasvaprajayā putrakāme
RV ahaṃ garbhamadadhāmoṣadhīṣvahaṃ viśveṣu bhuvaneṣvantaḥ ahaṃ prajā ajanayaṃ pṛthivyāmahaṃ janibhyo aparīṣuputrān
RV viṣṇuryoniṃ kalpayatu tvaṣṭā rūpāṇi piṃśatu
RV āsiñcatu prajāpatirdhātā garbhaṃ dadhātu te
RV garbhaṃ dhehi sinīvāli garbhaṃ dhehi sarasvati
RV garbhaṃ teaśvinau devāvā dhattāṃ puṣkarasrajā
RV hiraṇyayī araṇī yaṃ nirmanthato aśvinā
RV taṃ tegarbhaṃ havāmahe daśame māsi sūtave
RV mahi trīṇāmavo 'stu dyukṣaṃ mitrasyāryamṇaḥ
RV durādharṣaṃ varuṇasya
RV nahi teṣāmamā cana nādhvasu vāraṇeṣu
RV īśe ripuraghaśaṃsaḥ
RV yasmai putrāso aditeḥ pra jīvase martyāya
RV jyotiryachantyajasram
RV vāta ā vātu bheṣajaṃ śambhu mayobhu no hṛde
RV pra ṇaāyūṃṣi tāriṣat
RV uta vāta pitāsi na uta bhrātota naḥ sakhā
RV sa nojīvātave kṛdhi
RV yadado vāta te gṛhe 'mṛtasya nidhirhitaḥ
RV tato no dehijīvase
RV prāgnaye vācamīraya vṛṣabhāya kṣitīnām
RV sa naḥparṣadati dviṣaḥ
RV yaḥ parasyāḥ parāvatastiro dhanvātirocate
RV sa naḥparṣadati dviṣaḥ
RV yo rakṣāṃsi nijūrvati vṛṣā śukreṇa śociṣā
RV sa naḥparṣadati dviṣaḥ
RV yo viśvābhi vipaśyati bhuvanā saṃ ca paśyati
RV sa naḥparṣadati dviṣaḥ
RV yo asya pāre rajasaḥ śukro agnirajāyata
RV sa naḥ parṣadati dviṣaḥ
RV pra nūnaṃ jātavedasamaśvaṃ hinota vājinam
RV idaṃ nobarhirāsade
RV asya pra jātavedaso vipravīrasya mīḷuṣaḥ
RV mahīmiyarmisuṣṭutim
RV yā ruco jātavedaso devatrā havyavāhanīḥ
RV tābhirnoyajñaminvatu
RV āyaṃ gauḥ pṛśnirakramīdasadan mātaraṃ puraḥ
RV pitaraṃ ca prayan svaḥ
RV antaścarati rocanāsya prāṇādapānatī
RV vyakhyanmahiṣo divam
RV triṃśad dhāma vi rājati vāk pataṃgāya dhīyate
RV prativastoraha dyubhiḥ
RV ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ cābhīddhāt tapaso 'dhyajāyata
RV tatorātryajāyata tataḥ samudro arṇavaḥ
RV samudrādarṇavādadhi saṃvatsaro ajāyata
RV ahorātrāṇividadhad viśvasya miṣato vaśī
RV sūryācandramasau dhātā yathāpūrvamakalpayat
RV divaṃ capṛthivīṃ cāntarikṣamatho svaḥ
RV saṃsamid yuvase vṛṣannagne viśvānyarya ā
RV iḷas padesamidhyase sa no vasūnyā bhara
RV saṃ gachadhvaṃ saṃ vadadhvaṃ saṃ vo manāṃsi jānatām
RV devā bhāgaṃ yathā pūrve saṃjānānā upāsate
RV samāno mantraḥ samitiḥ samānī samānaṃ manaḥ saha cittameṣām
RV samānaṃ mantramabhi maṇtraye vaḥ samānena vohaviṣā juhomi
RV samānī va ākūtiḥ samānā hṛdayāni vaḥ
RV samānamastu vomano yathā vaḥ susahāsati
